<p><b><a href="/wiki/March" title="March">March</a></b> <b><a href="/wiki/2016" title="2016">2016</a></b> was the third month of that leap year. The month, which began on a <a href="/wiki/Tuesday" title="Tuesday">Tuesday</a>, ended on a <a href="/wiki/Thursday" title="Thursday">Thursday</a> after 31 days.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Portal:Current_events"><a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events" title="Portal:Current events">Portal:Current events</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/March_2016&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Portal:Current events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><i>This is an <a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events/How_to_archive_the_portal" title="Portal:Current events/How to archive the portal">archived version</a> of Wikipedia's <a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events" title="Portal:Current events">Current events Portal</a> from March 2016.</i></p>

<td style="vertical-align:top;">
<div id="2016_March_1"></div>
<div id="2016_March_01"></div>
<table class="vevent" style="width:100%; margin:7px 0px; padding:2px; background-color:white; border:1px #cef2e0 solid;">
<tr>
<td>
<table cellspacing="0" class="plainlinks" style="background-color:#cef2e0" width="100%">
<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> March 1, 2016<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2016-03-01</span>)</span> (Tuesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_1&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_1&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_1&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_Donbass" title="War in Donbass">War in Donbass</a>
<ul>
<li>Three soldiers are killed and two others are injured after a <a href="/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_Ukraine" title="Armed Forces of Ukraine">Ukrainian military</a> truck was blown up in the eastern part of <a href="/wiki/Luhansk_Oblast" title="Luhansk Oblast">Luhansk Oblast</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uatoday.tv/news/military-truck-blown-up-in-luhansk-region-three-killed-two-injured-601879.html" rel="nofollow">(Ukraine Today)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iraqi_Civil_War_(2014%E2%80%93present)" title="Iraqi Civil War (2014–present)">Iraqi Civil War (2014–present)</a>, <a href="/wiki/American-led_intervention_in_Iraq_(2014%E2%80%93present)" title="American-led intervention in Iraq (2014–present)">American-led intervention in Iraq (2014–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army" title="United States Army">United States Army</a>'s elite <a href="/wiki/Delta_Force" title="Delta Force">Delta Force</a> captures their first suspected <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a> operative during a raid in northern <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>. The detainee is being interrogated by the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> and is expected to be turned over to Iraqi officials in the coming days. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2016/03/01/politics/special-ops-captures-isis-detainee-iraq/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Israeli–Palestinian conflict (2015–present)">Israeli–Palestinian conflict</a>
<ul>
<li>Faulty readings from a <a href="/wiki/Waze" title="Waze">GPS system</a> apparently resulted in two <a href="/wiki/Israel_Defense_Forces" title="Israel Defense Forces">Israeli soldiers</a> driving into the <a href="/wiki/Kalandia#Kalandia_refugee_camp" title="Kalandia">Qalandiya refugee camp</a> in the occupied <a href="/wiki/West_Bank" title="West Bank">West Bank</a>. Israeli forces sent in on a rescue mission, engaged armed <a href="/wiki/Palestinians" title="Palestinians">Palestinians</a>. One 22-year-old Palestinian man was killed with 10 others wounded, one seriously, in the ensuing gun battle. At least 10 Israeli soldiers were wounded. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/middle_east/battles-erupts-after-israeli-soldiers-follow-apparent-gps-error-into-palestinian-zone/2016/03/01/940307ef-503f-4a98-8abb-01cf6357a850_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/middleeast/israel/12179149/Israeli-soldiers-accidentally-follow-GPS-into-a-Palestinian-refugee-camp-and-spark-night-of-rioting.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>At least 18 people are killed and 16 others injured in a multi-vehicle accident involving a bus near <a href="/wiki/Nahdah,_Oman" title="Nahdah, Oman">Nahdah</a> in northwestern <a href="/wiki/Oman" title="Oman">Oman</a>. Six of the dead were from Oman, four from <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a>, two from <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>, and one from <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>. Five others are unidentified. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/oman-police-18-killed-14-injured-bus-crash-37298878" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Peruvian_Army" title="Peruvian Army">Peruvian Army</a> is deployed on the country's northern and southern coasts to help cope with <a href="/wiki/El_Ni%C3%B1o" title="El Niño">El Niño</a>-related floods that have killed at least two people and left thousands homeless. <a class="external text" href="http://www.euronews.com/2016/03/01/peru-sends-in-army-to-deal-with-floods-blamed-on-el-nino/" rel="nofollow">(Euronews)</a></li>
<li>Residents from more than 50 homes in <a href="/wiki/Ripley,_New_York" title="Ripley, New York">Ripley, New York</a>, are evacuated following the derailment of a 34-car <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Southern_Railway" title="Norfolk Southern Railway">Norfolk Southern</a> train carrying <a href="/wiki/Dangerous_goods" title="Dangerous goods">hazardous materials</a> in the southwestern part of the state. <a href="/wiki/Ethanol" title="Ethanol">Ethanol</a> leaked from the two of the 16 derailed cars. A third car carrying <a href="/wiki/Propane" title="Propane">propane</a> crashed but did not leak. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-new-york-derailment-idUSKCN0W418C" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/us/2016/03/02/train-carrying-hazardous-materials-derails-in-upstate-new-york.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Health</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zika_virus_outbreak_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Zika virus outbreak (2015–present)">Zika virus outbreak (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>The first <a href="/wiki/Zika_virus" title="Zika virus">Zika virus</a> case is confirmed in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> state of <a href="/wiki/New_Hampshire" title="New Hampshire">New Hampshire</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wmur.com/health/first-case-of-zika-virus-confirmed-in-new-hampshire/38279260" rel="nofollow">(WMUR)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2016_North_Korean_nuclear_test" title="2016 North Korean nuclear test">2016 North Korean nuclear test</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> vote on the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>-<a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> draft resolution on <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> is rescheduled to 10:00 a.m. EST Wednesday. <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> requests more time to review the text. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-northkorea-nuclear-un-idUSKCN0W34QN" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Libyan_Crisis_(2011%E2%80%93present)" title="Libyan Crisis (2011–present)">Libyan Crisis (2011–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> is to send troops to <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a> to help the <a href="/wiki/Tunisian_Army" title="Tunisian Army">Tunisian Army</a> prevent <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant_in_Libya" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant in Libya">ISIL</a> militants from moving into the country from <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/uk-britain-tunisia-libya-idUKKCN0W33OY" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_migrant_crisis" title="European migrant crisis">European migrant crisis</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Nations_High_Commissioner_for_Refugees" title="United Nations High Commissioner for Refugees">United Nations refugee agency</a> spokesperson Adrian Edwards warns that <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a> is on the verge, "... of a largely self-induced humanitarian crisis, ..." if the rapid build-up of <a href="/wiki/Refugee" title="Refugee">migrants</a> continues at the <a href="/wiki/Geography_of_Greece#Physical_geography" title="Geography of Greece">northern borders</a> of an already over-stretched <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a>. There are at least 24,000 there now, including 8,500 at Idomeni, the site of yesterday's incident. <a class="external text" href="http://www.business-standard.com/article/news-ians/unhcr-warns-of-humanitarian-crisis-in-greece-as-influx-rises-116030101311_1.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Business Standard</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ekathimerini.com/206505/article/ekathimerini/news/europe-on-cusp-of-self-induced-humanitarian-crisis-unhcr-says" rel="nofollow">(<i>Kathimerini</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Territorial_disputes_in_the_South_China_Sea" title="Territorial disputes in the South China Sea">South China Sea disputes</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Filipino</a> fishermen say <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> has deployed up to five ships around the disputed Quirino Atoll, also known as Jackson Atoll, in the <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">South China Sea</a>, preventing them from accessing traditional fishing grounds. <a class="external text" href="http://www.channelnewsasia.com/news/asiapacific/filipino-fishermen-say/2564476.html" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Channel News Asia)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Grand_jury" title="Grand jury">grand jury</a> in the U.S. state of <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">Pennsylvania</a> reports that hundreds of children were sexually abused by about 50 priests in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Altoona-Johnstown_Diocese" title="Altoona-Johnstown Diocese">Altoona-Johnstown Diocese</a> over four decades. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-pennsylvania-sexcrimes-idUSKCN0W35NI" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a> bans government officials from publicly criticizing the work of state institutions and their colleagues, after damaging disclosures last month that highlighted slow progress in fighting corruption. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-ukraine-crisis-censorship-idUSKCN0W351A" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Discrimination_towards_non-binary_gender_persons" title="Discrimination towards non-binary gender persons">Transgender and schools</a>, <a href="/wiki/LGBT_rights_in_South_Dakota" title="LGBT rights in South Dakota">LGBT rights in South Dakota</a>
<ul>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_South_Dakota" title="Governor of South Dakota">South Dakota Governor</a> <a href="/wiki/Dennis_Daugaard" title="Dennis Daugaard">Dennis Daugaard</a> <a href="/wiki/Veto" title="Veto">vetoes</a> House Bill 1008 that would have required <a href="/wiki/Transgender" title="Transgender">transgender</a> students to use bathrooms, locker rooms, and other facilities based on their gender at birth in state public schools. The bill would have been law at midnight if the governor had not acted. <a class="external text" href="http://national.suntimes.com/national-world-news/7/72/2679253/south-dakota-anti-trans-bill-veto" rel="nofollow">(<i>Chicago Sun-Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.npr.org/sections/thetwo-way/2016/03/01/468732723/south-dakota-s-transgender-bathroom-bill-hits-deadline-for-governor" rel="nofollow">(NPR)</a></li>
<li>The primary sponsor of the legislation asks fellow lawmakers not to override the governor’s veto. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/national/the-latest-civil-rights-activists-celebrate-governors-veto/2016/03/01/21554cd8-e00b-11e5-8c00-8aa03741dced_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>In California, two current and one former <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco_Sheriff%27s_Department" title="San Francisco Sheriff's Department">San Franciscan sheriff deputies</a>, are charged with organizing an inmate "fight club" on the seventh floor of the city's <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco_County_Jails#Facilities" title="San Francisco County Jails">Hall of Justice jail</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/local/lanow/la-me-ln-sf-deputies-charged-20160301-story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/us/2016/03/02/2-california-sheriffs-deputies-charged-with-organizing-inmate-fight-club.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2016" title="United States presidential election, 2016">United States presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voters in the U.S. states of <a href="/wiki/Alabama" title="Alabama">Alabama</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a>, <a href="/wiki/Arkansas" title="Arkansas">Arkansas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colorado" title="Colorado">Colorado</a>, <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(U.S._state)" title="Georgia (U.S. state)">Georgia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts" title="Massachusetts">Massachusetts</a>, <a href="/wiki/Minnesota" title="Minnesota">Minnesota</a>, <a href="/wiki/Oklahoma" title="Oklahoma">Oklahoma</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tennessee" title="Tennessee">Tennessee</a>, <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vermont" title="Vermont">Vermont</a>, <a href="/wiki/Virginia" title="Virginia">Virginia</a>, and the overseas territory of <a href="/wiki/American_Samoa" title="American Samoa">American Samoa</a> go to the polls to vote on <a href="/wiki/Super_Tuesday#2016" title="Super Tuesday">Super Tuesday</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/02/29/politics/super-tuesday-republicans-democrats-vote/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/election-us-2016-35655400" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The results show <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> winning the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democratic Party</a> races in Georgia, Alabama, Tennessee, Arkansas, American Samoa. Massachusetts and Virginia while <a href="/wiki/Bernie_Sanders" title="Bernie Sanders">Bernie Sanders</a> has won <a href="/wiki/Vermont" title="Vermont">Vermont</a>, Minnesota, Oklahoma and Colorado. <a class="external text" href="http://www.oregonlive.com/today/index.ssf/2016/03/super_tuesday_2016_analysis_li.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Oregon Live</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://nypost.com/2016/03/01/super-tuesdays-winners-and-losers-state-by-state/?utm_medium=email&amp;utm_campaign=NY%2520Post%2520Breaking%2520News&amp;utm_source=Sailthru&amp;utm_term=breakingnews_exclusives" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Post</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/elections/results/arkansasv" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/elections/results" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Voting returns show that <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican Party</a> races in Georgia, Alabama, Massachusetts, Virginia, Vermont, Arkansas and Tennessee while <a href="/wiki/Ted_Cruz" title="Ted Cruz">Ted Cruz</a> wins Texas, Alaska and Oklahoma and Marco Rubio wins Minnesota. <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_1&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/on-a-fateful-super-tuesday-polls-have-opened-across-the-south-and-new-england/2016/03/01/995c7ec4-df64-11e5-846c-10191d1fc4ec_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.vox.com/2016/3/1/11143522/trump-wins-virginia-primary-results-super-tuesday-2016" rel="nofollow">(Vox)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2016-election/primaries/AK" rel="nofollow">(Alaska)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Corruption_in_South_Africa" title="Corruption in South Africa">Corruption in South Africa</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_South_Africa" title="President of South Africa">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Jacob_Zuma" title="Jacob Zuma">Jacob Zuma</a> survives a no-confidence vote in the <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_South_Africa" title="Parliament of South Africa">South African Parliament</a> in response to corruption allegations against him. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-africa-35694876" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Irish_general_election,_2016" title="Irish general election, 2016">Irish general election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Taoiseach" title="Taoiseach">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Enda_Kenny" title="Enda Kenny">Enda Kenny</a>, who rejected suggestions he should resign, says he will "fully and inclusively" engage with other parties, groups and Independents, including <a href="/wiki/Fianna_F%C3%A1il" title="Fianna Fáil">Fianna Fáil</a>, as he forms the country's government. <a href="/wiki/Sinn_F%C3%A9in" title="Sinn Féin">Sinn Féin</a> says it is not interested in forming a <a href="/wiki/Coalition_government" title="Coalition government">coalition government</a> with Kenny's <a href="/wiki/Fine_Gael" title="Fine Gael">Fine Gael</a> party. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.ie/irish-news/election-2016/kenny-performs-massive-uturn-as-he-opens-door-to-fianna-fil-34503717.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Irish Independent</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishexaminer.com/election2016/election2016-news-and-analysis/fine-gael-mull-rotating-taoiseach-to-get-fianna-fail-support-385074.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Irish Examiner</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/ISS_year_long_mission" title="ISS year long mission">ISS year long mission</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> astronaut <a href="/wiki/Scott_Kelly_(astronaut)" title="Scott Kelly (astronaut)">Scott Kelly</a> and <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> cosmonaut <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mikhail_Korniyenko" title="Mikhail Korniyenko">Mikhail Korniyenko</a> return to <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">Earth</a> after 340 days aboard the <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">International Space Station</a> (ISS). <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/science-environment-35651665" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Association_for_Computing_Machinery" title="Association for Computing Machinery">Association for Computing Machinery</a> awards the 2015 <a href="/wiki/Turing_Award" title="Turing Award">A.M. Turing Award</a> to <a href="/wiki/Whitfield_Diffie" title="Whitfield Diffie">Whitfield Diffie</a> and <a href="/wiki/Martin_Hellman" title="Martin Hellman">Martin Hellman</a> for the invention of <a href="/wiki/Public-key_cryptography" title="Public-key cryptography">public-key cryptography</a> and <a href="/wiki/Digital_signature" title="Digital signature">digital signatures</a> which revolutionized <a href="/wiki/Computer_security" title="Computer security">computer security</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.technewsworld.com/story/83182.html" rel="nofollow">(TechNewsWorld)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cuba%E2%80%93United_States_relations" title="Cuba–United States relations">Cuba–United States relations</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Major_League_Baseball" title="Major League Baseball">MLB</a> announces the <a href="/wiki/Tampa_Bay_Rays" title="Tampa Bay Rays">Tampa Bay Rays</a> <a href="/wiki/Professional_baseball" title="Professional baseball">professional baseball</a> team will play an exhibition game with the <a href="/wiki/Cuba_national_baseball_team" title="Cuba national baseball team">Cuban National Team</a> on March 22, 2016, in <a href="/wiki/Havana" title="Havana">Havana</a>. <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">United States President</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a>, who is scheduled to visit the island nation then, is expected to attend. <a class="external text" href="http://espn.go.com/mlb/story/_/id/14879877/president-barack-obama-expected-attend-exhibition-game-cuba" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.tampabay.com/blogs/rays/rays-trip-to-cuba-for-march-22-exhibition-finally-set/2267520" rel="nofollow">(<i>Tampa Bay Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> March 2, 2016<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2016-03-02</span>)</span> (Wednesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_2&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_2&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_2&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>One <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">Chinese</a> national is killed and three others injured in a possible militant attack on a Chinese-invested company in <a href="/wiki/Laos" title="Laos">Laos</a>, the official <a href="/wiki/Xinhua_News_Agency" title="Xinhua News Agency">Xinhua News Agency</a> reports. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-laos-china-attacks-idUSKCN0W40K4" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Israeli–Palestinian conflict (2015–present)">Israeli–Palestinian conflict</a>
<ul>
<li>Two <a href="/wiki/Palestinians" title="Palestinians">Palestinian</a> teenagers, from the nearby village of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Qaryout" title="Qaryout">Qaryout</a>, got into a Jewish settlement and stabbed an <a href="/wiki/Israeli_settlement" title="Israeli settlement">Israeli settler</a> at his home in the Eli settlement near <a href="/wiki/Nablus" title="Nablus">Nablus</a> in the <a href="/wiki/West_Bank#Political_status" title="West Bank">occupied West Bank</a>. They were stopped and killed by the army. The injured settler was taken to a hospital. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-israel-palestinians-idUSKCN0W40I8" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.i24news.tv/en/news/israel/diplomacy-defense/104762-160302-west-bank-two-palestinian-terrorists-killed-after-attempted-attack" rel="nofollow">(AFP via i24news)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Spillover_of_the_Syrian_Civil_War" title="Spillover of the Syrian Civil War">Spillover of the Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jordan" title="Jordan">Jordan</a> says an overnight raid on an <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a> cell in the city of <a href="/wiki/Irbid" title="Irbid">Irbid</a> has left seven militants and one security officer dead, with five others injured. Those killed were planning to blow up civilian and military targets in the country, according to the <a href="/wiki/General_Intelligence_Directorate_(Jordan)" title="General Intelligence Directorate (Jordan)">General Intelligence Directorate</a> (GID). <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/magazine-35701841" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2015–present)">War in Afghanistan (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>Nine people are killed in an attack on the Indian consulate In <a href="/wiki/Jalalabad" title="Jalalabad">Jalalabad</a>, <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ndtv.com/india-news/9-killed-in-attack-on-indian-consulate-in-afghanistans-jalalabad-1283335" rel="nofollow">(NDTV)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Libyan_Crisis_(2011%E2%80%93present)" title="Libyan Crisis (2011–present)">Libyan Crisis (2011–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Tunisian_Army" title="Tunisian Army">Tunisian Army</a> kills five suspected <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a> militants near the town of <a href="/wiki/Ben_Gardane" title="Ben Gardane">Ben Gardane</a> after they infiltrated across the border from neighboring <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/uk-tunisia-security-idUKKCN0W42OR" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Mining company <a href="/wiki/Samarco" title="Samarco">Samarco</a> agrees to pay $4.4bn reais (£804m) in compensation to victims of the <a href="/wiki/Bento_Rodrigues_dam_disaster" title="Bento Rodrigues dam disaster">Bento Rodrigues dam disaster</a> in <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/business-35713165" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqi</a> engineers warn that the <a href="/wiki/Mosul_Dam" title="Mosul Dam">Mosul Dam</a> could collapse at anytime, resulting in a catastrophic <a href="/wiki/Flash_flood" title="Flash flood">flash flood</a> that could kill up to one million people along the <a href="/wiki/Tigris" title="Tigris">Tigris</a>, with the major Iraqi cites of <a href="/wiki/Mosul" title="Mosul">Mosul</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tikrit" title="Tikrit">Tikrit</a>, <a href="/wiki/Samarra" title="Samarra">Samarra</a> and <a href="/wiki/Baghdad" title="Baghdad">Baghdad</a> all at risk. The <a href="/wiki/Embassy_of_the_United_States,_Baghdad" title="Embassy of the United States, Baghdad">U.S. embassy in Baghdad</a> has urged American citizens to leave the area. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/02/mosul-dam-engineers-warn-it-could-fail-at-any-time-killing-1m-people" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Sumatra_earthquake" title="2016 Sumatra earthquake">2016 Sumatra earthquake</a>
<ul>
<li>The Meteorological, Climatological and Geophysical Agency of <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a> (BMKG) and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Australian_Bureau_of_Meteorology" title="Australian Bureau of Meteorology">Australian Bureau of Meteorology</a> (BOM) issue <a href="/wiki/Tsunami" title="Tsunami">tsunami</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tsunami_warning" title="Tsunami warning">warnings</a>, after an undersea 7.9 <a href="/wiki/Richter_magnitude_scale" title="Richter magnitude scale">magnitude</a> <a href="/wiki/Earthquake" title="Earthquake">earthquake</a> strikes southwest of <a href="/wiki/Sumatra" title="Sumatra">Sumatra</a>, in the <a href="/wiki/Indian_Ocean" title="Indian Ocean">Indian Ocean</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://www.rt.com/news/334279-quake-strikes-off-indonesia/" rel="nofollow">(RT)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bom.gov.au/tsunami/national.shtml#nationalBulletin0" rel="nofollow">(BOM)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Territorial_disputes_in_the_South_China_Sea" title="Territorial disputes in the South China Sea">South China Sea disputes</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Department_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Philippines)" title="Department of Foreign Affairs (Philippines)">Philippines Foreign Secretary</a> <a href="/wiki/Albert_del_Rosario" title="Albert del Rosario">Albert del Rosario</a> says <a href="/wiki/Maritime_law_enforcement_agencies_in_China" title="Maritime law enforcement agencies in China">Chinese coast guard</a> ships that were sighted two weeks ago near the disputed Jackson Atoll in the northeast <a href="/wiki/Dangerous_Ground_(South_China_Sea)#NE" title="Dangerous Ground (South China Sea)">Dangerous Ground</a> are no longer there today. <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the People's Republic of China">Chinese Foreign Ministry spokesperson</a> <a href="/wiki/Hong_Lei_(diplomat)" title="Hong Lei (diplomat)">Hong Lei</a> said ships were dispatched to the area in late 2015 to salvage a fishing vessel that posed a risk to navigation. Chinese ships, “... persuaded fishing boats to leave the waters in an effort to ensure safety conditions for normal navigation," Hong said. In addition to China and the Philippines, <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Brunei" title="Brunei">Brunei</a> also lay claim to the <a href="/wiki/Spratly_Islands" title="Spratly Islands">Spratly Islands</a> waters. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia_pacific/philippines-spots-suspected-chinese-ships-at-disputed-atoll/2016/03/01/e03b65fa-e02f-11e5-8c00-8aa03741dced_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_migrant_crisis" title="European migrant crisis">European migrant crisis</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> launches a new aid program worth an initial 700 million euros (US$760 million) to address the growing refugee crisis in <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a>. <a href="/wiki/European_Commissioner_for_Humanitarian_Aid_and_Civil_Protection" title="European Commissioner for Humanitarian Aid and Civil Protection">EU Humanitarian Aid Commissioner</a> <a href="/wiki/Christos_Stylianides" title="Christos Stylianides">Christos Stylianides</a> says the so-called Emergency Assistance Instrument will be used to help migrants trapped in Greece and, if needed, in other countries on the migration route front lines. Approval by a majority of EU members is required. The next EU meeting is scheduled for Monday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/03/03/world/europe/eu-aid-migrants-greece.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-europe-migrants-eu-idUSKCN0W41DB" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ekathimerini.com/206539/article/ekathimerini/news/eu-eyes-spending-700-million-euros-for-refugee-crisis" rel="nofollow">(<i>Kathimerini</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Gulf_Cooperation_Council" title="Gulf Cooperation Council">Gulf Cooperation Council</a> formally designates <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Hezbollah" title="Hezbollah">Hezbollah militia</a> a terrorist organization. The GCC member states are <a href="/wiki/Bahrain" title="Bahrain">Bahrain</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kuwait" title="Kuwait">Kuwait</a>, <a href="/wiki/Oman" title="Oman">Oman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Qatar" title="Qatar">Qatar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates" title="United Arab Emirates">United Arab Emirates</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/middle_east/saudi-led-bloc-declares-iran-backed-hezbollah-terror-group/2016/03/02/7f660092-e06f-11e5-9c36-e1902f6b6571_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> adopts the toughest sanctions on <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> in twenty years due to continued efforts to develop a <a href="/wiki/North_Korea_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="North Korea and weapons of mass destruction">nuclear weapons program</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2016/03/02/un-approves-toughest-sanctions-on-north-korea-in-20-years.html" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Spanish_general_election,_2015" title="Spanish general election, 2015">Spanish general election, 2015</a>
<ul>
<li>The conservative <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Party_(Spain)" title="People's Party (Spain)">People's Party</a> (PP) and the left-wing <a href="/wiki/Podemos_(Spanish_political_party)" title="Podemos (Spanish political party)">Podemos</a> party, which together hold 192 seats in Spain’s 350-seat <a href="/wiki/Congress_of_Deputies_(Spain)" title="Congress of Deputies (Spain)">parliament</a> following December's election, confirm they will vote against <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Socialist_Workers%27_Party" title="Spanish Socialist Workers' Party">Spanish Socialist Workers' Party</a> (PSOE) leader <a href="/wiki/Pedro_S%C3%A1nchez_(Spanish_politician)" title="Pedro Sánchez (Spanish politician)">Pedro Sánchez’s</a> candidacy to form a new government. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/europe/spain-parliament-set-to-vote-down-socialist-govt-bid/2016/03/02/c0dbe992-e05b-11e5-8c00-8aa03741dced_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/DHKP/C_insurgency_in_Turkey" title="DHKP/C insurgency in Turkey">DHKP/C insurgency in Turkey</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Istanbul" title="Istanbul">Istanbul</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/General_Directorate_of_Security" title="General Directorate of Security">police</a>, after a standoff, shoot and kill two women from the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_People%27s_Liberation_Party/Front" title="Revolutionary People's Liberation Party/Front">Revolutionary People’s Liberation Army-Front</a> suspected of ambushing a riot police station in the <a href="/wiki/Bayrampa%C5%9Fa" title="Bayrampaşa">Bayrampaşa</a> neighborhood on the city’s <a href="/wiki/Continental_Europe" title="Continental Europe">European</a> side. Two policemen were injured. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/istanbul-security-forces-kill-2-women-suspected-in-police-attack/2016/03/03/4e07cacc-e131-11e5-8d98-4b3d9215ade1_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A nationwide <a href="/wiki/Power_outage" title="Power outage">power outage</a> hits <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>. The Syrian government says shortly before the power outage, militants had hit part of a power-generating station with rockets in the city of <a href="/wiki/Hama" title="Hama">Hama</a>, though it hasn't said whether this damage was linked to the nationwide outage. Also, it isn't clear how many people are affected by the power outage as many cities outside of the government's control already weren't being served by the government-run power grid. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2016/03/03/middleeast/syria-war/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>At least 31 people are killed in <a href="/wiki/Kwekwe" title="Kwekwe">Kwekwe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">Zimbabwe</a>, when a bus, with a blown front tire, switches lanes and slams into an oncoming public transport minibus. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2016/03/05/at-least-31-killed-in-zimbabwe-bus-crash.html" rel="nofollow">(AP ia Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="North Korea and weapons of mass destruction">North Korea and weapons of mass destruction</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> claims that <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> has launched several short range missiles into the <a href="/wiki/Sea_of_Japan" title="Sea of Japan">Sea of Japan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.yonhapnews.co.kr/news/2016/03/03/0200000000AEN20160303005400315.html?input=www.tweeter.com?47cb6080" rel="nofollow">(Yonhap)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/north-korea-fires-short-range-missiles-un-sanctions-014829039.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Yahoo! News)</a></li>
<li>North Korean leader <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kim_Jong_Un" title="Kim Jong Un">Kim Jong Un</a> orders nuclear weapons to be ready for use at any time. <a class="external text" href="http://www.skynews.com.au/news/world/asiapacific/2016/03/04/north-korea-fires-shots-after-un-sanctions.html" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Taliban_insurgency" title="Taliban insurgency">Taliban insurgency</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sartaj_Aziz" title="Sartaj Aziz">Sartaj Aziz</a>, a top foreign affairs adviser for <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>, publicly admits for the first time that the <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Afghan Taliban</a>'s leadership is living in the country and that <a href="/wiki/Islamabad" title="Islamabad">Islamabad</a> has "considerable influence" over them. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/pakistan-admits-afghan-taliban-leaders-living-there/27586816.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russian_military_intervention_in_Ukraine_(2014%E2%80%93present)" title="Russian military intervention in Ukraine (2014–present)">Russian military intervention in Ukraine (2014–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> extends sanctions against <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> over its military intervention in <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/obama-extends-sanctions-russia-ukraine-crisis/story?id=37362950" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jordan%E2%80%93United_States_relations" title="Jordan–United States relations">Jordan–United States relations</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> delivers eight <a href="/wiki/Sikorsky_UH-60_Black_Hawk" title="Sikorsky UH-60 Black Hawk">UH-60 Black Hawk</a> helicopters to <a href="/wiki/Jordan" title="Jordan">Jordan</a> to help the <a href="/wiki/Jordanian_Armed_Forces" title="Jordanian Armed Forces">Jordanian Armed Forces</a> defend the country from the threat of <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-mideast-crisis-jordan-usa-idUSKCN0W5230" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Honduran_people" title="Honduran people">Honduran</a> indigenous environmental activist <a href="/wiki/Berta_C%C3%A1ceres" title="Berta Cáceres">Berta Cáceres</a> is assassinated in her home in <a href="/wiki/La_Esperanza,_Honduras" title="La Esperanza, Honduras">La Esperanza</a> in <a href="/wiki/Intibuc%C3%A1_Department" title="Intibucá Department">Intibucá Department</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telesurtv.net/english/news/Honduras-Indigenous-Leader-Berta-Caceres-Assassinated-in-Home-20160303-0010.html" rel="nofollow">(Telesur)</a></li>
<li>A riot at a prison in <a href="/wiki/Guyana" title="Guyana">Guyana</a>'s capital <a href="/wiki/Georgetown,_Guyana" title="Georgetown, Guyana">Georgetown</a> leaves at least 16 people dead. The riot began when inmates angered by a search that led to the confiscation of <a href="/wiki/Mobile_phone" title="Mobile phone">mobile phones</a> set fires in one part of the prison. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/uk-guyana-riot-idUKKCN0W52KW" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_flag_debate" title="New Zealand flag debate">New Zealand flag debate</a>
<ul>
<li>Voting begins for the second stage of <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a>'s <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_flag_referendums,_2015%E2%80%9316" title="New Zealand flag referendums, 2015–16">flag referendum</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_New_Zealand" title="Flag of New Zealand">current flag</a> going up against the <a href="/wiki/Lockwood_silver_fern_flag" title="Lockwood silver fern flag">design</a> chosen on the first stage of the referendum. Voting will end on March 23 with polling showing the current flag is favoured to win. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-35704127" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2016/03/02/asia/new-zealand-flag-referendum/index.html?eref=edition" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9316_Venezuelan_protests" title="2014–16 Venezuelan protests">2014–16 Venezuelan protests</a>
<ul>
<li>Violence breaks out in in the <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> city of <a href="/wiki/San_Crist%C3%B3bal,_T%C3%A1chira" title="San Cristóbal, Táchira">San Cristóbal</a> between students and <a href="/wiki/Polic%C3%ADa_Nacional_Bolivariana" title="Policía Nacional Bolivariana">police</a> after a <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Tribunal_of_Justice_(Venezuela)" title="Supreme Tribunal of Justice (Venezuela)">supreme court</a> ruling curtailed the power of the opposition-controlled <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Assembly_of_Venezuela" title="National Assembly of Venezuela">National Assembly</a> to review government appointments of Supreme Court justices. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-latin-america-35716100" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Republican_Party_presidential_debates,_2016" title="Republican Party presidential debates, 2016">Republican Party presidential debates, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>The eleventh <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican Party</a> presidential debate of the election cycle takes place at the <a href="/wiki/Fox_Theatre_(Detroit)" title="Fox Theatre (Detroit)">Fox Theatre</a> in downtown <a href="/wiki/Detroit" title="Detroit">Detroit, Michigan</a>, airing live on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fox_News_Channel" title="Fox News Channel">Fox News Channel</a>. The debate features four Republican candidates, <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ted_Cruz" title="Ted Cruz">Ted Cruz</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marco_Rubio" title="Marco Rubio">Marco Rubio</a> and <a href="/wiki/John_Kasich" title="John Kasich">John Kasich</a>. <a href="/wiki/Ben_Carson" title="Ben Carson">Ben Carson</a> was also invited to the debate but he said that he would not be attending. An estimated 16.9 million viewers watched the debate, 5.5 million of them adults aged 25-54, making it the most watched debate since December 2015. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/live-coverage/fox-news-gop-debate" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://newyork.cbslocal.com/2016/03/03/gop-debate-detroit/" rel="nofollow">(CBS Local)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.hollywoodreporter.com/news/tv-ratings-fox-news-gop-872681" rel="nofollow">(Hollywood Reporter)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Astronomers use the <a href="/wiki/Hubble_Space_Telescope" title="Hubble Space Telescope">Hubble Space Telescope</a> to discover <a href="/wiki/GN-z11" title="GN-z11">GN-z11</a>, the remotest <a href="/wiki/Galaxy" title="Galaxy">galaxy</a> yet discovered. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2016-03-04/hubble-space-telescope-observes-most-remote-galaxy-ever-seen/7219846" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a></li>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Libyan_Civil_War_(2014%E2%80%93present)" title="Libyan Civil War (2014–present)">Libyan Civil War (2014–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> spokesperson says two <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italian</a> <a href="/wiki/Hostage" title="Hostage">hostages</a> are freed by local fighters from <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant_in_Libya" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant in Libya">Islamic State</a> custody in <a href="/wiki/Sabratha" title="Sabratha">Sabratha</a>, <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a>. He also confirms that two other Italian hostages were recently killed during local forces clashes with IS militants. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/italians-freed-islamic-state-western-libya-37391358" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yemeni_Civil_War_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Yemeni Civil War (2015–present)">Yemeni Civil War (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>Gunmen storm a retirement home in <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>, run by a charity established by <a href="/wiki/Mother_Teresa" title="Mother Teresa">Mother Teresa</a>, killing 16 people, including four Catholic nuns. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/aponline/2016/03/04/world/middleeast/ap-ml-yemen.html" rel="nofollow">(NY Times)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dissident_Irish_Republican_campaign" title="Dissident Irish Republican campaign">Dissident Irish Republican campaign (1998–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>A bomb explodes under a vehicle in <a href="/wiki/Belfast" title="Belfast">Belfast</a> injuring a prison officer; <a href="/wiki/Dissident_republican" title="Dissident republican">Dissident republicans</a> have claimed responsibility. <a class="external text" href="http://www.belfasttelegraph.co.uk/news/northern-ireland/belfast-bomb-further-attacks-highly-likely-as-dissidents-want-to-mark-easter-rising-centenary-by-killing-security-forces-live-updates-34510925.html" rel="nofollow">(Belfast Telegraph)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/PKK_rebellion_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="PKK rebellion (2015–present)">PKK rebellion (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>Two <a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Turkey" title="Law enforcement in Turkey">Turkish police</a> officers are killed and at least 14 others including several civilians are injured by a <a href="/wiki/Car_bomb" title="Car bomb">car bomb</a> attack on a police station in the town of <a href="/wiki/Nusaybin" title="Nusaybin">Nusaybin</a>, near the <a href="/wiki/Syria%E2%80%93Turkey_border" title="Syria–Turkey border">Syria–Turkey border</a>. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kurdistan_Workers_Party" title="Kurdistan Workers Party">Kurdistan Workers Party</a> (PKK) are blamed for the attack. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-35723733" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Observatory_for_Human_Rights" title="Syrian Observatory for Human Rights">Syrian Observatory for Human Rights</a> says <a href="/wiki/Syrian_opposition" title="Syrian opposition">Syrian rebels</a> have seized control of the al-Tanf border crossing on the <a href="/wiki/Iraq%E2%80%93Syria_border" title="Iraq–Syria border">Iraq–Syria border</a> from <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a> militants. The rebel fighters who took the crossing reportedly entered <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a> through <a href="/wiki/Jordan" title="Jordan">Jordan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/uk-mideast-crisis-syria-al-tanf-idUKKCN0W62MW" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Electricity" title="Electricity">Electricity</a> is gradually being restored across <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a> from a nationwide blackout that began early Thursday afternoon. <a href="/wiki/Council_of_Ministers_(Syria)#Current_cabinet" title="Council of Ministers (Syria)">Syria's Electricity Ministry</a> says the <a href="/wiki/Electrical_grid" title="Electrical grid">electrical grid</a> is expected to return to normal capacity by midnight. There is no immediate word on the cause. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wireupdate.com/2016/03/04/power-coming-back-on-in-syria-after-massive-blackout/" rel="nofollow">(WireUpdate.com)</a></li>
<li>Five people, including an 18-month-old baby, are missing from an <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesian</a> ferryboat traveling from <a href="/wiki/Bali" title="Bali">Bali</a> to <a href="/wiki/East_Java" title="East Java">East Java</a> that sank in the <a href="/wiki/Bali_Strait" title="Bali Strait">Bali Strait</a>; 76 people have been rescued. <a class="external text" href="http://jakartaglobe.beritasatu.com/news/76-rescued-five-missing-bali-ferry-capsizes/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jakarta Globe</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/South_China_Sea_disputes" title="South China Sea disputes">South China Sea disputes</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">U.S. Navy</a> dispatches a <a href="/wiki/Carrier_strike_group" title="Carrier strike group">carrier strike group</a> containing the <a href="/wiki/Nimitz-class_aircraft_carrier" title="Nimitz-class aircraft carrier"><i>Nimitz</i>-class</a> <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_reactor" title="Nuclear reactor">nuclear-powered</a> <a href="/wiki/Supercarrier" title="Supercarrier">supercarrier</a> <a href="/wiki/USS_John_C._Stennis" title="USS John C. Stennis">USS <i>John C. Stennis</i></a> to the South China Sea. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/checkpoint/wp/2016/03/03/navy-aircraft-carrier-group-moves-into-contested-south-china-sea-pentagon-says/" rel="nofollow">(Washington Post)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan%E2%80%93United_States_relations" title="Japan–United States relations">Japan–United States relations</a>, <a href="/wiki/Relocation_of_Marine_Corps_Air_Station_Futenma" title="Relocation of Marine Corps Air Station Futenma">Relocation of Marine Corps Air Station Futenma</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Japan" title="Prime Minister of Japan">Japanese Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Shinz%C5%8D_Abe" title="Shinzō Abe">Shinzō Abe</a> agrees to suspend work to expand the <a href="/wiki/Okinawa_Island#U.S._military" title="Okinawa Island">U.S. military base</a> on <a href="/wiki/Okinawa_Island" title="Okinawa Island">Okinawa Island</a>. Abe says his government will follow the court recommendation and settle several lawsuits over <a href="/wiki/Landfill" title="Landfill">landfill</a> work carried out to prepare for new <a href="/wiki/Runway" title="Runway">runways</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-04/japan-to-suspend-work-at-controversial-u-s-base-in-okinawa" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/France%E2%80%93Germany_relations" title="France–Germany relations">France–Germany relations</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> wants <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> to shut down the <a href="/wiki/Fessenheim_Nuclear_Power_Plant" title="Fessenheim Nuclear Power Plant">Fessenheim Nuclear Power Plant</a> near its border as soon as possible following media reports the April 9, 2014, incident was more serious than reported. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/germany-demands-closure-french-nuclear-plant-border-37392778" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw.com/en/reports-fessenheim-nuclear-accident-played-down-by-authorities/a-19093477" rel="nofollow">(Deutsche Welle)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_migrant_crisis" title="European migrant crisis">European migrant crisis</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Commission" title="European Commission">European Commission</a> proposes an end-of-year target date for lifting internal border checks and restoring the 26-nation, passport-free <a href="/wiki/Schengen_Area" title="Schengen Area">Schengen Area</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-europe-migrants-schengen-idUSKCN0W613U" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-04/eu-weighs-year-end-target-for-lifting-internal-border-controls" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Brazil" title="Law enforcement in Brazil">Brazilian police</a> raid the home of <a href="/wiki/President_of_Brazil" title="President of Brazil">ex-President</a> <a href="/wiki/Luiz_In%C3%A1cio_Lula_da_Silva" title="Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva">Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva</a> in relation to the <a href="/wiki/Petrobras" title="Petrobras">Petrobras</a> scandal. Lula is brought in for questioning. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-latin-america-35725415" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Media_freedom_in_Turkey" title="Media freedom in Turkey">Media freedom in Turkey</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkish</a> court places the influential <i><a href="/wiki/Zaman_(newspaper)" title="Zaman (newspaper)">Zaman</a></i> newspaper under state control. <i>Zaman</i> is closely linked to the <a href="/wiki/G%C3%BClen_movement" title="Gülen movement">Gülen movement</a> of influential <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a>-based cleric <a href="/wiki/Fethullah_G%C3%BClen" title="Fethullah Gülen">Fethullah Gülen</a>, a former ally of <a href="/wiki/President_of_Turkey" title="President of Turkey">Turkish President</a> <a href="/wiki/Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan" title="Recep Tayyip Erdoğan">Recep Tayyip Erdoğan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-35729114" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">United States Supreme Court</a>, with only <a href="/wiki/Clarence_Thomas" title="Clarence Thomas">Justice Clarence Thomas</a> dissenting, blocks implementation of a <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">Louisiana</a> law that could have forced all but one of the state's <a href="/wiki/Abortion_clinic" title="Abortion clinic">abortion clinics</a> to close, and restores an earlier judicial ban on enforcing the 2014 law. Last week, a federal appeals court said the law could be enforced. <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/nation/la-na-court-louisiana-abortion-20160304-story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.globalpost.com/article/6742171/2016/03/04/supreme-court-blocks-louisiana-abortion-restrictions" rel="nofollow">(AFP via GlobalPost)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Samoan_general_election,_2016" title="Samoan general election, 2016">Samoan general election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/Samoa" title="Samoa">Samoa</a> go to the polls for a general election. <a class="external text" href="http://www.radionz.co.nz/international/pacific-news/298064/voting-underway-in-samoa's-general-election" rel="nofollow">(Radio New Zealand)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Serbian_parliamentary_election,_2016" title="Serbian parliamentary election, 2016">Serbian parliamentary election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_Serbia" title="President of Serbia">Serbian President</a> <a href="/wiki/Tomislav_Nikoli%C4%87" title="Tomislav Nikolić">Tomislav Nikolić</a>, at the request of <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Serbia" title="Prime Minister of Serbia">Serbian Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Aleksandar_Vu%C4%8Di%C4%87" title="Aleksandar Vučić">Aleksandar Vučić</a>, dissolves <a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_(Serbia)" title="National Assembly (Serbia)">parliament</a> and calls for early elections to take place on April 24. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/serbia-parliament-dissolved-early-elections-vucic/27589299.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2016" title="United States presidential election, 2016">United States presidential election, 2016</a>, <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_presidential_candidates,_2016" title="Republican Party presidential candidates, 2016">Republican Party presidential candidates, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ben_Carson" title="Ben Carson">Ben Carson</a> suspends <a href="/wiki/Ben_Carson_presidential_campaign,_2016" title="Ben Carson presidential campaign, 2016">his campaign</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican Party</a> nomination. The expected announcement was made during a speech at the 2016 <a href="/wiki/Conservative_Political_Action_Conference" title="Conservative Political Action Conference">Conservative Political Action Conference</a> (CPAC). <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2016-election/ben-carson-suspends-2016-campaign-cpac-n532056" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_European_Union_membership_referendum,_2016" title="United Kingdom European Union membership referendum, 2016">United Kingdom European Union membership referendum, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/British_Chambers_of_Commerce" title="British Chambers of Commerce">British Chambers of Commerce</a> suspends Director-General <a href="/wiki/John_Longworth_(businessman)" title="John Longworth (businessman)">John Longworth</a> for announcing his personal views on Brexit. The BCC, whose members are split on this issue, will not campaign for either side. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/business-35732291" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> March 5, 2016<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2016-03-05</span>)</span> (Saturday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_5&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_5&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_5&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Taliban_insurgency" title="Taliban insurgency">Taliban insurgency</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Afghan Taliban</a> releases a statement rejecting peace talks with the government of <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> until <a href="/wiki/Resolute_Support_Mission" title="Resolute Support Mission">foreign forces</a> stop attacking their positions and withdraw from the country. Direct peace talks between the government and the Taliban were expected to take place in <a href="/wiki/Islamabad" title="Islamabad">Islamabad</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> next week. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/afghanistan-taliban-snubs-peace-talks/27591120.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Aden_unrest_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Aden unrest (2015–present)">Aden unrest (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>Gunmen shoot dead the police chief of <a href="/wiki/Aden" title="Aden">Aden</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Tawahi_(Aden)" title="Tawahi (Aden)">Tawahi district</a> and one of his aides. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-yemen-security-idUSKCN0W70MD" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> announces plans to build a railway linking the <a href="/wiki/Tibet" title="Tibet">Tibetan</a> capital <a href="/wiki/Lhasa" title="Lhasa">Lhasa</a> with <a href="/wiki/Chengdu" title="Chengdu">Chengdu</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.channelnewsasia.com/news/asiapacific/china-to-build-second-rai/2575104.html" rel="nofollow">(Channel News Asia)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>More than 60 people are hospitalized after an engine explodes on a crowded <a href="/wiki/Bangkok" title="Bangkok">Bangkok</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>, <a href="/wiki/Water_taxi" title="Water taxi">commuter boat</a>. Police suspect a <a href="/wiki/Liquefied_natural_gas" title="Liquefied natural gas">liquefied natural gas</a> leak caused the blast. The boat operator has been ordered to use <a href="/wiki/Diesel_fuel" title="Diesel fuel">diesel fuel</a> only on its 25-boat fleet. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/184862c9cda348698949d60f936f2bcd/blast-bangkok-river-taxi-injures-several-dozen" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ibtimes.com/thailand-ferry-explosion-injures-more-60-cause-blast-unclear-2330732" rel="nofollow">(<i>International Business Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea%E2%80%93Philippines_relations" title="North Korea–Philippines relations">North Korea–Philippines relations</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> impounds a <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korean</a> cargo ship in line with new <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">UN</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_United_Nations_Security_Council_resolutions_concerning_North_Korea" title="List of United Nations Security Council resolutions concerning North Korea">sanctions on North Korea</a> in response to <a href="/wiki/Pyongyang" title="Pyongyang">Pyongyang</a>'s recent <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2016_North_Korean_nuclear_test" title="2016 North Korean nuclear test">nuclear test</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kwangmy%C5%8Fngs%C5%8Fng-4" title="Kwangmyŏngsŏng-4">missile launch</a>. Presidential spokesman, <a href="/wiki/Manolo_Quezon" title="Manolo Quezon">Manolo Quezon</a>, said the 6,830-tonne cargo ship would not be allowed to leave the <a href="/wiki/Port_of_Subic" title="Port of Subic">Port of Subic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luzon" title="Luzon">Luzon</a>, where it has been docked for three days, and that its crew would be deported. <a class="external text" href="http://www.straitstimes.com/asia/se-asia/the-philippines-impounds-north-korean-ship-in-response-to-new-un-sanctions" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Media_freedom_in_Turkey" title="Media freedom in Turkey">Media freedom in Turkey</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Turkey" title="Law enforcement in Turkey">Turkish police</a> fire <a href="/wiki/Tear_gas" title="Tear gas">tear gas</a> at protesters outside the <a href="/wiki/Istanbul" title="Istanbul">Istanbul</a> headquarters of the <i><a href="/wiki/Zaman_(newspaper)" title="Zaman (newspaper)">Zaman</a></i> newspaper which has been taken over by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Turkey" title="Government of Turkey">Turkish government</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-35732424" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Gunmen dressed in police uniforms kill at least ten people in the <a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduran</a> capital of <a href="/wiki/Tegucigalpa" title="Tegucigalpa">Tegucigalpa</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/uk-honduras-attack-idUKKCN0W8021" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_presidential_primaries,_2016" title="Republican Party presidential primaries, 2016">Republican Party presidential primaries, 2016</a>, <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_presidential_primaries,_2016" title="Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2016">Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voters in the states of <a href="/wiki/Kansas" title="Kansas">Kansas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">Louisiana</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nebraska" title="Nebraska">Nebraska</a>, <a href="/wiki/Maine" title="Maine">Maine</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kentucky" title="Kentucky">Kentucky</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Commonwealth of Puerto Rico</a> participate in a party <a href="/wiki/Caucus" title="Caucus">caucus</a> or vote in a <a href="/wiki/Primary_election" title="Primary election">primary election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.uspresidentialelectionnews.com/2016-presidential-primary-schedule-calendar/" rel="nofollow">(Presidential Primary Schedule)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ted_Cruz" title="Ted Cruz">Ted Cruz</a> wins the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Republican_Party_United_States" title="Republican Party United States">Republican Party</a> caucus in <a href="/wiki/Kansas" title="Kansas">Kansas</a> and <a href="/wiki/Maine" title="Maine">Maine</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/news/kansas-republican-caucus-results-live-updates/" rel="nofollow">(CBS News)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/us-news/live/2016/mar/05/trump-clinton-sanders-michigan-maine-primary-caucuses" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">Louisiana</a> primary and Kentucky caucus. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/Politics/wireStory/donald-trump-wins-gop-presidential-primary-louisiana-37432187" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/elections/results/kentucky" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bernie_Sanders" title="Bernie Sanders">Bernie Sanders</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democratic Party</a> contests in Kansas and <a href="/wiki/Nebraska" title="Nebraska">Nebraska</a> while <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> wins in <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">Louisiana</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2016/03/05/politics/kansas-kentucky-louisiana-maine-nebraska-highlights/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a>, <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/post-politics/wp/2016/03/05/bernie-sanders-projected-to-win-the-democratic-caucuses-in-nebraska/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.nola.com/politics/index.ssf/2016/03/live_coverage_of_louisianas_20.html" rel="nofollow">(NOLA)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/election/primaries/states/la/Rep" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Slovak_parliamentary_election,_2016" title="Slovak parliamentary election, 2016">Slovak parliamentary election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/Slovakia" title="Slovakia">Slovakia</a> choose representatives for all 150 <a href="/wiki/National_Council_(Slovakia)" title="National Council (Slovakia)">National Council</a> seats. While anti-migrant <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Slovakia" title="Prime Minister of Slovakia">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Robert_Fico" title="Robert Fico">Robert Fico's</a> <a href="/wiki/Direction_%E2%80%93_Social_Democracy" title="Direction – Social Democracy">Smer party</a> is expected to lose its parliamentary majority, it should be in position to lead a <a href="/wiki/Coalition_government" title="Coalition government">coalition government</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.firstpost.com/world/slovaks-likely-to-re-elect-anti-immigrant-leftist-fico-reuters-2658036.html" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Firstpost)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://neurope.eu/article/slovakia-goes-to-the-polls/" rel="nofollow">(<i>New Europe</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-05/fico-s-slovak-election-win-trails-expectations-exit-poll-shows" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Samoan_general_election,_2016" title="Samoan general election, 2016">Samoan general election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Results from yesterday's election indicate that the ruling <a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Protection_Party" title="Human Rights Protection Party">Human Rights Protection Party</a> will retain power in a landslide. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2016-03-05/samoan-ruling-party-set-for-landslide-victory-in-election/7223890" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Anti-corruption_campaign_in_China" title="Anti-corruption campaign in China">Anti-corruption campaign in China</a>:
<ul>
<li>The former party chief of <a href="/wiki/Liaoning" title="Liaoning">Liaoning</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jilin" title="Jilin">Jilin</a> provinces, <a href="/wiki/Wang_Min" title="Wang Min">Wang Min</a>, is placed under investigation by the <a href="/wiki/Central_Commission_for_Discipline_Inspection" title="Central Commission for Discipline Inspection">Central Commission for Discipline Inspection</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.scmp.com/news/china/policies-politics/article/1920899/graft-cloud-falls-over-former-communist-party-boss" rel="nofollow">(SCMP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> March 6, 2016<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2016-03-06</span>)</span> (Sunday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_6&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_6&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_6&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
