<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iraqi_Civil_War_(2014%E2%80%93present)" title="Iraqi Civil War (2014–present)">Iraqi Civil War (2014–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Suicide_attack" title="Suicide attack">suicide bomber</a> kills at least 60 people and wounds 70 others after ramming his explosives-laden truck into a security checkpoint at one of the entrances to the <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqi</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Hillah" title="Hillah">Hillah</a>, south of <a href="/wiki/Baghdad" title="Baghdad">Baghdad</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a> claims responsibility for the attack. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-mideast-crisis-iraq-blast-idUSKCN0W80G3" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2016/03/06/at-least-11-killed-in-baghdad-suicide-attack.html" rel="nofollow">(FOX News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/iraq-suicide-attack-kills-least-11-south-baghdad-104807422.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Yahoo! News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Battle_of_Aleppo_(2012%E2%80%93present)" title="Battle of Aleppo (2012–present)">Battle of Aleppo (2012–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>At least nine civilians are killed and dozens are injured after rockets and mortars hit the mainly <a href="/wiki/Kurds_in_Syria" title="Kurds in Syria">Kurdish</a> neighborhood of <a href="/wiki/Sheikh_Maqsood" title="Sheikh Maqsood">Sheikh Maqsood</a> in the city of <a href="/wiki/Aleppo" title="Aleppo">Aleppo</a>. The neighborhood is controlled by the <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Protection_Units" title="People's Protection Units">People's Protection Units</a> (YPG). <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/uk-mideast-crisis-syria-aleppo-idUKKCN0W80S2" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/First_Lady_of_the_U.S." title="First Lady of the U.S.">First Lady of the U.S.</a> <a href="/wiki/Nancy_Reagan" title="Nancy Reagan">Nancy Reagan</a> dies at age 94. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/news/us-news/nancy-reagan-dead-94-n532871" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Twelve <a href="/wiki/Coal_mining" title="Coal mining">coal miners</a> are killed following a gas leak in a mine near the Chinese city of <a href="/wiki/Baishan" title="Baishan">Baishan</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jilin_province" title="Jilin province">Jilin province</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sbs.com.au/news/article/2016/03/07/12-killed-gas-leak-china-coal-mine" rel="nofollow">(AAP via SBS)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_migrant_crisis" title="European migrant crisis">European migrant crisis</a>
<ul>
<li>At least 25 migrants, including 10 children, drown after their wooden boat capsizes in the <a href="/wiki/Aegean_Sea" title="Aegean Sea">Aegean Sea</a> near the seaside town of <a href="/wiki/Didim" title="Didim">Didim</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coast_Guard_Command" title="Coast Guard Command">Turkish Coast Guard</a> was able to rescue 15 people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ibtimes.com/least-25-migrants-drown-after-boat-capsizes-turkish-coast-2331267" rel="nofollow">(<i>International Business Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://au.news.yahoo.com/world/a/31027765/migrant-boat-sinks-off-turkey-18-dead/" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Yahoo7 News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="North Korea and weapons of mass destruction">North Korea and weapons of mass destruction</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> threatens a pre-emptive nuclear strike against <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> in response to the two nations' annual joint military exercise which <a href="/wiki/Pyongyang" title="Pyongyang">Pyongyang</a> considers is a pretext for an invasion. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtontimes.com/news/2016/mar/6/north-korea-threatens-nuclear-strike-against-us-so/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> billionaire <a href="/wiki/Babak_Zanjani" title="Babak Zanjani">Babak Zanjani</a> is sentenced to death for corruption. Zanjani was arrested in December 2013 after accusations that he withheld billions in oil revenue channelled through his companies. He denies the allegations. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-35739377" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Interior_(Egypt)" title="Ministry of Interior (Egypt)">Egyptian interior minister</a> Magdy Abdel-Ghaffar accuses <a href="/wiki/Hamas" title="Hamas">Hamas</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Muslim_Brotherhood_in_Egypt" title="Muslim Brotherhood in Egypt">Egyptian Muslim Brotherhood</a> in the June 2015 assassination of Attorney General <a href="/wiki/Hisham_Barakat" title="Hisham Barakat">Hisham Barakat</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.laht.com/article.asp?ArticleId=2407154&amp;CategoryId=12395" rel="nofollow">(<i>Latin American Herald Tribune</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.debka.com/newsupdatepopup/15326/Egypt-accuses-Hamas-of-hand-in-chief-prosecutor%C3%A2%E2%82%AC%E2%84%A2s-assassination" rel="nofollow">(Debkafile)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Beninese_presidential_election,_2016" title="Beninese presidential election, 2016">Beninese presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/Benin" title="Benin">Benin</a> go to the polls for the first round of voting in a presidential election with 33 candidates vying to replace current <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_of_Benin" title="President of Benin">President</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thomas_Yayi_Boni" title="Thomas Yayi Boni">Thomas Yayi Boni</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-06/record-number-of-hopefuls-seek-benin-presidency-in-election" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Thousands of people gather in the <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgian</a> capital of <a href="/wiki/Tbilisi" title="Tbilisi">Tbilisi</a> to protest against their government's negotiations with <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> state-owned oil company <a href="/wiki/Gazprom" title="Gazprom">Gazprom</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/anti-russia-rally-georgia-gazprom/27592474.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2016" title="United States presidential election, 2016">United States presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Marco_Rubio" title="Marco Rubio">Marco Rubio</a> wins the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election_in_Puerto_Rico,_2016" title="United States presidential election in Puerto Rico, 2016">Puerto Rican</a> <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican Party</a> primary. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/election-us-2016-35741360" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bernie_Sanders" title="Bernie Sanders">Bernie Sanders</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election_in_Maine,_2016" title="United States presidential election in Maine, 2016">Maine Democratic caucuses</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/dynamic/stories/U/US_2016_ELECTION_MAINE_DEM?SITE=AP&amp;SECTION=HOME&amp;TEMPLATE=DEFAULT" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Slovak_parliamentary_election,_2016" title="Slovak parliamentary election, 2016">Slovak parliamentary election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Slovakia" title="Prime Minister of Slovakia">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Robert_Fico" title="Robert Fico">Robert Fico's</a> <a href="/wiki/Direction_%E2%80%93_Social_Democracy" title="Direction – Social Democracy">Smer party</a> won 28.3 percent of the vote, but with just 49 seats, lost its majority in the 150-member parliament. The <a href="/wiki/Freedom_and_Solidarity" title="Freedom and Solidarity">Freedom and Solidarity</a> party won 21 seats (12.1%), and the <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_People_(Slovakia)" title="Ordinary People (Slovakia)">Ordinary People</a> party took 19 seats (11.0%). <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailysabah.com/europe/2016/03/07/anti-migrant-fico-wins-slovakias-election-neo-nazis-gain-seats" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Daily Sabah</i>)</a></li>
<li>The right scored first-time seats. The <a href="/wiki/Slovak_National_Party" title="Slovak National Party">Slovak National Party</a> won 15 seats; and, the <a href="/wiki/Kotleba_%E2%80%93_People%27s_Party_Our_Slovakia" title="Kotleba – People's Party Our Slovakia">Kotleba – People's Party Our Slovakia</a> won 14 seats, nearly three times more than predicted. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/slovakia-in-shock-over-far-right-partys-parliament-election-success/2016/03/06/658b1a72-e3d5-11e5-bc08-3e03a5b41910_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.ie/world-news/europe/surprise-wins-for-far-right-in-slovakia-34516970.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Irish Independent</i>)</a></li>
<li>Analysts indicate Fico may find it very difficult to form a new government. Political analyst <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Abraham" title="Samuel Abraham">Samuel Abrahám</a> says coalition-building “could take weeks, even months. ... Fico's rhetoric strengthened the right in Slovakia." <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailytimes.com.pk/foreign/07-Mar-2016/slovakia-s-fico-wins-but-coalition-difficult-in-fragmented-vote" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://azertag.az/en/xeber/933250" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Azerbaijan State News Agency )</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Insurgency_in_the_Maghreb_(2002-present)" title="Insurgency in the Maghreb (2002-present)">Insurgency in the Maghreb (2002-present)</a>
<ul>
<li>At least 50 people are killed, including 33 militants, seven civilians and ten soldiers, in armed clashes between the <a href="/wiki/Tunisian_Army" title="Tunisian Army">Tunisian Army</a> and Islamist militants in the town of <a href="/wiki/Ben_Gardane" title="Ben Gardane">Ben Gardane</a>, near the border with <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-tunisia-security-idUSKCN0W90J6" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2016/03/tunisia-ben-gardane-clashes-160307070914234.html" rel="nofollow">(Al-Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/wires/afp/article-3480104/Three-civilians-19-dead-Tunisia-fighting.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Daily Mail)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_North-West_Pakistan" title="War in North-West Pakistan">War in North-West Pakistan</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_bomber" title="Suicide bomber">suicide bomber</a> hits a court complex in the town of <a href="/wiki/Charsadda_District,_Pakistan#Shabqadar" title="Charsadda District, Pakistan">Shabqadar</a> killing at least 13 people and injuring 36. <a href="/wiki/Jamaat-ul-Ahrar" title="Jamaat-ul-Ahrar">Jamaat-ul-Ahrar</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Tehrik-i-Taliban_Pakistan" title="Tehrik-i-Taliban Pakistan">Pakistani Taliban</a> faction, says the attack is retaliation for <a href="/wiki/Mumtaz_Qadri" title="Mumtaz Qadri">Mumtaz Qadri's</a> execution last week. <a class="external text" href="http://www.voanews.com/content/taliban-suicide-bomber-pakistan/3222653.html" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2016/03/07/Pakistan-suicide-bomber-kills-13-after-execution-of-assassin/9391457357685/" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_Somalia_(2009%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Somalia (2009–present)">War in Somalia (2009–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>According to the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Defense" title="United States Department of Defense">Pentagon</a>, more than 150 <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">al-Shabaab</a> fighters are reportedly killed Saturday by <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> manned and unmanned aircraft strikes targeting a training camp near the central <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somali</a> town of <a href="/wiki/Buloburde" title="Buloburde">Buloburde</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2016/03/07/us-drone-strike-kills-more-than-150-al-shabaab-fighters-pentagon-reveals.html" rel="nofollow">(FOX News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/03/08/world/africa/us-airstrikes-somalia.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Royal_Australian_Navy" title="Royal Australian Navy">Royal Australian Navy</a> seizes a large cache of weapons from a fishing vessel near <a href="/wiki/Oman" title="Oman">Oman</a>'s coast, that was bound for <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>. The Australian Navy, which patrols waters around the <a href="/wiki/Indian_Ocean" title="Indian Ocean">Indian Ocean</a> as part of an <a href="/wiki/Combined_Task_Force_150" title="Combined Task Force 150">international maritime force</a>, said it has seized nearly 2,000 <a href="/wiki/AK-47" title="AK-47">AK-47</a> rifles, 100 <a href="/wiki/Rocket-propelled_grenade" title="Rocket-propelled grenade">rocket-propelled grenade</a> launchers, 49 PKM machine guns, 39 PKM spare barrels and 20 mortar tubes from the <a href="/wiki/Flag_state" title="Flag state">stateless</a> vessel. 20 tonnes of weaponry in total. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-somalia-security-idUSKCN0W918C" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Arab_Air_Force" title="Syrian Arab Air Force">Syrian Arab Air Force</a> or <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> <a href="/wiki/Airstrike" title="Airstrike">airstrike</a> reportedly kills a dozen people at a market selling <a href="/wiki/Diesel_fuel" title="Diesel fuel">diesel fuel</a> in the rebel-held <a href="/wiki/Idlib_Governorate" title="Idlib Governorate">Idlib Governorate</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Observatory_for_Human_Rights" title="Syrian Observatory for Human Rights">Syrian Observatory for Human Rights</a> says the death toll is likely to rise. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-mideast-crisis-syria-idUSKCN0W91JQ" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany's</a> <a href="/wiki/BASF" title="BASF">BASF SE</a>, the <a href="/wiki/List_of_largest_chemical_producers" title="List of largest chemical producers">largest chemical producer in the world</a>, is pursuing a counterbid for <a href="/wiki/DuPont" title="DuPont">DuPont</a> that could short circuit the <a href="/wiki/Delaware" title="Delaware">Delaware</a>-based company's announced merger with fellow American firm, <a href="/wiki/Dow_Chemical_Company" title="Dow Chemical Company">Dow Chemical Company</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-06/basf-said-working-with-banks-to-weigh-counter-bid-for-dupont" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://fortune.com/2016/03/07/basf-is-weighing-a-counterbid-for-dupont/" rel="nofollow">(Fortune)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Apple_Inc." title="Apple Inc.">Apple Inc.</a> must pay the $450 million July 2014 settlement in a <a href="/wiki/Price_fixing" title="Price fixing">price fixing</a> case since the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">U.S. Supreme Court</a> will not hear its appeal of the June 2015 <a href="/wiki/United_States_Court_of_Appeals_for_the_Second_Circuit" title="United States Court of Appeals for the Second Circuit">Court of Appeals</a> ruling that it played a "central role" in a conspiracy with publishers to eliminate retail price competition and raise <a href="/wiki/E-book" title="E-book">e-book</a> prices. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-usa-court-ebooks-idUSKCN0W91LQ" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/politics/articles/2016-03-07/apple-rejected-by-u-s-high-court-in-450-million-e-book-case" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://appleinsider.com/articles/16/03/07/how-to-find-out-if-you-are-included-in-apples-450m-e-book-settlement" rel="nofollow">(AppleInsider)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>In the United States, an <a href="/wiki/Altamont_Corridor_Express" title="Altamont Corridor Express">Altamont Corridor Express</a> (ACE) <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco_Bay_Area" title="San Francisco Bay Area">San Francisco Bay Area</a> commuter train bound for <a href="/wiki/Stockton,_California" title="Stockton, California">Stockton, California</a>, derails and falls into a <a href="/wiki/Stream" title="Stream">creek</a>, injuring 14 people, four in serious condition. The crash shuts down service along the ACE system through Tuesday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/local/lanow/la-me-ln-bay-area-commuter-train-derails-20160307-story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/08/us/california-train-derailment/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea%E2%80%93United_States_relations" title="South Korea–United States relations">South Korea–United States relations</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> start a joint military exercise as <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> repeats threats of "indiscriminate" nuclear strikes. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rappler.com/world/regions/asia-pacific/124908-north-korea-threatens-pre-emptive-nuclear-strike" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Rappler)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Israeli–Palestinian conflict (2015–present)">Israeli–Palestinian conflict</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_Indonesia" title="President of Indonesia">Indonesian President</a> <a href="/wiki/Joko_Widodo" title="Joko Widodo">Joko “Jokowi” Widodo</a> calls on <a href="/wiki/Muslim_world" title="Muslim world">Muslim</a> leaders at the <a href="/wiki/Organisation_of_Islamic_Cooperation" title="Organisation of Islamic Cooperation">Organisation of Islamic Cooperation</a> (OIC) summit meeting in <a href="/wiki/Jakarta" title="Jakarta">Jakarta</a> to unite and be part of the solution on <a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">Palestine</a>, noting the entire world is concerned about its deteriorating situation. Jokowi also criticizes what he calls <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel's</a> "unilateral and illegal policies." <a class="external text" href="http://www.thejakartapost.com/news/2016/03/07/jokowi-calls-unity-reconciliation-palestine.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Jakarta Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.appeal-democrat.com/news/regional_news/asia/indonesia-leader-calls-on-muslim-world-to-unite-on-palestine/article_2dda51ea-7385-555e-8898-54ac43fcb40f.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Appeal-Democrat</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_migrant_crisis" title="European migrant crisis">European migrant crisis</a>
<ul>
<li>Today's <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> summit with <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Turkey" title="Prime Minister of Turkey">Turkish Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Ahmet_Davuto%C4%9Flu" title="Ahmet Davutoğlu">Ahmet Davutoğlu</a> in <a href="/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">Brussels</a>, <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a>, will discuss ways to stanch the flow of European-bound migrants. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/07/europe/europe-migrant-crisis-summit/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.voanews.com/content/eu-looks-to-turkey-to-ease-migrant-crisis/3222611.html" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.consilium.europa.eu/en/meetings/international-summit/2016/07/" rel="nofollow">(Summit website)</a>
<ul>
<li>The EU plans to boost aid to Greece and declare the route north through the <a href="/wiki/Balkans" title="Balkans">Balkans</a> closed. Presently, about 13,000 people are stranded at the <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a>-<a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Macedonia" title="Republic of Macedonia">Macedonia</a> border. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-35741494" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ekathimerini.com/206691/article/ekathimerini/news/eu-set-to-propose-more-greece-aid-as-balkan-route-now-closed" rel="nofollow">(<i>Kathimerini</i>)</a></li>
<li>The leaders plan to give <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> €3bn to take back thousands who don't qualify for asylum. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ekathimerini.com/206691/article/ekathimerini/news/eu-set-to-propose-more-greece-aid-as-balkan-route-now-closed" rel="nofollow">(<i>Kathimerini</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bdlive.co.za/world/europe/2016/03/07/eu-leaders-press-turkey-to-help-ease-migrant-crisis" rel="nofollow">(<i>Business Day</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Amnesty_International" title="Amnesty International">Amnesty International</a> takes on the EU for using Turkey as a buffer to police Europe’s borders. Deputy Director Gauri van Gulik says Europe has an absolute duty to protect refugees and must fast-track significant, unconditional resettlement. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/europe/eu-leaders-to-press-turkey-back-greece-at-migrant-summit/2016/03/07/254d4e06-e440-11e5-a9ce-681055c7a05f_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/M%C3%A9decins_Sans_Fronti%C3%A8res" title="Médecins Sans Frontières">Médecins Sans Frontières</a> (Doctors Without Borders) opens a humanitarian camp for migrants in the <a href="/wiki/Grande-Synthe" title="Grande-Synthe">Grande-Synthe</a> suburb of <a href="/wiki/Dunkirk" title="Dunkirk">Dunkerque</a>, <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/doctors-borders-opens-migrant-camp-france-37464390" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Enlargement_of_the_European_Union" title="Enlargement of the European Union">Enlargement of the European Union</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Embassy_of_Turkey,_London" title="Embassy of Turkey, London">Turkish deputy ambassador</a> to <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">Britain</a> says <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> should be allowed to join the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> in order to help solve the Syrian refugee crisis. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/middle-east/turkey-says-letting-it-join-the-eu-would-help-solve-the-refugee-crisis-a6916606.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israel-United_States_relations" title="Israel-United States relations">Israel-United States relations</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel" title="Prime Minister of Israel">Israeli Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu" title="Benjamin Netanyahu">Benjamin Netanyahu</a> cancels a trip to the United States for an <a href="/wiki/American_Israel_Public_Affairs_Committee" title="American Israel Public Affairs Committee">American Israel Public Affairs Committee</a> conference that was to include a meeting with <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">U.S. President</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/usa-israel-idINKCN0WA0VJ" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/.premium-1.707495" rel="nofollow">(<i>Haaretz</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/03/08/us/politics/netanyahu-calls-off-washington-visit-and-fingers-point.html?_r=0" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Israeli reports indicate Mr. Netanyahu cancelled because he had not been offered a meeting with Mr. Obama. The White House, which states it had not been directly informed of this change of plans, insists Mr. Netanyahu had turned down a chance to meet with the president. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/03/08/us/politics/netanyahu-calls-off-washington-visit-and-fingers-point.html?_r=0" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A gunman, who killed one man, injured two others, and was holding three people hostage, is found dead when an <a href="/wiki/SWAT" title="SWAT">armed tactical response police team</a> storms a building in the <a href="/wiki/Ingleburn,_New_South_Wales" title="Ingleburn, New South Wales">Ingleburn</a> industrial area in suburban <a href="/wiki/Sydney" title="Sydney">Sydney</a>, <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>. All hostages were unharmed. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/nsw/police-ambulances-rush-to-scene-of-shooting-in-sydneys-south-20160307-gnc6zf.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.stuff.co.nz/world/australia/77620675/Sydney-shooting-Police-still-negotiating-with-gunman-after-triple-shooting" rel="nofollow">(Stuff.co.nz)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.klfm967.co.uk/news/world-news/1908521/reports-of-hostages-after-australia-shooting/" rel="nofollow">(Sky News via KLFM)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelan</a> <a href="/wiki/National_Bolivarian_Armed_Forces_of_Venezuela" title="National Bolivarian Armed Forces of Venezuela">security forces</a> search for 30 gold miners reportedly killed last week in the <a href="/wiki/Bol%C3%ADvar_(state)" title="Bolívar (state)">state of Bolívar</a> in the country's southeast. Survivor reports state the miners were shot last Friday in a fight for control of a gold deposit by criminals who then hid the bodies. <a href="/wiki/List_of_Governors_of_Bol%C3%ADvar" title="List of Governors of Bolívar">Bolívar Governor</a> <a href="/wiki/Francisco_Rangel_G%C3%B3mez" title="Francisco Rangel Gómez">Francisco Rangel Gómez</a> denies any such massacre occurred. <a class="external text" href="http://latino.foxnews.com/latino/news/2016/03/07/security-forces-search-for-miners-reported-killed-in-venezuela/" rel="nofollow">(EFE via Fox New Latino)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/world/rest-of-world/Venezuela-says-its-probing-alleged-killing-of-miners/articleshow/51295002.cms" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via <i>The Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pitcairn_sexual_assault_trial_of_2004" title="Pitcairn sexual assault trial of 2004">Pitcairn sexual assault trial of 2004</a>
<ul>
<li>Former mayor of the <a href="/wiki/Pitcairn_Islands" title="Pitcairn Islands">Pitcairn Islands</a> <a href="/wiki/Mike_Warren_(mayor)" title="Mike Warren (mayor)">Mike Warren</a> is found guilty of downloading more than 1000 images and videos of child abuse and child pornography while working in child protection and is sentenced to 20 months in prison. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/07/former-pitcairn-mayor-found-guilty-over-child-pornography" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>American sportscaster <a href="/wiki/Erin_Andrews" title="Erin Andrews">Erin Andrews</a> is awarded $55 million damages after a stranger, in 2008, secretly recorded her in the nude through a hotel door <a href="/wiki/Peephole" title="Peephole">peephole</a>, and posted the video on the <a href="/wiki/Internet" title="Internet">Internet</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nydailynews.com/news/national/erin-andrews-awarded-55-million-nude-video-lawsuit-article-1.2556066" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Daily News</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2016" title="United States presidential election, 2016">United States presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/Mayor_of_New_York_City" title="Mayor of New York City">New York City mayor</a> <a href="/wiki/Michael_Bloomberg" title="Michael Bloomberg">Michael Bloomberg</a> announces he will not run for president in 2016 because of the impact his candidacy might have on the outcome in November. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/news/michael-bloomberg-rules-out-2016-presidential-run/" rel="nofollow">(CBS News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Research, published in the <a href="/wiki/Peer_review" title="Peer review">peer-reviewed</a> <a href="/wiki/Scientific_journal" title="Scientific journal">scientific journal</a> <i><a href="/wiki/Nature_Geoscience" title="Nature Geoscience">Nature Geoscience</a></i>, confirms that <a href="/wiki/Mercury_(planet)" title="Mercury (planet)">Mercury's</a> darker than expected crusty exterior is from <a href="/wiki/Carbon" title="Carbon">carbon</a>, likely the remains of the planet's ancient <a href="/wiki/Crust_(geology)" title="Crust (geology)">surface crust</a> of <a href="/wiki/Graphite" title="Graphite">graphite</a>, rather than carbon dust from <a href="/wiki/Impact_event" title="Impact event">comet impacts</a> as previously postulated. <a class="external text" href="http://www.csmonitor.com/Science/2016/0307/Mystery-of-Mercury-What-makes-the-planet-s-surface-so-dark" rel="nofollow">(<i>Christian Science Monitor</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/speaking-of-science/wp/2015/03/30/scientists-find-the-invisible-paint-that-makes-mercury-darker-than-dark/?tid=a_inl" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nature.com/ngeo/journal/vaop/ncurrent/full/ngeo2669.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Nature Geoscience</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> <a href="/wiki/Tennis" title="Tennis">tennis</a> star <a href="/wiki/Maria_Sharapova" title="Maria Sharapova">Maria Sharapova</a> tests positive for <a href="/wiki/Meldonium" title="Meldonium">meldonium</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2016_Australian_Open" title="2016 Australian Open">2016 Australian Open</a> tennis championship. She has taken the drug since 2006 on prescription for health issues. <a href="/wiki/World_Anti-Doping_Agency" title="World Anti-Doping Agency">World Anti-Doping Agency</a> <a href="/wiki/Craig_Reedie" title="Craig Reedie">President Craig Reedie</a> says an athlete found guilty of using meldonium would normally face a one-year suspension. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/sport/tennis/35750285" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nola.com/sports/index.ssf/2016/03/maria_sharapova_admits_failing.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Times-Picayune</i>)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nike,_Inc." title="Nike, Inc.">Nike</a> suspends ties with Sharapova after the positive test is revealed. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-tennis-sharapova-idUSKCN0W929E" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxsports.com/tennis/story/nike-maria-sharapova-suspends-deal-positive-drug-test-030716" rel="nofollow">(Fox Sports)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/American_football" title="American football">American football</a> <a href="/wiki/Quarterback" title="Quarterback">quarterback</a> <a href="/wiki/Peyton_Manning" title="Peyton Manning">Peyton Manning</a> retires after eighteen seasons in the <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">National Football League</a> with two <a href="/wiki/Super_Bowl" title="Super Bowl">Super Bowl</a> championships, five <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League_Most_Valuable_Player_Award" title="National Football League Most Valuable Player Award">MVP awards</a>, and single-season and career league records for most passing yards and <a href="/wiki/Touchdown" title="Touchdown">touchdown</a> passes. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nfl.com/news/story/0ap3000000641930/article/peyton-manning-announces-retirement-from-nfl" rel="nofollow">(NFL)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Spillover_of_the_Syrian_Civil_War" title="Spillover of the Syrian Civil War">Spillover of the Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li>Mortar shells fired from <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a> kill at least one person and injure another in the <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkish</a> border town of <a href="/wiki/Kilis" title="Kilis">Kilis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/uk-mideast-crisis-turkey-syria-idUKKCN0WA1J3" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Israeli–Palestinian conflict (2015–present)">Israeli–Palestinian conflict</a>
<ul>
<li>Three terror attacks are reported that result in the deaths of four <a href="/wiki/Palestinians" title="Palestinians">Palestinians</a> and an American tourist with 12 Israelis wounded, including two <a href="/wiki/Israel_Police" title="Israel Police">Israeli policemen</a>, as <a href="/wiki/Vice_President_of_the_United_States" title="Vice President of the United States">United States Vice President</a> <a href="/wiki/Joe_Biden" title="Joe Biden">Joe Biden</a> arrives in <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> for a two-day visit that includes meetings with Israeli and Palestinian leaders.One of the attacks occurred less than a kilometer from where Joe Biden was at the time. <a class="external text" href="http://www.9and10news.com/story/31413844/biden-arrives-in-israel-amid-rash-in-palestinian-attacks" rel="nofollow">(AP via WWTV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/israel-palestinian-woman-stab-officers-killed-37483085" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/08/middleeast/israel-violence/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>The deceased American is Taylor Force, a West Point graduate and former <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army#Commissioned_officers" title="United States Army">U.S. Army officer</a> from <a href="/wiki/Lubbock,_Texas" title="Lubbock, Texas">Lubbock, Texas</a>, who was in the first year of a MBA program at <a href="/wiki/Vanderbilt_University" title="Vanderbilt University">Vanderbilt University</a>. Force was part of a 33-person Vanderbilt group that was in Israel to study <a href="/wiki/Entrepreneurship#Background" title="Entrepreneurship">global entrepreneurship</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/08/middleeast/israel-violence/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.chron.com/news/houston-texas/article/Texas-man-killed-in-Tel-Aviv-mass-stabbing-6878717.php" rel="nofollow">(<i>Houston Chronicle</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Spillover of the <a href="/wiki/Libyan_Civil_War_(2014%E2%80%93present)" title="Libyan Civil War (2014–present)">Libyan Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Tunisian_Army" title="Tunisian Army">army</a> and security forces kill another five suspected terrorists in an operation near the <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libyan</a> border. <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/five-terrorists-killed-security-operation-near-tunisia-libya-230124253.html;_ylt=AwrC0wzxXN9W3GsALVPQtDMD;_ylu=X3oDMTByOHZyb21tBGNvbG8DYmYxBHBvcwMxBHZ0aWQDBHNlYwNzcg--" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Yahoo! News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Military_intervention_against_ISIL" title="Military intervention against ISIL">Military intervention against ISIL</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Defense" title="United States Department of Defense">United States military</a> says <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL's</a> so-called minister-of-war, <a href="/wiki/Abu_Omar_al-Shishani" title="Abu Omar al-Shishani">Abu Omar al-Shishani</a>, né Tarkhan Tayumurazovich Batirashvili, appears to have been killed in a U.S. <a href="/wiki/Airstrike" title="Airstrike">air strike</a> near the town of <a href="/wiki/Al-Shaddadah" title="Al-Shaddadah">Al-Shaddadi</a> in <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msn.com/en-us/news/world/islamic-states-minister-of-war-likely-killed-in-us-air-strike-officials/ar-AAgxCvq#image=1" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via msn.com)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/International_Women%27s_Day" title="International Women's Day">International Women's Day</a> is celebrated. The International Women’s Day theme for 2016 is "Planet 50-50 by 2030: Step It Up for Gender Equality". <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/morning-mix/wp/2016/03/08/celebrating-international-womens-day-around-the-world/" rel="nofollow">(The Washington Post)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Health and medicine</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zika_virus_outbreak_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Zika virus outbreak (2015–present)">Zika virus outbreak (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a> cautions pregnant women against traveling to areas where there is ongoing transmission of <a href="/wiki/Zika_virus" title="Zika virus">Zika virus</a>, echoing earlier alerts from the <a href="/wiki/Centers_for_Disease_Control_and_Prevention" title="Centers for Disease Control and Prevention">U.S. Centers for Disease Control and Prevention</a>, and other health agencies in areas where virus infection has been prevalent. <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization#Assembly_and_Executive_Board" title="World Health Organization">Director General</a> <a href="/wiki/Margaret_Chan" title="Margaret Chan">Margaret Chan</a> says evidence strongly suggests <a href="/wiki/Transmission_(medicine)#Sexual" title="Transmission (medicine)">sexual transmission</a> is more common than previously assumed. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/to-your-health/wp/2016/03/08/stronger-zika-links-to-sexual-transmission-birth-defects-who-says/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Export restrictions placed by the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Commerce" title="United States Department of Commerce">commerce department of the United States</a> against <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>'s state-owned <a href="/wiki/ZTE" title="ZTE">ZTE</a> for alleged violations of U.S.-imposed <a href="/wiki/Trade_barrier" title="Trade barrier">export controls</a> on Iran takes effect. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-zte-usa-china-idUSKCN0W80AV" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/us-hits-chinese-telecom-firm-zte-sanctions-selling-to-iran-high-goods/27596680.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_migrant_crisis" title="European migrant crisis">European migrant crisis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Enlargement_of_the_European_Union" title="Enlargement of the European Union">Enlargement of the European Union</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> and <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> agree on broad principles for a plan to ease the migration crisis which includes returning thousands of <a href="/wiki/Emigration" title="Emigration">migrants</a> to Turkey. For this, the EU will swiftly ease <a href="/wiki/Visa_requirements_for_Turkish_citizens" title="Visa requirements for Turkish citizens">visa requirements</a> for <a href="/wiki/Turkish_nationality_law" title="Turkish nationality law">Turks</a> and speed up <a href="/wiki/Minister_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Turkey)" title="Minister of Foreign Affairs (Turkey)">Ankara's</a> <a href="/wiki/Enlargement_of_the_European_Union#Mediterranean_enlargements" title="Enlargement of the European Union">EU accession</a> talks. A final agreement is to be ready for next week's two-day EU summit in <a href="/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">Brussels</a>, <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.voanews.com/content/european-union-turkey-agree-details-migrant-accord/3224260.html" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-35749837" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.consilium.europa.eu/en/meetings/european-council/2016/03/17-18/" rel="nofollow">(March 17-18, 2016, EU agenda)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> and <a href="/wiki/Human_rights_group" title="Human rights group">human rights groups</a> warn the tentative EU deal with Turkey that would return <a href="/wiki/Illegal_immigration" title="Illegal immigration">irregular migrants</a> in exchange for political and financial rewards could be illegal. <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_High_Commissioner_for_Refugees" title="United Nations High Commissioner for Refugees">U.N. High Commissioner for Refugees</a> <a href="/wiki/Filippo_Grandi" title="Filippo Grandi">Filippo Grandi</a> says it's unclear whether migrants, set to be returned, would be afforded the refugee protection as stated in international law. <a href="/wiki/Amnesty_International" title="Amnesty International">Amnesty International's</a> Gauri van Gulik says this is outsourcing Europe's refugee responsibility. "The EU is treating Turkey as the only solution it has to the refugee crisis," van Gulik added.<a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-europe-migrants-idUSKCN0WA1D4" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/world/europe/la-fg-europe-turkey-migrants-20160309-story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea%E2%80%93South_Korea_relations" title="North Korea–South Korea relations">North Korea–South Korea relations</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> imposes direct <a href="/wiki/International_sanctions" title="International sanctions">sanctions</a> against <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> that blacklists dozens of Northern companies and people for the first time, and bans ships that have visited North Korean ports in the previous 180 days from its waters. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/south-korea-imposes-new-sanctions-on-north-tells-pyongyang-it-must-change/2016/03/08/15b0d29e-490a-4697-9742-3c81dde5eb5f_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/news/world/2016/03/08/south-korea-unilateral-sanctions/81468684/" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel%E2%80%93Palestine_relations" title="Israel–Palestine relations">Israel–Palestine relations</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Pew_Research_Center" title="Pew Research Center">Pew Research Center</a> survey of Jewish and non-Jewish Israelis, via face-to-face interviews from October 2014 through May 2015, finds deep divisions in Israeli society – not only between <a href="/wiki/Israeli_Jews" title="Israeli Jews">Israeli Jews</a> and the country’s <a href="/wiki/Arab_citizens_of_Israel" title="Arab citizens of Israel">Arab citizen</a> minority, but also among the religious subgroups that make up <a href="/wiki/Israeli_Jews#Growth" title="Israeli Jews">Israeli Jewry</a>. An overwhelming majority (98%) of Israeli Jews agree all Jews should have the right to <a href="/wiki/Law_of_Return" title="Law of Return">move to Israel and receive immediate citizenship</a>. Close to half (48 percent) support the expulsion or transfer of Arabs from Israel, yet most secular Jews disagree (58%) with this, as do 54 percent of those in the center politically (more so from the left). Meanwhile, Israeli Arabs, currently about one-in-five of the country's adults, generally do not think Israel can be a Jewish state and a democracy at the same time. Fewer Arabs (down 24 points) think a peaceful, two-state solution is possible, from 74% in 2013 to 50% now. Both groups are skeptical of the peace process: Israeli Arabs question the sincerity of the Israeli government in seeking a peace agreement, while Israeli Jews are equally skeptical about the sincerity of Palestinian leaders. (Pew is a non-partisan American think tank based in <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a>) <a class="external text" href="http://www.pewforum.org/2016/03/08/israels-religiously-divided-society/" rel="nofollow">(Pew Research Center)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_Israel" title="President of Israel">Israeli President</a> <a href="/wiki/Reuven_Rivlin" title="Reuven Rivlin">Reuven Rivlin</a> says the Pew study brings up troubling challenges that need to be dealt with immediately. The finding that 48 percent of Jewish Israelis believe Arabs should be transferred out of Israel is particularly troubling to Rivlin. <a href="/wiki/List_of_Arab_members_of_the_Knesset" title="List of Arab members of the Knesset">MK</a> <a href="/wiki/Yousef_Jabareen" title="Yousef Jabareen">Yousef Jabareen</a>, chair of the <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Israel#Political_centre" title="Politics of Israel">Knesset Lobby for Jewish-Arab Coexistence</a>, said, "The transfer of citizens, for whatever reason, is a crime against humanity, and I am frightened to see that half of those polled support such a step." <a href="/wiki/Human_rights_in_Israel" title="Human rights in Israel">Human rights organizations</a>, such as <a href="/wiki/Amnesty_International#National_sections" title="Amnesty International">Amnesty International Israel</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Anna_Lindh_Euro-Mediterranean_Foundation_for_the_Dialogue_Between_Cultures" title="Anna Lindh Euro-Mediterranean Foundation for the Dialogue Between Cultures">Anne Lindh Foundation's Association for the Advancement of Civic Equality in Israel</a>, denounced <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel" title="Prime Minister of Israel">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu" title="Benjamin Netanyahu">Benjamin Netanyahu</a> for the results of the study. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Israel-News/You-cant-have-democracy-just-for-Jews-Rivlin-said-in-wake-of-Pew-poll-447319" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Australia%E2%80%93United_States_relations" title="Australia–United States relations">Australia–United States relations</a>, <a href="/wiki/Territorial_disputes_in_the_South_China_Sea" title="Territorial disputes in the South China Sea">Territorial disputes in the South China Sea</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Defense" title="United States Department of Defense">U.S. military</a> is in discussions with Australian officials about the possibility of basing <a href="/wiki/Rockwell_B-1_Lancer" title="Rockwell B-1 Lancer">long-range bombers</a>, whose striking distance would include the <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">South China Sea</a>, in <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-southchinasea-australia-usa-idUSKCN0WB05Q" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Media_freedom_in_Turkey" title="Media freedom in Turkey">Media freedom in Turkey</a>
<ul>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/Istanbul" title="Istanbul">Istanbul</a> court places the <a href="/wiki/Cihan_News_Agency" title="Cihan News Agency">Cihan News Agency</a> under state control. The seizure of the <a href="/wiki/Fethullah_G%C3%BClen" title="Fethullah Gülen">Fethullah Gülen</a>-linked news agency comes just days after the Turkish government seized control of the opposition <i><a href="/wiki/Zaman_(newspaper)" title="Zaman (newspaper)">Zaman</a></i> newspaper. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/uk-turkey-politics-gulen-idUKKCN0WA0P5" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Acting on requests from neighboring <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Switzerland" title="Law enforcement in Switzerland">Swiss authorities</a> arrest 15 people sought as suspected members of the <a href="/wiki/%27Ndrangheta" title="'Ndrangheta">'Ndrangheta</a> <a href="/wiki/Organized_crime" title="Organized crime">organized crime</a> syndicate, a <a href="/wiki/Mafia" title="Mafia">Mafia</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Organized_crime" title="Organized crime">organization</a> centered in <a href="/wiki/Calabria" title="Calabria">Calabria</a>, Italy. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/f27dd26ce1c44f97adb9e156a1e266e6/swiss-arrest-15-suspected-members-italian-crime-syndicate" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_presidential_primaries,_2016" title="Republican Party presidential primaries, 2016">Republican Party presidential primaries, 2016</a>, <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_presidential_primaries,_2016" title="Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2016">Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voters in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> states of <a href="/wiki/Mississippi" title="Mississippi">Mississippi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Michigan" title="Michigan">Michigan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hawaii" title="Hawaii">Hawaii</a> and <a href="/wiki/Idaho" title="Idaho">Idaho</a> vote in <a href="/wiki/Primary_election" title="Primary election">primary elections</a> and <a href="/wiki/Caucus" title="Caucus">caucuses</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.uspresidentialelectionnews.com/2016-presidential-primary-schedule-calendar/" rel="nofollow">(Presidential Election News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Mississippi" title="Mississippi">Mississippi</a> Democratic primary. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/elections/results" rel="nofollow">(New York Times)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bernie_Sanders" title="Bernie Sanders">Bernie Sanders</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Michigan" title="Michigan">Michigan</a> Democratic primary. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2016-election/michigan-primary-headlines-tuesday-contests-presidential-races-n533826?cid=eml_nbn_20160308" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a>, <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/the-fix/wp/2016/03/08/the-two-big-warning-signs-for-hillary-clinton-in-michigan/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> wins both the <a href="/wiki/Michigan" title="Michigan">Michigan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mississippi" title="Mississippi">Mississippi</a> Republican primaries and the <a href="/wiki/Hawaii" title="Hawaii">Hawaii</a> caucus. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/americas/us-elections/hillary-clinton-projected-to-win-in-mississippi-a6920506.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ted_Cruz" title="Ted Cruz">Ted Cruz</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Idaho" title="Idaho">Idaho</a> Republican primary. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/election/primaries/states/id/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a>, <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/trump-wins-mississippi-michigan-primaries/2016/03/08/ecb576d6-e539-11e5-b0fd-073d5930a7b7_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The United States <a href="/wiki/Federal_Communications_Commission" title="Federal Communications Commission">Federal Communications Commission</a> announces an expansion of the federal <a href="/wiki/Universal_Service_Fund#Low_income_.28Lifeline.29" title="Universal Service Fund">Lifeline program</a>, which currently offers monthly subsidies for phone and basic cell service, to include broadband Internet service, pending approval at the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Communications_Commission#Commissioners" title="Federal Communications Commission">Commissioners'</a> March 31 meeting. <a class="external text" href="http://thehill.com/regulation/overnights/272267-overnight-regulation-fcc-to-offer-internet-subsidies-to-40m-households" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Hill</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-fcc-internet-subsidy-idUSKCN0WA219" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.multichannel.com/news/fcc/reaction-fcc-broadband-lifeline-piles/403172" rel="nofollow">(Multichannel News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Philippine_presidential_election,_2016" title="Philippine presidential election, 2016">Philippine presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_Philippines" title="Supreme Court of the Philippines">Supreme Court of the Philippines</a>, in a 9-6 ruling, reverses the <a href="/wiki/Commission_on_Elections_(Philippines)" title="Commission on Elections (Philippines)">Commission on Elections</a> order that had disqualified <a href="/wiki/Grace_Poe" title="Grace Poe">Senator Grace Poe</a> from running in the May 9, 2016, presidential election. The petitioners plan to file a motion for reconsideration. <a class="external text" href="http://newsinfo.inquirer.net/771846/sc-poe-can-run-for-president" rel="nofollow">(<i>Philippine Daily Inquirer</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Major_airlines_of_the_United_States" title="Major airlines of the United States">U.S. carrier</a> <a href="/wiki/Alaska_Airlines" title="Alaska Airlines">Alaska Airlines</a> reschedules Flight 870 from <a href="/wiki/Anchorage,_Alaska" title="Anchorage, Alaska">Anchorage, Alaska</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Honolulu" title="Honolulu">Honolulu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hawaii" title="Hawaii">Hawaii</a>, to depart at 2:00 p.m. local time (23:00 UTC) so passengers can view <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse_of_March_9,_2016" title="Solar eclipse of March 9, 2016">2016's only total solar eclipse</a> for 1 minute and 59 seconds, 695 miles north of Honolulu at 37,000 feet. <a class="external text" href="http://www.king5.com/story/news/features/2016/03/07/alaska-airlines-flight-see-total-eclipse-36000-feet/81439796/" rel="nofollow">(KING-TV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://blog.alaskaair.com/alaska-airlines/news/eclipse-flight/" rel="nofollow">(Alaska Airlines)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.theverge.com/2016/3/8/11175142/total-solar-eclipse-march-2016-time-live-stream" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Verge</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nasa.gov/multimedia/nasatv/" rel="nofollow">(NASA TV stream)</a></li>
<li>Boston College (U.S.) researchers, in findings published in the <a href="/wiki/ELife" title="ELife">eLife scientific journal</a>, have uncovered the global spread of an ancient group of retroviruses that affected about 28 of 50 modern mammals' ancestors back as far as 30 million years ago. <a class="external text" href="http://www.hngn.com/articles/186242/20160308/the-history-of-ancient-viruses-that-existed-30-million-years-ago-is-uncovered.htm" rel="nofollow">(Headlines &amp; Global News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.eurekalert.org/pub_releases/2016-03/e-suh030716.php" rel="nofollow">(American Association for the Advancement of Science)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2015–present)">War in Afghanistan (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> militants attack government offices in the southern <a href="/wiki/Helmand_Province" title="Helmand Province">Helmand Province</a> of <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>, with at least 10 killed, including seven of the attackers. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/afghanistan-militants-attack-helmand/27599826.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_Somalia_(2009%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Somalia (2009–present)">War in Somalia (2009–present)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special_Forces_(United_States_Army)" title="Special Forces (United States Army)">U.S. special forces</a>, landing in two helicopters, stage an overnight raid on the <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">al-Shabaab</a>-controlled town of <a href="/wiki/Awdhegele" title="Awdhegele">Awdhegele</a> in <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Lower_Shebelle" title="Lower Shebelle">Lower Shebelle</a> region. Al-Shabaab spokesman, Sheik Abduasiz Abu Musab, confirmed the raid saying "The helicopters landed outside town and the ground forces entered, there was heavy fighting and they were forced to flee"."They were masked and spoke foreign languages which our fighters could not understand," Abu Musab told Reuters. "We do not know who they were but we foiled them." <a class="external text" href="https://www.yahoo.com/news/special-forces-stage-helicopter-raid-somalias-shebab-083932693.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Yahoo! News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-somalia-attacks-islamist-idUSKCN0WB0MT" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Insurgency_in_the_North_Caucasus" title="Insurgency in the North Caucasus">North Caucasus clashes</a>
<ul>
<li>A group of nine <a href="/wiki/Human_rights_activists" title="Human rights activists">human rights activists</a> and <a href="/wiki/Journalist" title="Journalist">journalists</a>, heading to <a href="/wiki/Grozny" title="Grozny">Grozny</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chechnya" title="Chechnya">Chechnya</a>, in a small bus, are attacked on the Kavkaz federal highway near the Ordzhonikidzovskaya settlement at the <a href="/wiki/Ingushetia" title="Ingushetia">Ingushetia</a> border. About 20 masked men assaulted the group, confiscated some mobile phones, and set their vehicle on fire. Two of the journalists, the NGO lawyer, and the bus driver were hospitalized. A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Committee_Against_Torture_(Russia)" title="Committee Against Torture (Russia)">Committee to Prevent Torture</a> representative said this is the first press tour that was not organized by the Chechen government. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wsoctv.com/news/russian-group-journalists-attacked-near-chechnya-border/153075154" rel="nofollow">(AP via WSOC-TV)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://sg.news.yahoo.com/journalists-attacked-chechnya-press-tour-rights-group-191625652.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Yahoo! News)</a><a class="external text" href="http://tass.ru/en/society/861307" rel="nofollow">(Telegraph Agency of the Soviet Union)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The man who served as <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>'s deputy chief trade negotiator for the <a href="/wiki/Trans-Pacific_Partnership" title="Trans-Pacific Partnership">Trans-Pacific Partnership</a> Trade deal, says that there is no room for the sort of renegotiation of a particular provision suggested by former U.S. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Secretary_of_State" title="Secretary of State">Secretary of State</a> <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-trade-tpp-japan-idUSKCN0WC05J" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>At least 30 people are killed after a five-story building still under construction collapses in <a href="/wiki/Lagos" title="Lagos">Lagos</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/nigeriaNews/idAFL5N16H44K" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Seattle" title="Seattle">Seattle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Washington_(state)" title="Washington (state)">Washington</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Seattle_Fire_Department" title="Seattle Fire Department">Seattle Fire Department</a> crew, responding to reports of a <a href="/wiki/Gas_leak" title="Gas leak">natural gas leak</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Greenwood,_Seattle" title="Greenwood, Seattle">Greenwood</a> neighborhood, are caught in an explosion that injures nine firefighters. The explosion blew out windows in businesses and storefronts in the surrounding blocks, destroying three businesses and heavily damaging a fourth. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/post-nation/wp/2016/03/09/massive-explosion-injures-9-firefighters-levels-several-buildings-in-seattle/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.king5.com/story/news/2016/03/09/massive-explosion-rocks-greenwood-several-firefighters-hurt/81518136/" rel="nofollow">(KING-TV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://fireline.seattle.gov/2016/03/09/greenwoodexplosion/" rel="nofollow">(Seattle Fire Department)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Health</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/American_Academy_of_Pediatrics" title="American Academy of Pediatrics">American Academy of Pediatrics</a> recommends physicians ask about basic needs to screen for <a href="/wiki/Diseases_of_poverty" title="Diseases of poverty">poverty-related health risk factors</a>, participate in programs that help children develop resilience, assist families in identifying and maximizing <a href="/wiki/Protective_factor" title="Protective factor">protective factors</a>, and advocate for <a href="/wiki/Social_safety_net" title="Social safety net">safety net programs</a> that assist children. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/to-your-health/wp/2016/03/09/doctors-should-screen-for-poverty-during-child-wellness-visits-american-academy-of-pediatrics-recommends/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.post-gazette.com/news/health/2016/03/09/American-Academy-of-Pediatrics-Pediatrics-group-advocates-screening-for-poverty/stories/201603090032" rel="nofollow">(<i>Pittsburgh Post-Gazette</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.2minutemedicine.com/american-academy-of-pediatrics-calls-for-action-on-poverty/" rel="nofollow">(2 Minute Medicine)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Newark,_New_Jersey" title="Newark, New Jersey">Newark, New Jersey's</a> 30 <a href="/wiki/Newark,_New_Jersey#Public_school" title="Newark, New Jersey">public schools</a> shut off all <a href="/wiki/Drinking_fountain" title="Drinking fountain">water fountains</a> after <a href="/wiki/Lead_poisoning#Water" title="Lead poisoning">elevated levels of lead</a> were found in nearly half of the schools during the <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey_Department_of_Environmental_Protection" title="New Jersey Department of Environmental Protection">state Department of Environmental Protection</a> testing. The agency confirmed lead has not been found in the 280,000 residents' city water supply. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-new-jersey-lead-idUSKCN0WB2N6" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="North Korea and weapons of mass destruction">North Korea and weapons of mass destruction</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea's</a> <a href="/wiki/Korean_Central_News_Agency" title="Korean Central News Agency">state media</a> reports <a href="/wiki/List_of_leaders_of_North_Korea" title="List of leaders of North Korea">Supreme Leader</a> <a href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-un" title="Kim Jong-un">Kim Jong-un</a>, in comments released today, states the country has miniaturized <a href="/wiki/Tactical_nuclear_weapon" title="Tactical nuclear weapon">nuclear warheads</a> to be mounted on <a href="/wiki/Ballistic_missile" title="Ballistic missile">ballistic missiles</a>, and has ordered improvements in the power and precision of its <a href="/wiki/North_Korea_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction#Delivery_systems" title="North Korea and weapons of mass destruction">arsenal</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/northkorea-nuclear-kim-idUSKCN0WA2QK" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_migrant_crisis" title="European migrant crisis">European migrant crisis</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Macedonia" title="Republic of Macedonia">Macedonia</a> says it will no longer let any migrants through its southern border with <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a>, effectively blocking the <a href="/wiki/Balkans" title="Balkans">Balkan</a> route for migrants. The decision came after <a href="/wiki/Slovenia" title="Slovenia">Slovenia</a> barred access to migrants transiting the country. There are around 13,000 migrants now stranded at the Macedonia-Greece border. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-35763101" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabian-led_intervention_in_Yemen" title="Saudi Arabian-led intervention in Yemen">Saudi Arabian-led intervention in Yemen</a>
<ul>
<li>A Saudi-led coalition spokesman announces they have exchanged prisoners with their <a href="/wiki/Houthis" title="Houthis">Houthi opponents</a> and "welcome a pause in the combat on the border." <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Saudi_Arabia)" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs (Saudi Arabia)">Saudi Foreign Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Adel_al-Jubeir" title="Adel al-Jubeir">Adel al-Jubeir</a> said the lull was important to deliver <a href="/wiki/Humanitarian_aid" title="Humanitarian aid">aid</a> and <a href="/wiki/Medical_equipment" title="Medical equipment">medical supplies</a> to people in northern regions of <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>. Yesterday, a Houthi delegation was in <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a> for talks to end the war. Al-Jubeir and his <a href="/wiki/Abdulmalik_Al-Mekhlafi" title="Abdulmalik Al-Mekhlafi">Yemeni counterpart</a> noted formal negotiations to end the fighting can only take place under the auspices of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/yemen-security-iran-idINKCN0WB1YS" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aawsat.com/2016/03/article55348327/saudi-arabia-houthis-swap-prisoners-raising-hopes-peace-talks" rel="nofollow">(<i>Asharq Al-Awsat</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Shahbaz Taseer, the son of <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Punjab,_Pakistan" title="Governor of Punjab, Pakistan">Pakistani Punjab governor</a> <a href="/wiki/Salmaan_Taseer" title="Salmaan Taseer">Salmaan Taseer</a> who was murdered in 2011 for criticizing the country's blasphemy laws, is reunited with his family four-and-a-half years after his kidnapping. Tuesday, Shahbaz was rescued by Pakistani secret service and counter-terrorism operatives in <a href="/wiki/Kuchlak" title="Kuchlak">Kuchlak</a>, <a href="/wiki/Balochistan,_Pakistan" title="Balochistan, Pakistan">Balochistan Province</a>. He had been abducted in <a href="/wiki/Lahore" title="Lahore">Lahore</a> in August 2011, seven months after his father's murder by bodyguard <a href="/wiki/Mumtaz_Qadri" title="Mumtaz Qadri">Mumtaz Qadri</a>. Qadri was executed on February 29, 2016. His death was claimed as the reason for the deadly <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> <a href="/wiki/Suicide_attack" title="Suicide attack">suicide bombing</a> in <a href="/wiki/Charsadda_District,_Pakistan#Shabqadar" title="Charsadda District, Pakistan">Shabqadar</a> two days ago. <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/pakistan-kidnapping-idINKCN0WB19A" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.geo.tv/latest/101971-Shahbaz-Taseer-being-flown-back-to-Quetta-ISPR" rel="nofollow">(GEO TV Lahore)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://tribune.com.pk/story/1061730/shahbaz-taseer-recovered-from-balochistan-after-five-years/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Express Tribune</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Niq%C4%81b_in_Egypt" title="Niqāb in Egypt">Niqāb in Egypt</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Egypt" title="Parliament of Egypt">Parliament of Egypt</a> drafts a law which will ban women from wearing full-face veils such as the <a href="/wiki/Niq%C4%81b" title="Niqāb">niqāb</a> and <a href="/wiki/Burqa" title="Burqa">burqa</a> in public places and government institutions. The move comes after <a href="/wiki/Cairo_University" title="Cairo University">Cairo University</a> recently banned nurses and doctors from wearing veils in medical schools and in teaching hospitals, arguing the ban would “protect patients’ rights and interests”. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/africa/egypt-drafts-bill-to-ban-niqab-veil-in-public-places-a6920701.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>At least eight people have been shot and five killed in <a href="/wiki/Wilkinsburg,_Pennsylvania" title="Wilkinsburg, Pennsylvania">Wilkinsburg, Pennsylvania</a> near the American city of <a href="/wiki/Pittsburgh" title="Pittsburgh">Pittsburgh</a>. '<a class="external text" href="https://au.news.yahoo.com/a/31065681/at-least-4-dead-8-injured-in-pittsburgh-mass-shooting/" rel="nofollow">(Yahoo! 7 News)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/us/2016/03/10/at-least-5-killed-in-shooting-outside-pittsburgh-police-searching-for-2-gunmen.html" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Peruvian_general_election,_2016" title="Peruvian general election, 2016">Peruvian general election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru's</a> electoral court bans two leading candidates - <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Julio_Guzman" title="Julio Guzman">Julio Guzman</a> and <a href="/wiki/C%C3%A9sar_Acu%C3%B1a_Peralta" title="César Acuña Peralta">César Acuña Peralta</a> - from participating in next month's election due to breaches of electoral law. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-latin-america-35768068" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Brazil" title="President of Brazil">President of Brazil</a> <a href="/wiki/Luiz_In%C3%A1cio_Lula_da_Silva" title="Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva">Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva</a> is charged with <a href="/wiki/Money_laundering" title="Money laundering">money laundering</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-latin-america-35770299" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse_of_March_9,_2016" title="Solar eclipse of March 9, 2016">Solar eclipse of March 9, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>A total <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">solar eclipse</a> occurs in <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>, and later, east of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/International_date_line" title="International date line">international date line</a>, in the northern <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">Pacific Ocean</a>. A partial eclipse occurs in <a href="/wiki/Northern_Australia" title="Northern Australia">northern Australia</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/South-East_Asia" title="South-East Asia">South-East Asia</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Asia-Pacific" title="Asia-Pacific">Pacific</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2016-03-09/total-solar-eclipse-attracts-hordes-of-sky-gazers/7232406" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Google_DeepMind" title="Google DeepMind">DeepMind</a> <a href="/wiki/AlphaGo" title="AlphaGo">AlphaGo</a> <a href="/wiki/Artificial_intelligence" title="Artificial intelligence">artificial intelligence</a> program defeats <a href="/wiki/South_Korean_people" title="South Korean people">South Korean</a> grand master <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lee_Se-dol" title="Lee Se-dol">Lee Se-dol</a> in the ancient game of <a href="/wiki/Go_(game)" title="Go (game)">Go</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theage.com.au/technology/sci-tech/go-master-walloped-by-emotionless-challenger-a-google-computer-program-20160309-gnf2hl.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i> via <i>Melbourne Age</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<ul>
<li>Clashes between the <a href="/wiki/Lebanese_Armed_Forces" title="Lebanese Armed Forces">Lebanese Army</a> and jihadist militants near the village of <a href="/wiki/Ras_Baalbek" title="Ras Baalbek">Ras Baalbek</a> in northeast <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a>, close to the <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syrian</a> border, leaves one soldier and eight militants dead. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/wires/afp/article-3486074/Nine-dead-Lebanese-army-clashes-jihadists.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Daily Mail)</a></li>

<ul>

<ul>
<li>Two days of heavy rain in the American state of <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">Louisiana</a> has caused at least three deaths and caused more than a thousand people to evacuate their homes. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/us/2016/03/10/flooding-forces-more-than-1000-from-homes-in-louisiana.html" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a></li>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a> recalls its <a href="/wiki/Charg%C3%A9_d%27affaires" title="Chargé d'affaires">chargé d'affaires</a> from <a href="/wiki/Embassy_of_Venezuela,_Washington,_D.C." title="Embassy of Venezuela, Washington, D.C.">its embassy</a> in <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a> after <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">U.S. President</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> renewed a decree imposing sanctions on several top Venezuelan officials. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-venezuela-usa-idUSKCN0WC029" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> fires two missiles into the <a href="/wiki/Sea_of_Japan" title="Sea of Japan">Sea of Japan</a> and announces its intention to liquidate all remaining <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korean</a> assets on its territory. <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/north-korea-says-liquidate-south-assets-joint-projects-025316445.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Yahoo! News)</a></li>

</dl>
<ul>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> Press Minister <a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Lesin" title="Mikhail Lesin">Mikhail Lesin</a> was found by a American investigation to have died of blunt force injuries in <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a> in November last year. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-russia-mikhaillesin-idUSKCN0WC2W1?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=topNews" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>A jury in a <a href="/wiki/United_States_District_Court_for_the_Middle_District_of_Pennsylvania" title="United States District Court for the Middle District of Pennsylvania">U.S. federal court</a> in <a href="/wiki/Scranton,_Pennsylvania" title="Scranton, Pennsylvania">Scranton, Pennsylvania</a> says that <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cabot_Oil" title="Cabot Oil">Cabot Oil</a> must pay plaintiffs $4.2 million in damages that resulted from Cabot's <a href="/wiki/Hydraulic_fracturing_in_the_United_States" title="Hydraulic fracturing in the United States">fracking</a> operations in the northeast part of that state. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-pennsylvania-fracking-idUSKCN0WC2I8" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
