<ul>
<li>Three candidates are put forward to become <a href="/wiki/President_of_Myanmar" title="President of Myanmar">President of Myanmar</a>: <a href="/wiki/Htin_Kyaw" title="Htin Kyaw">Htin Kyaw</a> and Sai Nyunt Lwin from the <a href="/wiki/National_League_for_Democracy" title="National League for Democracy">National League for Democracy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Khin_Aung_Myint" title="Khin Aung Myint">Khin Aung Myint</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Tatmadaw" title="Tatmadaw">military</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2016-03-10/myanmar-presidential-candidates-announced-htin-kyaw-frontrunner/7236790" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Ireland" title="Ireland">Irish</a> <a href="/wiki/D%C3%A1il_%C3%89ireann" title="Dáil Éireann">Dáil Éireann</a> (parliament) fails to elect a new <a href="/wiki/Taoiseach" title="Taoiseach">taoiseach</a> (Prime Minister) with incumbent <a href="/wiki/Enda_Kenny" title="Enda Kenny">Enda Kenny</a> carrying on as a caretaker. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-35765813" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_11&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Insurgency_in_the_Maghreb_(2002%E2%80%93present)" title="Insurgency in the Maghreb (2002–present)">Insurgency in the Maghreb (2002–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/People%27s_National_Army_(Algeria)" title="People's National Army (Algeria)">Algerian Army</a> kills three suspected Islamist militants near the eastern city of <a href="/wiki/El_Oued" title="El Oued">El Oued</a> and seizes a large quantity of weapons, including six anti-aircraft missiles. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-algeria-security-idUSKCN0WD1ZB" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yemeni_Civil_War_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Yemeni Civil War (2015–present)">Yemeni Civil War (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>More than 50 people have died in fighting in the <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemeni</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Taiz" title="Taiz">Taiz</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.alarabiya.net/en/News/middle-east/2016/03/12/More-than-50-die-in-clashes-in-Yemen-s-besieged-Taiz.html" rel="nofollow">(Al-Arabiya)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>American veterans’ nonprofit charity The <a href="/wiki/Wounded_Warrior_Project" title="Wounded Warrior Project">Wounded Warrior Project</a> board of directors removes chief executive officer Steven Nardizzi and chief operation officer Al Giordano after an independent investigation confirms earlier news reports about lavish spending on employee perks, high overhead, and other perceived malfeasance. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/03/11/us/wounded-warrior-board-ousts-top-two-executives.html?hp&amp;action=click&amp;pgtype=Homepage&amp;clickSource=story-heading&amp;module=first-column-region&amp;region=top-news&amp;WT.nav=top-news" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bangladesh_Bank_money_laundering_case" title="Bangladesh Bank money laundering case">Bangladesh Bank money laundering case</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bangladesh_Bank" title="Bangladesh Bank">Bangladeshi bank officials</a> say unknown <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hacker_(computer_security)" title="Hacker (computer security)">hackers</a> installed <a href="/wiki/Malware" title="Malware">malware</a> in the bank's computer systems in last month's attempt to steal nearly $1 billion from the central bank's account at the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Reserve_Bank_of_New_York" title="Federal Reserve Bank of New York">Federal Reserve Bank of New York</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.businessinsider.com/r-malware-suspected-in-bangladesh-bank-heist-officials-2016-3" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via <i>Business Insider</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/General_Motors" title="General Motors">General Motors</a> acquires Cruise Automation, a three-year old <a href="/wiki/Software_industry" title="Software industry">software company</a> that's been testing <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_car" title="Autonomous car">self-driving cars</a> on the streets of <a href="/wiki/San_Francisco" title="San Francisco">San Francisco</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.businessinsider.com/ap-gm-buys-software-company-to-speed-autonomous-car-development-2016-3" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Business Insider</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>’s <a href="/wiki/Emperor_of_Japan" title="Emperor of Japan">emperor</a> and <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Japan" title="Prime Minister of Japan">prime minister</a> attend a memorial service marking the fifth anniversary of the <a href="/wiki/2011_T%C5%8Dhoku_earthquake_and_tsunami" title="2011 Tōhoku earthquake and tsunami">2011 Tōhoku earthquake and tsunami</a> in which 15,894 people died and caused the <a href="/wiki/Fukushima_Daiichi_nuclear_disaster" title="Fukushima Daiichi nuclear disaster">Fukushima Daiichi nuclear disaster</a>. Many people remain displaced and <a href="/wiki/Fukushima_disaster_cleanup" title="Fukushima disaster cleanup">recovery</a> efforts are ongoing. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/aponline/2016/03/11/world/asia/ap-as-japan-tsunami-anniversary.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_flood_and_mudslide" title="2016 São Paulo flood and mudslide">2016 São Paulo flood and mudslide</a>
<ul>
<li>At least 15 people are killed by flooding and mudslides in and around <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="São Paulo">São Paulo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>, following heavy rain. <a class="external text" href="http://www.channelnewsasia.com/news/world/floods-and-mudslides-kill/2594738.html" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Channel News Asia)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="North Korea and weapons of mass destruction">North Korea and weapons of mass destruction</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-un" title="Kim Jong-un">Kim Jong-un</a>, the <a href="/wiki/List_of_leaders_of_North_Korea" title="List of leaders of North Korea">supreme leader</a> of <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a>, orders the country to conduct more tests of nuclear weapons to improve its capacity. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/wires/reuters/article-3486979/North-Korean-leader-Kim-orders-nuclear-tests-KCNA.html" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via <i>Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Sudanese_Civil_War" title="South Sudanese Civil War">South Sudanese Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li>A new <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> report on <a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">South Sudan</a> describes one of the most horrendous <a href="/wiki/Human_rights_in_South_Sudan" title="Human rights in South Sudan">human rights situations</a> in the world, in particular by Government forces, including use of <a href="/wiki/Wartime_sexual_violence" title="Wartime sexual violence">rape as a widespread weapon of war</a> and recommends the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.N._Security_Council" title="U.N. Security Council">U.N. Security Council</a> consider imposing a comprehensive <a href="/wiki/Arms_embargo" title="Arms embargo">arms embargo</a> on South Sudan and referring the matter to the <a href="/wiki/International_Criminal_Court" title="International Criminal Court">International Criminal Court</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.newsweek.com/south-sudan-human-rights-violations-horrendous-un-435904" rel="nofollow">(<i>Newsweek</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/africa/un-cites-horrendous-human-rights-situation-in-south-sudan/2016/03/11/d25f22ca-e76c-11e5-a9ce-681055c7a05f_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Arab_League" title="Arab League">Arab League</a> declares the <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a>-based Shiite group <a href="/wiki/Hezbollah" title="Hezbollah">Hezbollah</a> a terrorist organization. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-mideast-crisis-arabs-idUSKCN0WD239" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The delegation from <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a> departed from the meeting of the <a href="/wiki/Arab_League" title="Arab League">Arab League</a>, offended by remarks of the Foreign Minister of <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ibrahim_al-Jaafari" title="Ibrahim al-Jaafari">Ibrahim al-Jaafari</a>, an indication of increasing tension among Arab states. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-mideast-crisis-arabs-idUSKCN0WD1J7" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_peace_process" title="Syrian peace process">Syrian peace process</a>
<ul>
<li>The High Negotiations Committee, <a href="/wiki/Syrian_opposition" title="Syrian opposition">Syria's main opposition group</a>, will attend Monday's <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">U.N.</a>-brokered peace talks in <a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">Geneva</a>, <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a>, a day shy of the fifth anniversary of the start of the conflict, and two-plus weeks into the <a href="/wiki/Ceasefire" title="Ceasefire">ceasefire</a> agreement. Although fighting continues, a significant drop in violence has been seen during the <a href="/wiki/Syrian_peace_process#Cessation_of_hostilities_.2827_February_2016.29" title="Syrian peace process">truce</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Geneva_peace_talks_on_Syria_(2016)" title="Geneva peace talks on Syria (2016)">first round of Geneva talks</a> collapsed on Feb. 3 during a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Northern_Aleppo_offensive_(2016)" title="Northern Aleppo offensive (2016)">government offensive</a> against rebels in <a href="/wiki/Aleppo" title="Aleppo">Aleppo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/news/syria-opposition-geneva-peace-talks-bashar-assad-cease-fire-truce/" rel="nofollow">(CBS News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/mideast-crisis-syria-idINKCN0WD1WX" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw.com/en/syrian-truce-holds-as-delegates-prep-for-talks/a-19104260" rel="nofollow">(Deutsche Welle)</a></li>
<li>UN envoy <a href="/wiki/Staffan_de_Mistura" title="Staffan de Mistura">Staffan de Mistura</a> says new elections should be held 18 months from the start of talks, i.e., in September 2017. <a class="external text" href="http://www.firstpost.com/world/un-calls-for-syria-elections-in-18-months-opposition-announces-it-will-attend-peace-talks-next-week-2671070.html?utm_source=FP_CAT_LATEST_NEWS" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Firstpost)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2016" title="United States presidential election, 2016">United States presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Donald_Trump_Chicago_rally_protest" title="2016 Donald Trump Chicago rally protest">2016 Donald Trump Chicago rally protest</a>
<ul>
<li>Donald Trump postpones a rally at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Illinois_at_Chicago" title="University of Illinois at Chicago">University of Illinois at Chicago</a> due to security issues amid fights between protestors and supporters. Five people are arrested, and two officers injured, according to <a href="/wiki/Chicago_Police_Department" title="Chicago Police Department">Chicago police</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2016-03-12/donald-trump-cancels-chicago-rally-amid-protests/7242108" rel="nofollow">(AFP vis ABC News Australia)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/11/politics/donald-trump-chicago-protests/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2016-election/trump-rally-chicago-called-after-clashes-n537001" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
<li>Rival Republican presidential candidates <a href="/wiki/Ted_Cruz" title="Ted Cruz">Ted Cruz</a>, <a href="/wiki/John_Kasich" title="John Kasich">John Kasich</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Marco_Rubio" title="Marco Rubio">Marco Rubio</a> state Mr. Trump bears some responsibility for the disturbance. <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/nation/politics/trailguide/la-na-trailguide-03112016-htmlstory.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Thirty-two people are arrested, all but one charged with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Disturbing_the_peace" title="Disturbing the peace">general peace disturbance</a>, at an earlier Trump event at the <a href="/wiki/Peabody_Opera_House" title="Peabody Opera House">Peabody Opera House</a> in <a href="/wiki/St._Louis" title="St. Louis">St. Louis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Missouri" title="Missouri">Missouri</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.chicagotribune.com/news/nationworld/politics/ct-trump-rally-st-louis-arrests-20160311-story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Chicago Tribune</i>)</a></li>
<li>A Donald Trump supporter is charged with <a href="/wiki/Assault" title="Assault">assault</a> after social media videos show him <a href="/wiki/Sucker_punch" title="Sucker punch">sucker punching</a> a protester at Wednesday's campaign rally in <a href="/wiki/Fayetteville,_North_Carolina" title="Fayetteville, North Carolina">Fayetteville, North Carolina</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/morning-mix/wp/2016/03/10/trump-protester-sucker-punched-at-north-carolina-rally-videos-show/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.csmonitor.com/USA/Politics/Decoder/2016/0311/Has-Donald-Trump-brought-new-whiff-of-violence-to-US-politics" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Christian Science Monitor</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Marco_Rubio" title="Marco Rubio">Marco Rubio</a> OK's supporters voting for <a href="/wiki/John_Kasich" title="John Kasich">John Kasich</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ohio" title="Ohio">Ohio</a> since the state's former governor, "... is the only one who can beat <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> in Ohio." <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/post-politics/wp/2016/03/11/in-anti-trump-move-rubio-frees-up-ohio-supporters-to-vote-for-kasich/?wpmm=1&amp;wpisrc=nl_evening" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.politico.com/blogs/2016-gop-primary-live-updates-and-results/2016/03/marco-rubio-ohio-kasich-220635" rel="nofollow">(Politico)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Donald_Trump_presidential_campaign_endorsements,_2016" title="List of Donald Trump presidential campaign endorsements, 2016">Donald Trump presidential campaign endorsements, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Retired American neurosurgeon and <a href="/wiki/Ben_Carson_presidential_campaign,_2016" title="Ben Carson presidential campaign, 2016">former presidential candidate</a> <a href="/wiki/Ben_Carson" title="Ben Carson">Ben Carson</a> formally endorses <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Mar-a-Lago" title="Mar-a-Lago">Mar-a-Lago</a> landmark estate in <a href="/wiki/Palm_Beach,_Florida" title="Palm Beach, Florida">Palm Beach</a>, <a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">Florida</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/politics/2016/03/10/ben-carson-expected-to-endorse-trump-sources-say.html" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A report by a team of Japanese scientists, published in the <a href="/wiki/American_Association_for_the_Advancement_of_Science" title="American Association for the Advancement of Science">American Association for the Advancement of Science</a> journal <a href="/wiki/Science_(journal)" title="Science (journal)"><i>Science</i></a>, has identified <a href="/wiki/Bacteria" title="Bacteria">bacteria</a> -- isolated from outside a <a href="/wiki/Bottle_recycling" title="Bottle recycling">bottle recycling</a> facility -- that can break down and metabolize <a href="/wiki/Plastic" title="Plastic">plastic</a>. The microbe appears to have evolved a pair of <a href="/wiki/Enzyme" title="Enzyme">enzymes</a> it uses to break down <a href="/wiki/Polyethylene_terephthalate" title="Polyethylene terephthalate">polyethylene terephthalate</a> or PET, the most common <a href="/wiki/Thermoplastic" title="Thermoplastic">thermoplastic polymer</a> resin in consumer products. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/news/plastic-eating-bacteria-could-help-make-trash-disappear/" rel="nofollow">(<i>LiveScience</i> via CBS News)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/speaking-of-science/wp/2016/03/11/these-plastic-eating-bacteria-could-help-cut-down-on-waste/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://science.sciencemag.org/content/351/6278/1196" rel="nofollow">(<i>Science</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Astronaut" title="Astronaut">Astronaut</a> <a href="/wiki/Scott_Kelly_(astronaut)" title="Scott Kelly (astronaut)">Scott Kelly</a> announces his retirement from <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a> effective April 1. Kelly holds the record for the American who has spent the most time in space. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nasa.gov/press-release/astronaut-scott-kelly-to-retire-from-nasa-in-april" rel="nofollow">(NASA)</a></li>
<li>A report from the <a href="/wiki/National_Academies_of_Sciences,_Engineering,_and_Medicine" title="National Academies of Sciences, Engineering, and Medicine">National Academies of Sciences, Engineering, and Medicine</a> states <a href="/wiki/Climatology" title="Climatology">climate science</a> progress makes it possible to accurately detect <a href="/wiki/Global_warming" title="Global warming">global warming's</a> fingerprints on certain <a href="/wiki/Extreme_weather" title="Extreme weather">extreme weather</a> events. There is "high confidence" in studies looking for climate change connections between extreme hot and cold temperatures, while efforts trying to attribute droughts and extreme rainfall has medium confidence. <a class="external text" href="http://www.businessinsider.com/ap-panel-finding-climate-fingerprints-in-wild-weather-is-valid-2016-3" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Business Insider</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.wltx.com/weather/forecast/climate/national-academy-of-sciences-report-links-extreme-weather-to-climate-change/78152696" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i> via WLTX)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www8.nationalacademies.org/onpinews/newsitem.aspx?RecordID=21852" rel="nofollow">(National Academies)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United F.C.</a> (NUFC) appoint <a href="/wiki/Rafael_Ben%C3%ADtez" title="Rafael Benítez">Rafael Benítez</a> as manager on a three-year deal after sacking <a href="/wiki/Steve_McClaren" title="Steve McClaren">Steve McClaren</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/football/2016/03/10/newcastle-sack-steve-mcclaren-rafael-benitez-to-replace-him/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>

<li><a href="/wiki/Iraqi_Civil_War_(2014%E2%80%93present)" title="Iraqi Civil War (2014–present)">Iraqi Civil War (2014–present)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Use_of_chemical_weapons_in_the_Iraqi_Civil_War" title="Use of chemical weapons in the Iraqi Civil War">Use of chemical weapons in the Iraqi Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a> fire mortars containing an unidentified <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chemical_agent" title="Chemical agent">chemical agent</a> killing one and injuring 600 in <a href="/wiki/Taza_Khurmatu" title="Taza Khurmatu">Taza Khurmatu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2016/03/12/iraq-officials-say-islamic-state-chemical-attacks-kill-child-wound-600.html" rel="nofollow">(FOX News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nasdaq.com/article/islamic-state-struck-town-with-chemical-weapons-iraq-says-20160311-00527" rel="nofollow">(NASDAQ)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Naxalite%E2%80%93Maoist_insurgency" title="Naxalite–Maoist insurgency">Naxalite–Maoist insurgency</a>
<ul>
<li>Two <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> <a href="/wiki/Border_Security_Force" title="Border Security Force">Border Security Force</a> soldiers are killed and four injured in a conflict in the state of <a href="/wiki/Chhattisgarh" title="Chhattisgarh">Chhattisgarh</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.hindustantimes.com/india/2-bsf-men-killed-4-injured-in-naxal-encounter-in-chhattisgarh/story-7TBJBbqxxXd2AYXGPpa0YI.html" rel="nofollow">(PTI via <i>Hindustan Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Israeli–Palestinian conflict (2015–present)">Israeli–Palestinian conflict</a>
<ul>
<li>A 10-year-old <a href="/wiki/Palestinians" title="Palestinians">Palestinian</a> boy and his 6-year-old sister in <a href="/wiki/Gaza_City" title="Gaza City">Gaza</a> are killed by fragments from a <a href="/wiki/Air-to-surface_missile" title="Air-to-surface missile">missile</a> fired by an <a href="/wiki/Israeli_Air_Force#Current" title="Israeli Air Force">Israeli aircraft</a> targeting four <a href="/wiki/Hamas" title="Hamas">Hamas</a> training camps after four missiles landed in open areas in <a href="/wiki/Southern_District_(Israel)" title="Southern District (Israel)">southern Israel</a> late yesterday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/world/middleeast/la-fg-gaza-airstrike-20160312-story.html" rel="nofollow">(LA Times)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-israel-palestinians-gaza-idUSKCN0WE09T" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turkey%E2%80%93PKK_conflict_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Turkey–PKK conflict (2015–present)">Turkey–PKK conflict (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Turkish_Air_Force" title="Turkish Air Force">Turkish Air Force</a> airstrikes reportedly kill at least 67 <a href="/wiki/Kurdistan_Workers%27_Party" title="Kurdistan Workers' Party">PKK</a> militants in <a href="/wiki/Iraqi_Kurdistan" title="Iraqi Kurdistan">northern Iraq</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.worldbulletin.net/world/170394/six-killed-in-italian-alps-avalanche" rel="nofollow">(World Bulletin)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.voanews.com/content/turkish-air-strikes-kill-kurdish-militants-in-iraq/3233119.html" rel="nofollow">(VOA News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jaysh_al-Nasr" title="Jaysh al-Nasr">Jaysh al-Nasr</a> rebels say they have shot down a fighter jet over the <a href="/wiki/Hama_Governorate" title="Hama Governorate">Hama Governorate</a> in western <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Observatory_for_Human_Rights" title="Syrian Observatory for Human Rights">Syrian Observatory for Human Rights</a> confirmed the shoot down, saying a rebel group had brought down the jet by firing two heat-seeking missiles. A pro-government source acknowledged that a <a href="/wiki/Mikoyan-Gurevich_MiG-21" title="Mikoyan-Gurevich MiG-21">MiG-21</a> warplane went down over <a href="/wiki/Kafr_Nabudah" title="Kafr Nabudah">Kafr Nabudah</a>, but said it was due to “technical difficulties”, denying it had been shot down. <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/syria-rebels-shot-down-warplane-170059577.html" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Yahoo! News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/12/syrian-government-calls-bashar-al-assad-a-red-line-in-peace-talks" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yemeni_Civil_War_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Yemeni Civil War (2015–present)">Yemeni Civil War (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Aden_unrest_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Aden unrest (2015–present)">Aden unrest</a>
<ul>
<li>Airstrikes on the <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda_in_the_Arabian_Peninsula" title="Al-Qaeda in the Arabian Peninsula">Al-Qaeda</a>-held <a href="/wiki/Al-Mansoura_(Aden)" title="Al-Mansoura (Aden)">Al-Mansoura</a> district in the port city of <a href="/wiki/Aden" title="Aden">Aden</a>, kill at least 17 militants and injure 20 civilians, according to local medics and a <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemeni</a> security official. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/uk-yemen-security-idUKKCN0WF04F" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Reuters reports, on the basis of unnamed sources "familiar with the matter," that <a href="/wiki/Energy_Transfer_Equity" title="Energy Transfer Equity">Energy Transfer Equity</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Private_equity" title="Private equity">private equity</a> concern, is in talks to sell <a href="/wiki/Sunoco" title="Sunoco">Sunoco</a>, a deal which would be valued at more than $2 billion. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-energytransfer-sunoco-exlusive-idUSKCN0WD2MB" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/Avalanche" title="Avalanche">avalanche</a> kills six skiers in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Italian_Alps" title="Italian Alps">Italian Alps</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-italy-avalanche-idUSKCN0WE0KC" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Moment_magnitude_scale" title="Moment magnitude scale">magnitude</a> 6.3 <a href="/wiki/Earthquake" title="Earthquake">earthquake</a> strikes off <a href="/wiki/Atka_Island" title="Atka Island">Atka Island</a>, southwest <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a>. There are no reports of a tsunami. <a class="external text" href="http://bnonews.com/news/index.php/news/id3821" rel="nofollow">(BNO News)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Tugboat" title="Tugboat">tugboat</a> crash on the <a href="/wiki/Hudson_River" title="Hudson River">Hudson River</a> north of <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a> results in one death and two people missing. <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/dynamic/stories/U/US_RIVER_COLLISION_NYOL-?SITE=AP&amp;SECTION=HOME&amp;TEMPLATE=DEFAULT" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>

<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_presidential_primaries,_2016" title="Republican Party presidential primaries, 2016">Republican Party presidential primaries, 2016</a>, <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_presidential_primaries,_2016" title="Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2016">Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/Guam" title="Guam">Guam</a>, <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wyoming" title="Wyoming">Wyoming</a> head to the polls to vote in <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican Party</a> caucuses, while <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democratic Party</a> members vote in the <a href="/wiki/Northern_Mariana_Islands" title="Northern Mariana Islands">Northern Mariana Islands</a> caucus. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2016/03/11/politics/northern-mariana-islands-guam-dc-wyoming-saturday-vote/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ted_Cruz" title="Ted Cruz">Ted Cruz</a> wins the most delegates in <a href="/wiki/Wyoming" title="Wyoming">Wyoming</a>, while <a href="/wiki/Marco_Rubio" title="Marco Rubio">Marco Rubio</a> wins in Washington D.C. <a class="external text" href="http://nypost.com/2016/03/12/ted-cruz-wins-most-delegates-at-stake-in-wyoming/?utm_medium=email&amp;utm_campaign=NY%2520Post%2520Breaking%2520News&amp;utm_source=Sailthru&amp;utm_term=breakingnews_exclusives" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Post</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/us-news/ng-interactive/2016/mar/12/primary-caucus-live-results-wyoming-washington-dc-election-2016" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> wins the Northern Mariana Islands caucus. <a class="external text" href="http://www.breakingnews.com/item/2016/03/13/hillary-clinton-wins-northern-mariana-islands-demo/" rel="nofollow">(NBC News, New York Times <i>via Breaking News)</i></a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump_presidential_campaign,_2016" title="Donald Trump presidential campaign, 2016">Donald Trump presidential campaign, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>A protestor attempts to storm the stage as <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> was talking at a rally in <a href="/wiki/Dayton,_Ohio" title="Dayton, Ohio">Dayton, Ohio</a>, causing <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secret_Service" title="United States Secret Service">Secret Service</a> agents to jump on the stage and form a wall around the presidential candidate amid the chaos. The suspect was identified as Thomas Dimassimo, 32, and was charged with disorderly conduct and inducing panic, according to Chief Mike Etter of the Dayton Police Department. Dimassimo is a <a href="/wiki/Black_Lives_Matter" title="Black Lives Matter">Black Lives Matter</a> activist. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2016-election/secret-service-rushes-stage-protect-donald-trump-ohio-rally-n537181" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Polish_Constitutional_Court_crisis,_2015" title="Polish Constitutional Court crisis, 2015">Polish Constitutional Court crisis, 2015</a>.
<ul>
<li>Thousands of people take to the streets of <a href="/wiki/Warsaw" title="Warsaw">Warsaw</a> and other cities in <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a> in protest against the government after it refused to publish the <a href="/wiki/Constitutional_Tribunal_(Poland)" title="Constitutional Tribunal (Poland)">Constitutional Court's</a> ruling that the government cannot change how the court works. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-35793914" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Democratic_Movement_Party" title="Brazilian Democratic Movement Party">Brazilian Democratic Movement Party</a> sets a deadline of 30 days to determine the status of its alliance with <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff" title="Dilma Rousseff">Dilma Rousseff’s</a> administration, including the option to leave the coalition. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-12/rousseff-allies-to-vote-in-30-days-on-fate-of-brazil-coalition" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/AlphaGo_versus_Lee_Sedol" title="AlphaGo versus Lee Sedol">AlphaGo versus Lee Sedol</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a> <a href="/wiki/Artificial_intelligence" title="Artificial intelligence">artificial intelligence</a> company <a href="/wiki/DeepMind" title="DeepMind">DeepMind</a>'s <a href="/wiki/AlphaGo" title="AlphaGo">AlphaGo</a> program takes an unbeatable three to zero lead in a five-game <a href="/wiki/Go_(game)" title="Go (game)">Go</a> match against grand master <a href="/wiki/Lee_Sedol" title="Lee Sedol">Lee Sedol</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wired.com/2016/03/third-straight-win-googles-ai-claims-victory-historic-match-go-champ/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Wired</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> March 13, 2016<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2016-03-13</span>)</span> (Sunday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_13&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_13&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_13&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_2016_Ankara_bombing" title="March 2016 Ankara bombing">March 2016 Ankara bombing</a>
<ul>
<li>An explosion occurs in central <a href="/wiki/Ankara" title="Ankara">Ankara</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>, with at least 34 people killed and 125 wounded. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/middle-east/ankara-explosion-several-reportedly-injured-after-big-explosion-in-turkish-capital-a6928926.html" rel="nofollow">(The Independent)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/europe/turkey/12192759/Ankara-explosion-Several-wounded-in-centre-of-Turkish-capital-Kizilay.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turkey%E2%80%93PKK_conflict_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Turkey–PKK conflict (2015–present)">Turkey–PKK conflict (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> declares a <a href="/wiki/Curfew" title="Curfew">curfew</a> in the town of <a href="/wiki/Y%C3%BCksekova" title="Yüksekova">Yüksekova</a> on the border with <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> as <a href="/wiki/Turkish_Armed_Forces" title="Turkish Armed Forces">Turkish forces</a> prepare an offensive against the <a href="/wiki/Kurdistan_Workers%27_Party" title="Kurdistan Workers' Party">PKK</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/dynamic/stories/E/EU_TURKEY_KURDS?SITE=AP&amp;SECTION=HOME&amp;TEMPLATE=DEFAULT" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Grand-Bassam_shootings" title="2016 Grand-Bassam shootings">2016 Grand-Bassam shootings</a>
<ul>
<li>Gunmen attack two hotels in the <a href="/wiki/Ivory_Coast" title="Ivory Coast">Ivory Coast</a> town of <a href="/wiki/Grand-Bassam" title="Grand-Bassam">Grand-Bassam</a>. At least 15 people are reportedly killed. Witnesses claim the attackers shouted "<a href="/wiki/Takbir" title="Takbir">Allahu Akbar</a>" ("God is [the] greatest") during the gunfire. <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda_in_the_Islamic_Maghreb" title="Al-Qaeda in the Islamic Maghreb">Al-Qaeda in the Islamic Maghreb</a> (AQIM) claim responsibility for the attack. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2016/03/13/africa/ivory-coast-attack/index.html?eref=edition" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/africaandindianocean/cotedivoire/12192667/Ivory-Coast-hotel-shooting-Gunmen-open-fire-and-kill-11-in-beach-resort-Grand-Bassam-latest.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nation.co.ke/news/africa/Al-Qaeda-affiliate-claims-Ivory-Coast-attack/-/1066/3115890/-/yht1kxz/-/index.html" rel="nofollow">(Daily Nation)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Maarat_al-Nu%27man" title="Second Battle of Maarat al-Nu'man">Second Battle of Maarat al-Nu'man</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al-Nusra_Front" title="Al-Nusra Front">al-Nusra Front</a>, an <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda" title="Al-Qaeda">al-Qaeda</a> affiliate, assaults the <a href="/wiki/Free_Syrian_Army" title="Free Syrian Army">Free Syrian Army's</a> 13th Division in <a href="/wiki/Maarrat_al-Nu%27man" title="Maarrat al-Nu'man">Maarrat al-Nu'man</a>, killing seven FSA fighters with 40 captured. The <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Observatory_for_Human_Rights" title="Syrian Observatory for Human Rights">Syrian Observatory for Human Rights</a> says Nusra seized <a href="/wiki/Anti-tank_missile" title="Anti-tank missile">anti-tank missiles</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vehicle_armour" title="Vehicle armour">armored vehicles</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Tank" title="Tank">tank</a>, and other arms from the U.S.-backed division. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/al-qaida-seizes-weapons-bases-us-backed-syrian-37612542" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Five people are dead after a building collapses in the <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Meerut" title="Meerut">Meerut</a> caused by heavy rain. <a class="external text" href="http://indiatoday.intoday.in/story/two-storey-building-collapses-in-meerut-5-dead/1/618825.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>India Today</i>)</a></li>
<li>Heavy rain in <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> has led to fifteen deaths in two days including at least eight deaths in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coal_mine" title="Coal mine">coal mine</a> collapse in the <a href="/wiki/Orakzai_Agency" title="Orakzai Agency">Orakzai Tribal Area</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2016/03/13/coal-mine-collapse-in-pakistan-kills-8-another-4-missing.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>
<li>Six people have been killed in <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">Louisiana</a>, <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Oklahoma" title="Oklahoma">Oklahoma</a>, with two <a href="/wiki/Mississippi" title="Mississippi">Mississippi</a> fishermen missing, in this week's flooding in the <a href="/wiki/Deep_South" title="Deep South">America's Deep South</a>. More than 24 inches of rain has fallen in some of the hardest-hit areas with more rain today that is expected to lead to additional flooding later this week. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/us/2016/03/13/6-dead-in-widespread-flooding-across-south-as-area-braces-for-tornadoes.html" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/US/2016/03/13/At-least-6-dead-in-Louisiana-Mississippi-Oklahoma-flooding-more-rain-expected/2171457882698/" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Northwest_windstorm" title="Pacific Northwest windstorm">Pacific Northwest windstorm</a> strikes <a href="/wiki/Western_Washington" title="Western Washington">Western Washington</a>, killing at least one person, leaving 300,000 residents without power, and closing several bridges. <a class="external text" href="http://www.king5.com/story/weather/2016/03/12/sunday-windstorm-could-pack-55-70-mph-winds/81694150/" rel="nofollow">(KING-TV)</a></li>
<li>A six-seat <a href="/wiki/Cessna_206" title="Cessna 206">Cessna 206</a> crashes into a market in the <a href="/wiki/Beni_Department" title="Beni Department">Beni Department</a> of northeastern <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a>, killing all four aboard the plane and injuring three others. (Another report states seven were killed with 15 injured). The plane was flying from <a href="/wiki/Santa_Ana_del_Yacuma" title="Santa Ana del Yacuma">Santa Ana del Yacuma</a> to departmental capital <a href="/wiki/Trinidad,_Bolivia" title="Trinidad, Bolivia">Trinidad</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/plane-hits-market-bolivia-aboard-dead-vendors-hurt-37622255" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.hindustantimes.com/world/bolivia-7-killed-as-small-plane-crashes-into-rural-market/story-CP5t5pwlmhRd8iBVwZztPI.html" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via <i>Hindustan Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a> bans the recruitment of foreign workers after protests over plans to recruit 1.5 million people from <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/news/international/world-news/malaysia-bans-recruitment-of-foreign-workers/articleshow/51374006.cms" rel="nofollow">(Economic Times)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/China%E2%80%93Pakistan_relations" title="China–Pakistan relations">China–Pakistan relations</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>'s <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Liberation_Army" title="People's Liberation Army">People's Liberation Army</a> (PLA) will be deployed in <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> to protect the <a href="/wiki/China%E2%80%93Pakistan_Economic_Corridor" title="China–Pakistan Economic Corridor">China–Pakistan Economic Corridor</a> that connects the Chinese-operated <a href="/wiki/Gwadar_Port" title="Gwadar Port">Gwadar Port</a> in <a href="/wiki/Balochistan,_Pakistan" title="Balochistan, Pakistan">Balochistan, Pakistan</a> to China's <a href="/wiki/Xinjiang" title="Xinjiang">Xinjiang</a> region. Neighboring <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> has voiced concern about the planned move. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ndtv.com/india-news/chinese-troops-will-be-positioned-in-pakistan-security-agencies-to-government-1286550" rel="nofollow">(NDTV)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> officials say <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> has apparently lost contact with one of its <a href="/wiki/Submarine" title="Submarine">submarines</a>. The U.S. was watching the sub off North Korea's <a href="/wiki/Geography_of_North_Korea#Boundaries.2C_coastline.2C_and_islands" title="Geography of North Korea">eastern coast</a> when it vanished earlier this week. Officials are unsure whether the missing vessel is <a href="/wiki/List_of_ship_directions" title="List of ship directions">adrift</a> or has <a href="/wiki/Shipwrecking" title="Shipwrecking">sunk</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://stv.tv/news/international/1346310-north-korea-loses-submarine-as-south-conducts-war-games-with-the-us/" rel="nofollow">(STV)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/13/north-korean-submarine-missing-and-presumed-sunk-say-reports" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel%E2%80%93Palestine_relations" title="Israel–Palestine relations">Israel–Palestine relations</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Foreign_Affairs_Minister_of_the_Palestinian_National_Authority" title="Foreign Affairs Minister of the Palestinian National Authority">Palestinian Ministry of Foreign Affairs</a> says <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> prevented <a href="/wiki/Cabinet_of_Indonesia#Current_cabinet" title="Cabinet of Indonesia">Indonesian Foreign Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Retno_Marsudi" title="Retno Marsudi">Retno Marsudi</a> from entering the <a href="/wiki/West_Bank" title="West Bank">West Bank</a> to meet with <a href="/wiki/Palestinian_National_Authority" title="Palestinian National Authority">Palestinian officials</a>. The Israeli spokesman would not comment. Israel and <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a> do not have formal diplomatic relations. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/national/palestinians-israel-denies-indonesian-fm-entry-to-west-bank/2016/03/13/ac98a92c-e950-11e5-a9ce-681055c7a05f_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.business-standard.com/article/pti-stories/israel-stops-indonesian-minister-west-bank-visit-palestinians-116031300743_1.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>Business Standard</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Israeli–Palestinian conflict (2015–present)">Israeli–Palestinian conflict</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli_Defence_Forces" title="Israeli Defence Forces">Israeli Defence Forces</a> arrest 15 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_people" title="Palestinian people">Palestinian</a> suspects overnight. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Breaking-News/IDF-arrests-15-Palestinian-suspects-overnight-in-West-Bank-447722?utm_source=dlvr.it&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Belarus" title="Law enforcement in Belarus">Authorities</a> in <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a> detain prominent businessman <a href="/wiki/Yury_Chyzh" title="Yury Chyzh">Yury Chyzh</a>, once a close adviser to <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Lukashenko" title="Alexander Lukashenko">Alexander Lukashenko</a> and included in the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">EU's</a> sanctions list, on suspicion of large-scale <a href="/wiki/Tax_evasion" title="Tax evasion">tax evasion</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/belarus-detains-businessman/27607733.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Elections_in_Germany" title="Elections in Germany">Elections in Germany</a>
<ul>
<li>Regional elections take place in the <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">German</a> states of <a href="/wiki/Baden-W%C3%BCrttemberg_state_election,_2016" title="Baden-Württemberg state election, 2016">Baden-Württemberg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rhineland-Palatinate_state_election,_2016" title="Rhineland-Palatinate state election, 2016">Rhineland-Palatinate</a> and <a href="/wiki/Saxony-Anhalt_state_election,_2016" title="Saxony-Anhalt state election, 2016">Saxony-Anhalt</a> with the governing <a href="/wiki/Christian_Democratic_Union_of_Germany" title="Christian Democratic Union of Germany">Christian Democratic Union</a> performing poorly, the centre-left <a href="/wiki/Social_Democratic_Party_of_Germany" title="Social Democratic Party of Germany">Social Democratic Party of Germany</a> winning in Rhineland-Palatinate, and the anti-immigrant <a href="/wiki/Alternative_for_Germany" title="Alternative for Germany">Alternative for Germany</a> performing well in all three states. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-35796831" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.ibtimes.com/german-state-elections-results-2016-angela-merkels-christian-democrats-brace-refugee-2335502" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>International Business Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Hundreds of thousands in <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil's</a> major cities, some estimates say more than 3 million people, protest the weak economy and <a href="/wiki/Political_corruption" title="Political corruption">political corruption</a>, and call for <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff" title="Dilma Rousseff">President Dilma Rousseff's</a> <a href="/wiki/Impeachment" title="Impeachment">impeachment</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/brazil-rousseff-protests-idUSL2N16L054" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-13/brazil-protesters-assemble-as-rousseff-s-future-hangs-in-balance" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-14/millions-join-brazil-impeachment-chorus-in-threat-to-rousseff" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg Business)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Six_Nations_Championship" title="2016 Six Nations Championship">2016 Six Nations Championship</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Scotland_national_rugby_union_team" title="Scotland national rugby union team">Scotland's</a> win over <a href="/wiki/France_national_rugby_union_team" title="France national rugby union team">France</a> gives <a href="/wiki/England_national_rugby_union_team" title="England national rugby union team">England</a> the title. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/sport/2016/mar/13/england-win-six-nations-scotland-france" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Ligue_1" title="2015–16 Ligue 1">2015–16 Ligue 1</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> win the title with eight games to spare, after a 9–0 win at <a href="/wiki/Troyes_AC" title="Troyes AC">Troyes</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/sport/football/35749229" rel="nofollow">(BBC Sport)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_NCAA_Division_I_men%27s_basketball_season" title="2015–16 NCAA Division I men's basketball season">2015–16 NCAA Division I men's basketball season</a>
<ul>
<li>The field of 68 teams for the <a href="/wiki/2016_NCAA_Men%27s_Division_I_Basketball_Tournament" title="2016 NCAA Men's Division I Basketball Tournament">NCAA Tournament</a> is announced. <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Kansas_Jayhawks_men%27s_basketball_team" title="2015–16 Kansas Jayhawks men's basketball team">Kansas</a> is the top overall seed, with <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_North_Carolina_Tar_Heels_men%27s_basketball_team" title="2015–16 North Carolina Tar Heels men's basketball team">North Carolina</a>, <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Oregon_Ducks_men%27s_basketball_team" title="2015–16 Oregon Ducks men's basketball team">Oregon</a>, and <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Virginia_Cavaliers_men%27s_basketball_team" title="2015–16 Virginia Cavaliers men's basketball team">Virginia</a> rounding out the #1 seeds. In a minor controversy, the entire bracket is leaked during the selection show, several minutes before the South and West Regions are officially announced. <a class="external text" href="http://espn.go.com/mens-college-basketball/story/_/id/14658737/2016-ncaa-tournament-schedule-key-dates" rel="nofollow">(ESPN, overall field)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://espn.go.com/mens-college-basketball/story/_/id/14966467/ncaa-tournament-bracket-apparently-leaked" rel="nofollow">(ESPN, bracket leak)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_2016_Ankara_bombing" title="March 2016 Ankara bombing">March 2016 Ankara bombing</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey’s</a> Interior Minister <a href="/wiki/Efkan_Ala" title="Efkan Ala">Efkan Ala</a> says the results of the investigation into yesterday's bombing in <a href="/wiki/Ankara" title="Ankara">Ankara</a> will be made public later today. <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Health_(Turkey)" title="Ministry of Health (Turkey)">Health Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Mehmet_M%C3%BCezzino%C4%9Flu" title="Mehmet Müezzinoğlu">Mehmet Müezzinoğlu</a> says 125 people were transported to a hospital, with 19 in critical condition. Two <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kurdish_people" title="Kurdish people">Kurdish</a> militants have been blamed for the bombing. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-35799998" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/travel/travel-updates/incidents/27-dead-as-explosion-rocks-turkey/news-story/9bc111dee645f531a86a05b87335ef66" rel="nofollow">(News.com.au)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2016/03/14/kurdish-militants-blamed-for-turkey-bombing-that-killed-at-least-37.html" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Israeli–Palestinian conflict (2015–present)">Israeli–Palestinian conflict (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>Three <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_people" title="Palestinian people">Palestinians</a> are shot and killed by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli_Defence_Forces" title="Israeli Defence Forces">Israeli Defence Forces</a> after attempting to run over <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli_people" title="Israeli people">Israeli</a> soldiers. Multiple guns were found in their car. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/world/news/article.cfm?c_id=2&amp;objectid=11605544" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The New Zealand Herald</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mexican_Drug_War" title="Mexican Drug War">Mexican Drug War</a>
<ul>
<li>At least nine suspected cartel members are killed in gunfights with government forces during an anti-cartel operation in the city of <a href="/wiki/Reynosa" title="Reynosa">Reynosa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.appeal-democrat.com/news/regional_news/latin-america/suspected-cartel-members-killed-in-mexico-border-city/article_0d74dfba-b4ef-52e3-9859-823214654bd1.html" rel="nofollow">(Appeal Democrat)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabian-led_intervention_in_Yemen" title="Saudi Arabian-led intervention in Yemen">Saudi Arabian-led intervention in Yemen</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates_Air_Force" title="United Arab Emirates Air Force">United Arab Emirates Air Force</a> fighter jet crashes in a mountainous area near the southern <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemeni</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Aden" title="Aden">Aden</a>, killing both pilots. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-35800511" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russian_military_intervention_in_the_Syrian_Civil_War" title="Russian military intervention in the Syrian Civil War">Russian military intervention</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_Russia" title="President of Russia">Russian President</a> <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a> orders <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Defence_(Russia)" title="Ministry of Defence (Russia)">Defence Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Sergey_Shoygu" title="Sergey Shoygu">Sergey Shoygu</a> to start the withdrawal of <a href="/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces" title="Russian Armed Forces">Russian Armed Forces</a> from <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>, saying during a meeting with Shoygu, "I consider the objectives that have been set for the Defense Ministry to be generally accomplished. That is why I order to start withdrawal of the main part of our military group from the territory of the Syrian Arab Republic starting from tomorrow.” <a class="external text" href="https://www.rt.com/news/335554-putin-orders-syria-withdrawal/" rel="nofollow">(RT)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-35807689" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Flood warnings are put in place and roads are closed after a heavy rain continues to fall in the <a href="/wiki/North_Queensland" title="North Queensland">northern</a> parts of the <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australian</a> state of <a href="/wiki/Queensland" title="Queensland">Queensland</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.9news.com.au/national/2016/03/13/15/23/monsoonal-low-could-develop-over-qld" rel="nofollow">(AAP via NineMSN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Siam_Commercial_Bank" title="Siam Commercial Bank">Siam Commercial Bank</a> reports eight people were killed and seven others injured in the basement of its <a href="/wiki/Bangkok" title="Bangkok">Bangkok</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>, headquarters during an upgrade of the building's <a href="/wiki/Fire_safety" title="Fire safety">fire safety</a> system Sunday evening. It appears that workers mistakenly activated a system that released <a href="/wiki/Fire_extinguisher" title="Fire extinguisher">pyrogen</a>, a chemical that deprives a fire of oxygen. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/718a087904774dd2af8ef33b889a1703/8-killed-chemical-accident-thai-banks-headquarters" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-35800392" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/Amtrak" title="Amtrak">Amtrak</a> passenger train derails west of <a href="/wiki/Dodge_City,_Kansas" title="Dodge City, Kansas">Dodge City</a> in the American state of <a href="/wiki/Kansas" title="Kansas">Kansas</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/news/amtrak-derailment-in-kansas-5-cars-on-their-side/" rel="nofollow">(CBS News)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>International relations</dt>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="North Korea and weapons of mass destruction">North Korea and weapons of mass destruction</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a>'s <a href="/wiki/List_of_leaders_of_North_Korea" title="List of leaders of North Korea">supreme leader</a> <a href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-un" title="Kim Jong-un">Kim Jong-un</a> says his country will soon conduct a nuclear warhead test and test launch ballistic missiles capable of carrying nuclear warheads, according to North Korea's <a href="/wiki/Korean_Central_News_Agency" title="Korean Central News Agency">state media</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-northkorea-nuclear-idUSKCN0WG2IQ" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Freedom_of_the_press#Status_of_press_freedom_worldwide" title="Freedom of the press">Status of press freedom worldwide</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Foreign_Affairs_(Australia)" title="Minister for Foreign Affairs (Australia)">Australian Foreign Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Julie_Bishop" title="Julie Bishop">Julie Bishop</a> says the government is very concerned about Saturday's arrest and detention of two <a href="/wiki/Australian_Broadcasting_Corporation" title="Australian Broadcasting Corporation">Australian Broadcasting Corporation</a> <a href="/wiki/Journalist" title="Journalist">journalists</a> who attempted to interview <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Malaysia" title="Prime Minister of Malaysia">Malaysian Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Najib_Razak" title="Najib Razak">Najib Razak</a>. The pair, who are in Malaysia to investigate allegations of corruption and bribery involving the prime minister, were detained by <a href="/wiki/Royal_Malaysia_Police" title="Royal Malaysia Police">Malaysian police</a> for six hours, and told not to leave the country. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia_pacific/australia-raises-case-of-detained-newsmen-with-malaysia/2016/03/13/33332e50-e97c-11e5-a9ce-681055c7a05f_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/malaysia-politics-australia-idINL3N16M087" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/national/abc-four-corners-crew-grateful-for-support-after-being-detained-in-malaysia-20160314-gni83g.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

</dl>
<ul>
<li>The joint <a href="/wiki/European_Space_Agency" title="European Space Agency">European Space Agency</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russian_Federal_Space_Agency" title="Russian Federal Space Agency">Russian Federal Space Agency</a> <a href="/wiki/ExoMars_Trace_Gas_Orbiter" title="ExoMars Trace Gas Orbiter">ExoMars Trace Gas Orbiter</a> blasts off from the <a href="/wiki/Baikonur_Cosmodrome" title="Baikonur Cosmodrome">Baikonur Cosmodrome</a> in <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan" title="Kazakhstan">Kazakhstan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/science-environment-35800975" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>

<li>The <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">National Football League</a>'s top health and safety official acknowledges a link between <a href="/wiki/American_football" title="American football">American football</a> and <a href="/wiki/Chronic_traumatic_encephalopathy" title="Chronic traumatic encephalopathy">chronic traumatic encephalopathy</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://espn.go.com/espn/otl/story/_/id/14972296/top-nfl-official-acknowledges-link-football-related-head-trauma-cte-first" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_NCAA_Division_I_women%27s_basketball_season" title="2015–16 NCAA Division I women's basketball season">2015–16 NCAA Division I women's basketball season</a>
<ul>
<li>The field of 64 teams for the <a href="/wiki/2016_NCAA_Women%27s_Division_I_Basketball_Tournament" title="2016 NCAA Women's Division I Basketball Tournament">NCAA Tournament</a> is announced. Unbeaten <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Connecticut_Huskies_women%27s_basketball_team" title="2015–16 Connecticut Huskies women's basketball team">Connecticut</a> is the top overall seed, with <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Baylor_Lady_Bears_basketball_team" title="2015–16 Baylor Lady Bears basketball team">Baylor</a>, <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Notre_Dame_Fighting_Irish_women%27s_basketball_team" title="2015–16 Notre Dame Fighting Irish women's basketball team">Notre Dame</a>, and <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_South_Carolina_Gamecocks_women%27s_basketball_team" title="2015–16 South Carolina Gamecocks women's basketball team">South Carolina</a> rounding out the #1 seeds.<a class="external text" href="http://espn.go.com/womens-college-basketball/story/_/id/14972898/2016-women-ncaa-tournament-connecticut-huskies-overall-no-1-seed" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
