<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/American-led_intervention_in_Syria" title="American-led intervention in Syria">American-led intervention in Syria</a>
<ul>
<li>A senior <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqi</a> intelligence official, who is also a Syrian activist leader, says <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a> commander <a href="/wiki/Abu_Omar_al-Shishani" title="Abu Omar al-Shishani">Omar al-Shishani</a> (Omar the Chechen, real name Tarkhan Tayumurazovich Batirashvili) died of wounds suffered in a March 4 <a href="/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces" title="United States Armed Forces">U.S.</a> <a href="/wiki/Airstrike" title="Airstrike">airstrike</a> near the <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syrian</a> town of <a href="/wiki/Al-Shaddadah" title="Al-Shaddadah">Al-Shaddadah</a>. The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_State" title="United States Department of State">U.S. State Department</a> offered up to $5 million for information on his whereabouts. Amaq news agency, which supports ISIL, says Shishani is neither dead nor hurt. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/03/15/world/middleeast/omar-chechen-isis-killed-us-airstrike-syria.html?ribbon-ad-idx=3&amp;rref=world&amp;module=ArrowsNav&amp;contentCollection=Middle%20East&amp;action=keypress&amp;region=FixedRight&amp;pgtype=article" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.chicagotribune.com/news/nationworld/ct-islamic-state-leader-dead-20160315-story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Chicago Tribune</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.swissinfo.ch/eng/reuters/islamic-state-s-shishani-unhurt---amaq-news-agency/42023042" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Swiss Broadcasting Corporation)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2016_Brussels_police_raid" title="2016 Brussels police raid">2016 Brussels police raid</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgian</a> security forces hunt gunmen linked to the <a href="/wiki/November_2015_Paris_attacks" title="November 2015 Paris attacks">November 2015 Paris attacks</a> following a raid on a house in <a href="/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">Brussels</a> which left four officers wounded and one suspect dead after an exchange of gunfire. Roads have been blocked off in the Belgian capital's southern suburb of <a href="/wiki/Forest,_Belgium" title="Forest, Belgium">Forest</a> as one or more gunmen remain at large. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/europe/brussels-anti-terror-raid-shooting-a6932326.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.irishtimes.com/news/world/europe/brussels-on-high-alert-after-anti-terrorism-raid-leaves-one-dead-1.2573973" rel="nofollow">(Irish Times)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabian-led_intervention_in_Yemen" title="Saudi Arabian-led intervention in Yemen">Saudi Arabian-led intervention in Yemen</a>
<ul>
<li>Airstrikes reportedly kill at least 41 people and wound 75 others in <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>'s northern <a href="/wiki/Hajjah_Governorate" title="Hajjah Governorate">Hajjah Governorate</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/uk-yemen-security-idUKKCN0WH1WC" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pope_Francis" title="Pope Francis">Pope Francis</a> announces that <a href="/wiki/Mother_Teresa" title="Mother Teresa">Mother Teresa</a> will be <a href="/wiki/Canonization" title="Canonization">canonized</a> on September 4. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/news/2016/mar/15/vatican-due-to-approve-mother-teresas-sainthood" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brookfield_Asset_Management" title="Brookfield Asset Management">Brookfield Asset Management</a> Inc and <a href="/wiki/Qube_Holdings" title="Qube Holdings">Qube Holdings</a> join forces to make a <a href="/wiki/Australian_dollar" title="Australian dollar">A$</a> 9.1 billion bid for Australian freight logistics company <a href="/wiki/Asciano_Limited" title="Asciano Limited">Asciano Limited</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-15/brookfield-qube-groups-join-forces-in-a-9-1-billion-asciano-bid" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Linn_Energy" title="Linn Energy">Linn Energy</a>, an oil-and-gas producer with about $10 billion in debt, says a bankruptcy filing may be unavoidable. The company was founded in 2003 and had its <a href="/wiki/Initial_public_offering" title="Initial public offering">initial public offering</a> in 2006. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/lnn-going-concern-idUSL2N16N17N" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2016_Ecuadorian_Air_Force_Arava_crash" title="2016 Ecuadorian Air Force Arava crash">2016 Ecuadorian Air Force Arava crash</a>
<ul>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/Ecuadorian_Air_Force" title="Ecuadorian Air Force">Ecuadorian Air Force</a> <a href="/wiki/IAI_Arava" title="IAI Arava">IAI Arava 201</a> crashes near <a href="/wiki/Shell_Mera" title="Shell Mera">Shell Mera</a> in a mountainous part of eastern <a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">Ecuador</a> during military exercises, killing all of the 22 soldiers on board. <a class="external text" href="http://bnonews.com/news/index.php/news/id3860" rel="nofollow">(BNO News)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://aviation-safety.net/database/record.php?id=20160315-0" rel="nofollow">(Aviation Safety Network)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The entire Washington D.C. <a href="/wiki/Washington_Metro" title="Washington Metro">Metro system</a> will shut down for 29 hours beginning at midnight Wednesday for an emergency investigation after an electric cable caught fire on Monday. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/local/2016/03/15/8e0b2be4-eae8-11e5-b0fd-073d5930a7b7_story.html?hpid=hp_rhp-top-table-high_metro-4pm%3Ahomepage%2Fstory" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcwashington.com/news/local/metro-shutdown--372144902.html" rel="nofollow">(NBC4 Washington)</a></li>
<li>A fire severely damages the 16th century <a href="/wiki/Wythenshawe_Hall" title="Wythenshawe Hall">Wythenshawe Hall</a>, near <a href="/wiki/Manchester" title="Manchester">Manchester</a>, <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-manchester-35809417" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A deadly fire breaks out at a rehabilitation center for addicts in <a href="/wiki/Sterlitamak" title="Sterlitamak">Sterlitamak</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bashkortostan" title="Bashkortostan">Bashkortostan</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Republics_of_Russia" title="Republics of Russia">Republic</a> of <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>, killing 12 people. An investigation was immediately launched. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/deadly-fire-bashkortostan/27612620.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Health and medicine</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Centers_for_Disease_Control_and_Prevention" title="Centers for Disease Control and Prevention">U.S. Centers for Disease Control and Prevention</a> issues final recommendations urging doctors to try something besides an <a href="/wiki/Opioid" title="Opioid">opioid</a> when first treating pain, and if an opioid drug, such as <a href="/wiki/Hydrocodone" title="Hydrocodone">hydrocodone</a> or <a href="/wiki/Oxycodone" title="Oxycodone">oxycodone</a>, is the best choice, start with the <a href="/wiki/Effective_dose_(pharmacology)" title="Effective dose (pharmacology)">lowest possible dose</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/powerpost/wp/2016/03/15/cdc-warns-doctors-about-the-dangers-of-prescribing-opioid-painkillers/?wpmm=1&amp;wpisrc=nl_evening" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/health/health-news/new-cdc-painkiller-guidelines-go-low-use-less-n538986" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Burundian_unrest_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Burundian unrest (2015–present)">Burundian unrest (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> suspends direct financial aid to <a href="/wiki/Burundi" title="Burundi">Burundi</a> after concluding that the Burundian authorities had not done enough to find a political solution to the ongoing conflict occurring in the country. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/global-development/2016/mar/15/eu-suspends-aid-to-burundi-government" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Argentina%E2%80%93China_relations" title="Argentina–China relations">Argentina–China relations</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Argentine_Naval_Prefecture" title="Argentine Naval Prefecture">coastguard</a> says it has sunk a <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">Chinese</a> fishing trawler that was operating illegally within its territorial waters. The coastguard says it rescued four of the trawler's crew while others who abandoned ship were picked up by another Chinese vessel shadowing the pursuit. <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/argentina-sinks-chinese-trawler-fishing-illegally-coastguard-210035916.html" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Yahoo! News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/House_of_Representatives_(Netherlands)" title="House of Representatives (Netherlands)">parliament</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a> passes a resolution calling on the government to stop selling arms to <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a>, citing ongoing "violations of humanitarian law" in <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.middleeasteye.net/news/dutch-parliament-calls-arms-embargo-saudi-arabia-over-yemen-war-1861032989" rel="nofollow">(Middle East Eye)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Shooting_of_Michael_Brown" title="Shooting of Michael Brown">Shooting of Michael Brown</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ferguson_unrest" title="Ferguson unrest">Ferguson unrest</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Ferguson,_Missouri" title="Ferguson, Missouri">Ferguson, Missouri</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ferguson,_Missouri#Government" title="Ferguson, Missouri">city council</a>, after last month voting to change the terms of the agreement, reverses course and unanimously (6-0) agrees to accept a <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Justice" title="United States Department of Justice">U.S. Justice Department</a> overhaul of its troubled <a href="/wiki/Ferguson_Police_Department_(Missouri)" title="Ferguson Police Department (Missouri)">police force</a> and <a href="/wiki/State_court_(United_States)#Types_of_state_courts" title="State court (United States)">municipal courts</a>. This avoided a likely expensive legal battle with the federal government which had filed suit against the city following last month's vote. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/15/us/ferguson-justice-department-agreement-vote/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2016" title="United States presidential election, 2016">United States presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voters in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> states of <a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">Florida</a>, <a href="/wiki/Illinois" title="Illinois">Illinois</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ohio" title="Ohio">Ohio</a>, <a href="/wiki/Missouri" title="Missouri">Missouri</a>, <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">North Carolina</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_(U.S._insular_area)" title="Commonwealth (U.S. insular area)">commonwealth</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Northern_Mariana_Islands" title="Northern Mariana Islands">Northern Mariana Islands</a> head to the polls for <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_presidential_primaries,_2016" title="Republican Party presidential primaries, 2016">Republican</a> and <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_presidential_primaries,_2016" title="Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2016">Democratic Party</a> primaries that the media has dubbed "Super Tuesday 2". <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/white-house-hopefuls-hustle-votes-race-turns-toxic-031836358.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Yahoo! News)</a></li>
<li>Donald Trump wins primaries in Illinois, North Carolina, Missouri and Florida while <a href="/wiki/John_Kasich" title="John Kasich">John Kasich</a> wins in Ohio. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nydailynews.com/news/politics/trump-builds-gop-delegate-lead-big-florida-win-article-1.2565714" rel="nofollow">(NY Daily News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.decisiondeskhq.com/results/2016/primary/gop/president/florida/" rel="nofollow">(Decision Desk HQ)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/election/primaries/states/oh/Rep" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/news/2016/03/15/illinois-voters-go-polls-tight-races/81802380/" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2016-election/2016-candidates-aim-change-race-huge-tuesday-primaries-loom-n537966?cid=eml_nbn_20160315" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Northern_Mariana_Islands" title="Northern Mariana Islands">Northern Mariana Islands</a> caucus. <a class="external text" href="http://www.politico.com/blogs/2016-gop-primary-live-updates-and-results/2016/03/trump-wins-9-delegates-in-northern-marina-islands-220763" rel="nofollow">(Politico)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> wins the Democratic primaries in Florida, Illinois, Ohio, Missouri and North Carolina. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/politics/elections/2016/live-blog" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a>, <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/post-politics/wp/2016/03/15/trump-clinton-projected-to-win-florida-primaries/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/video/watch-live-clinton-speaks-after-primary-results-322524227825" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/politics/2016-election/2016-candidates-aim-change-race-huge-tuesday-primaries-loom-n537966?cid=eml_nbn_20160315" rel="nofollow">(NBC News Live Blog)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Marco_Rubio" title="Marco Rubio">Marco Rubio</a> suspends <a href="/wiki/Marco_Rubio_presidential_campaign,_2016" title="Marco Rubio presidential campaign, 2016">his presidential campaign</a> following a disappointing defeat in his home state of <a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">Florida</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/03/16/us/politics/marco-rubio.html?_r=0" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">North Carolina's</a> controversial <a href="/wiki/Voter_ID_laws_in_the_United_States" title="Voter ID laws in the United States">voter ID law</a> is in effect for the first time. Voters without these new <a href="/wiki/Identity_document" title="Identity document">ID credentials</a>, including voters with a “reasonable impediment” to obtaining an ID, can cast a provisional ballot. Citizens (2,567) faced this problem during early voting, including <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">U.S. Senator</a> <a href="/wiki/Richard_Burr" title="Richard Burr">Richard Burr</a> who, because his driver's license was stolen, was without ID. In addition, votes for <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">congressional candidates</a> for <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">House seats</a> don't count because the state's congressional district map was redrawn after the ballots were printed. The actual congressional primary is scheduled for June 7. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wral.com/voters-without-photo-id-run-into-new-election-rules/15519142/" rel="nofollow">(WRAL)</a><a class="external text" href="http://billmoyers.com/story/north-carolinas-voter-id-law-could-block-218000-registered-voters-from-the-polls/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Nation</i> via <i>Moyers &amp; Company</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.npr.org/2016/03/10/469548881/north-carolinas-congressional-primaries-are-a-mess-because-of-these-maps?utm_medium=RSS&amp;utm_campaign=storiesfromnpr" rel="nofollow">(NPR)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.charlotteobserver.com/news/politics-government/article65555907.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Charlotte Observer</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/03/11/us/north-carolina-voting-rights-redistictricting-battles.html?em_pos=large&amp;emc=edit_nn_20160315&amp;nl=morning-briefing&amp;nlid=11553763&amp;module=ArrowsNav&amp;contentCollection=U.S.&amp;action=keypress&amp;region=FixedLeft&amp;pgtype=article" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nigerien_general_election,_2016" title="Nigerien general election, 2016">Nigerien general election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>The government will release opposition candidate <a href="/wiki/Hama_Amadou" title="Hama Amadou">Hama Amadou</a> from prison due to health issues. Amadou is facing off against incumbent <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_of_Niger" title="President of Niger">President of Niger</a> <a href="/wiki/Mahamadou_Issoufou" title="Mahamadou Issoufou">Mahamadou Issoufou</a> in the second round of voting on Sunday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/niger-election-idUSL5N16N00C" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Myanmar" title="Myanmar">Myanmar</a> <a href="/wiki/Assembly_of_the_Union" title="Assembly of the Union">Assembly of the Union</a>, or parliament, <a href="/wiki/Presidential_Electoral_College" title="Presidential Electoral College">selects</a> <a href="/wiki/Htin_Kyaw" title="Htin Kyaw">Htin Kyaw</a> as the new <a href="/wiki/President_of_Myanmar" title="President of Myanmar">President</a>. Kyaw, a confidant of <a href="/wiki/Aung_San_Suu_Kyi" title="Aung San Suu Kyi">Aung San Suu Kyi</a>, will be the first civilian president in decades. Suu Kyi, a <a href="/wiki/Nobel_Peace_Prize" title="Nobel Peace Prize">Nobel Peace Prize</a> recipient, is <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_Myanmar" title="Constitution of Myanmar">constitutionally</a> barred from the office. <a class="external text" href="http://indianexpress.com/article/world/world-news/myanmar-parliament-to-select-countrys-president-on-tuesday/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Indian Express</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2016-03-15/myanmar-elects-htin-kyaw-as-first-civilian-leader-in-decades/7248728" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Presidency_of_Barack_Obama" title="Presidency of Barack Obama">Obama administration</a> announces it is cancelling plans to permit <a href="/wiki/Oil_well#drilling" title="Oil well">drilling for oil and gas</a> off the <a href="/wiki/Southeastern_United_States" title="Southeastern United States">southeastern U.S.</a> <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">Atlantic coast</a>. A new plan involves 10 potential lease sales in the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico" title="Gulf of Mexico">Gulf of Mexico</a> and three off the coast of <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/money/2016/03/15/offshore-oil-president-obama/81800458/" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://islandfreepress.org/2016Archives/03.15.25016-FederalOfficialsReverseCourseOnOffshoreDrilling.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Island Free Press</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Andrew_Wiles" title="Andrew Wiles">Andrew Wiles</a> wins the 2016 <a href="/wiki/Abel_Prize" title="Abel Prize">Abel Prize</a> for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wiles%27_proof_of_Fermat%27s_Last_Theorem" title="Wiles' proof of Fermat's Last Theorem">his solution</a> to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fermat%27s_last_theorem" title="Fermat's last theorem">Fermat's last theorem</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nature.com/news/fermat-s-last-theorem-earns-andrew-wiles-the-abel-prize-1.19552" rel="nofollow">(Nature)</a></li>
<li>Scientists, in the <i><a href="/wiki/Proceedings_of_the_National_Academy_of_Sciences_of_the_United_States_of_America" title="Proceedings of the National Academy of Sciences of the United States of America">Proceedings of the National Academy of Sciences</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Scientific_journal" title="Scientific journal">scientific journal</a>, report that so-called <a href="/wiki/Fairy_circle_(arid_grass_formation)" title="Fairy circle (arid grass formation)">fairy circles</a> are caused by the plants themselves, which have <a href="/wiki/Self-organization" title="Self-organization">self-organized</a>. Michael Cramer and Nichole Barger suggested this in 2013. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/morning-mix/wp/2016/03/15/dragons-aliens-bugs-scientists-may-have-solved-the-mystery-of-the-deserts-fairy-circles/?wpmm=1&amp;wpisrc=nl_mix" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.pnas.org/content/early/2016/03/09/1522130113" rel="nofollow">(PNAS)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.theatlantic.com/science/archive/2016/03/mysterious-fairy-circles-australia-namibia/473625/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Atlantic</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Peshawar_bus_bombing" title="2016 Peshawar bus bombing">2016 Peshawar bus bombing</a>
<ul>
<li>A bomb detonates in a bus carrying government employees in <a href="/wiki/Peshawar" title="Peshawar">Peshawar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>, killing 15 and injuring at least 54. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/news/pakistan-bus-bomb-targets-government-workers-peshawar/" rel="nofollow">(AP via CBS)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Boko_Haram_insurgency" title="Boko Haram insurgency">Boko Haram insurgency</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Maiduguri_suicide_bombings" title="2016 Maiduguri suicide bombings">2016 Maiduguri suicide bombings</a>
<ul>
<li>Two female suicide bombers detonate their explosives at a mosque during morning prayer on the outskirts of <a href="/wiki/Maiduguri" title="Maiduguri">Maiduguri</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a>, killing 22 and injuring 18. <a class="external text" href="http://mobile.nytimes.com/aponline/2016/03/16/world/africa/ap-af-nigeria-boko-haram.html?_r=0&amp;referer=https://news.google.com/" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.newsweek.com/nigeria-suicide-bombers-kill-scores-boko-haram-birthplace-437343" rel="nofollow">(<i>Newsweek</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Washington_Metro" title="Washington Metro">Washington Metro</a>, a commuter rail system which transports nearly 1 million passengers across the <a href="/wiki/Washington_metropolitan_area" title="Washington metropolitan area">Washington, D.C. metropolitan area</a> per day, shuts down to allow for an emergency inspection of 600 electrical cables, following two fires occurring over the past 14 months. Officials say the system is scheduled to resume service by the following morning, though individual Metro lines or stations could remain closed indefinitely if problems are identified. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/local/trafficandcommuting/washington-braces-for-full-day-of-metro-shutdown-to-deal-with-safety-concerns/2016/03/16/42324598-eb3f-11e5-b0fd-073d5930a7b7_story.html?hpid=hp_rhp-top-table-low_metro-620a%3Ahomepage%2Fstory" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtontimes.com/news/2016/mar/15/metrorail-close-all-day-wednesday/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/news/dc-commuters-facing-subway-shutdown-metromageddon/" rel="nofollow">(CBS News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Health and medicine</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zika_virus_outbreak_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Zika virus outbreak (2015–present)">Zika virus outbreak</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuban</a> officials announce they have detected the first case of the <a href="/wiki/Zika_virus" title="Zika virus">Zika virus</a> transmitted inside the country: a 21-year-old <a href="/wiki/Havana" title="Havana">Havana</a> woman who had not traveled abroad. Cuba has reported a handful of travel-associated Zika cases, all believed imported from <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://medicalxpress.com/news/2016-03-cuba-case-zika-transmitted-island.html" rel="nofollow">(Medical Xpress)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://outbreaknewstoday.com/cuba-local-transmission-of-zika-reported-in-havana-67102/" rel="nofollow">(Outbreak News Today)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea%E2%80%93United_States_relations" title="North Korea–United States relations">North Korea–United States relations</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> sentences American <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Otto_Frederick_Warmbier" title="Otto Frederick Warmbier">Otto Warmbier</a>, a 21-year-old from <a href="/wiki/Cincinnati" title="Cincinnati">Cincinnati</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ohio" title="Ohio">Ohio</a>, studying at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Virginia" title="University of Virginia">University of Virginia</a>, to 15 years hard labor for removing a <a href="/wiki/Poster#Political_uses" title="Poster">political poster</a> from a hotel. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/16/north-korea-sentences-us-student-to-15-years-hard-labour" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/morning-mix/wp/2016/03/16/north-korea-sentences-u-va-student-to-15-years-of-hard-labor-in-prison/?wpmm=1&amp;wpisrc=nl_headlines" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> orders new sanctions against <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> in response to 'illicit' nuclear, missile tests. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/d090a54b2358491182c681bb86045d71/obama-orders-new-sanctions-against-north-korea-response" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>, <a href="/wiki/Syrian_peace_process" title="Syrian peace process">Syrian peace process</a>
<ul>
<li>The delegation of the government of <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a> rules out starting any direct talks with the <a href="/wiki/Syrian_opposition" title="Syrian opposition">opposition</a> delegation as <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">U.N.</a> sponsored peace talks enter a third day in <a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">Geneva</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-35820823" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kurds_in_Syria" title="Kurds in Syria">Kurdish</a> officials say they plan to declare a <a href="/wiki/Federalism" title="Federalism">federal region</a> in northern <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a> after being excluded from peace talks in <a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">Geneva</a> aimed at ending the 5-year-old conflict. The move will combine three Kurdish-led autonomous areas into a federal system in what is set to alarm neighboring <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/news/world/2016/03/16/reports-kurds-plan-declare-federal-region-syria/81849838/" rel="nofollow">(USA Today)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Turkey%E2%80%93United_Kingdom_relations" title="Turkey–United Kingdom relations">Turkey–United Kingdom relations</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> deports <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Academia" title="Academia">academic</a> Chris Stephenson, a <a href="/wiki/Computer_science" title="Computer science">computer science</a> lecturer at <a href="/wiki/Istanbul_Bilgi_University" title="Istanbul Bilgi University">Bilgi University</a> in <a href="/wiki/Istanbul" title="Istanbul">Istanbul</a>, who is charged with making terrorism propaganda. The <a href="/wiki/Foreign_and_Commonwealth_Office" title="Foreign and Commonwealth Office">UK Foreign Office</a> said it was providing assistance; there has been no comment from Turkish officials. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/10170d3628a14a43b96130abdab1ce0a/turkey-deports-british-academic-accused-terror-propaganda" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The travel ban for former <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistani</a> President <a href="/wiki/Pervez_Musharraf" title="Pervez Musharraf">Pervez Musharraf</a> is lifted by the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Pakistan" title="Supreme Court of Pakistan">Supreme Court of Pakistan</a>. Musharraf is currently facing treason charges in Pakistan. <a class="external text" href="http://mobile.reuters.com/article/idUSKCN0WI10W" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/PKK_rebellion_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="PKK rebellion (2015–present)">PKK rebellion (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Turkey" title="Law enforcement in Turkey">Authorities</a> in <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> arrest three academics on charges of "terrorist propaganda" after they called for an end to security operations in the country's Kurdish-majority southeast. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/turkey-academics-arrested-terrorist-propaganda/27616332.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Attacks_on_humanitarian_workers" title="Attacks on humanitarian workers">Attacks on humanitarian workers</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces" title="United States Armed Forces">U.S. military</a> disciplines more than a dozen personnel for mistakes that led to the bombing of a <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A9decins_Sans_Fronti%C3%A8res" title="Médecins Sans Frontières">Médecins Sans Frontières</a> (Doctors Without Borders) hospital that killed 42 people in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> last October. No criminal charges are pending. The partially <a href="/wiki/Redaction" title="Redaction">redacted</a> investigation report is expected to be made public shortly. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/d4f37ad3616f46e8b980bc8a10435e29/more-12-punished-mistaken-hospital-attack" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_presidential_debates_and_forums,_2016" title="Republican Party presidential debates and forums, 2016">Republican Party presidential debates and forums, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> announces he will skip the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fox_News_Channel" title="Fox News Channel">Fox News</a> GOP presidential debate between the three remaining candidates on March 21, saying he thinks "we had enough of debates." <a class="external text" href="http://www.newsmax.com/Headline/Donald-Trump-Fox-News-debate/2016/03/16/id/719324/" rel="nofollow">(Newsmax)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ohio" title="Ohio">Ohio</a> Governor <a href="/wiki/John_Kasich" title="John Kasich">John Kasich</a> says he will also skip the debate if Donald Trump follows through on his vow not to attend. <a class="external text" href="http://thehill.com/blogs/ballot-box/presidential-races/273226-kasich-skipping-debate-after-trump-bails" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Hill</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fox_News_Channel" title="Fox News Channel">Fox News</a> cancels the Republican debate scheduled for Monday in <a href="/wiki/Salt_Lake_City" title="Salt Lake City">Salt Lake City</a>, <a href="/wiki/Utah" title="Utah">Utah</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Utah_Republican_Party" title="Utah Republican Party">Utah Republican Party</a> has received more than 50,000 ticket requests. <a href="/wiki/Lieutenant_Governor_of_Utah" title="Lieutenant Governor of Utah">Utah Lieutenant Governor</a> <a href="/wiki/Spencer_Cox_(politician)" title="Spencer Cox (politician)">Spencer Cox</a> is upset Trump, "...is snubbing the state of Utah." According to <i><a href="/wiki/Deseret_News" title="Deseret News">Deseret News</a></i>, Trump is in fourth place in Utah polls. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sltrib.com/news/3669839-155/debate-scrapped-after-donald-trump-says" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Salt Lake Tribune</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.deseretnews.com/article/865650178/Trump-wont-participate-in-SLC-debate-giving-speech-instead.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Deseret News</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2016_Republican_Party_presidential_primaries" title="2016 Republican Party presidential primaries">2016 Republican Party presidential primaries</a>:
<ul>
<li>Senior GOP rules committee member <a href="/wiki/Curly_Haugland" title="Curly Haugland">Curly Haugland</a> says that "We (RCN committee members) choose the nominee, not the voters". <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/the-fix/wp/2016/03/16/rnc-member-political-parties-choose-their-nominee-not-the-general-public/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2016" title="United States presidential election, 2016">United States presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election_in_Missouri,_2016" title="United States presidential election in Missouri, 2016">Missouri Primary</a>, media outlets have held off calling yesterday's races due to the extremely close results. Donald Trump and <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> lead in their party's vote, but by just two-tenths of 1 percent ahead of <a href="/wiki/Ted_Cruz" title="Ted Cruz">Ted Cruz</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bernie_Sanders" title="Bernie Sanders">Bernie Sanders</a>, respectively. <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Missouri" title="Government of Missouri">Missouri law</a> states a recount may be requested if the margin is less than half a percentage point. Either Cruz or Sanders or both can request a recount. These results are unofficial, until they’re certified by the <a href="/wiki/Jason_Kander" title="Jason Kander">Missouri Secretary of State</a>, which reportedly could take up to four weeks. Trump leads by about 1,700 votes and Clinton's edge is about 1,500. The state also needs to count the remaining absentee and provisional ballots; the deadline for overseas ballots is noon Friday. <a class="external text" href="http://thehill.com/blogs/ballot-box/presidential-races/273266-close-results-in-missouri-primary-could-lead-to-recounts" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Hill</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/16/politics/super-tuesday-missouri-delegates/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama_Supreme_Court_candidates" title="Barack Obama Supreme Court candidates">Barack Obama Supreme Court candidates</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> nominates <a href="/wiki/Merrick_Garland" title="Merrick Garland">Merrick Garland</a> to replace <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Scalia" title="Antonin Scalia">Antonin Scalia</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">Supreme Court of the United States</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-us-canada-35823234" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2016/03/16/politics/obama-supreme-court-announcement/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>'s ex-president <a href="/wiki/Luiz_In%C3%A1cio_Lula_da_Silva" title="Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva">Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva</a> takes Cabinet post as chief of staff to Brazil's current president, <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff" title="Dilma Rousseff">Dilma Rousseff</a>, thereby gaining legal shield. Only the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Federal_Court" title="Supreme Federal Court">Brazilian Supreme Court</a> can try presidential Cabinet members for crimes. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/03/17/world/americas/brazil-ex-president-luiz-inacio-lula-da-silva.html" rel="nofollow">(New York Times)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2016/03/16/Brazils-Rousseff-names-former-president-Lula-her-chief-of-staff/7441458144589/?spt=hs&amp;or=tn_int" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a>
<ul>
<li>Protests erupt outside the <a href="/wiki/Pal%C3%A1cio_da_Alvorada" title="Palácio da Alvorada">presidential palace</a> in <a href="/wiki/Bras%C3%ADlia" title="Brasília">Brasília</a>, and on <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="São Paulo">São Paulo's</a> main <a href="/wiki/Paulista_Avenue" title="Paulista Avenue">Avenue Paulista</a>. on news of Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva's appointment as President Rousseff's chief of staff. Federal Judge <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A9rgio_Moro" title="Sérgio Moro">Sérgio Moro</a> says taped conversations between the two show Lula and Rousseff, apparently, trying to influence the investigation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-brazil-rousseff-idUSKCN0WI1T0" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Scientists release a small flock of <a href="/wiki/Columbidae" title="Columbidae">pigeons</a>, dubbed "The Pigeon Air Patrol", carrying tiny backpacks to monitor <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>'s air quality during a period of moderate to high pollution. The backpacks contain sensors used to measure <a href="/wiki/Nitrogen_dioxide" title="Nitrogen dioxide">nitrogen dioxide</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ozone" title="Ozone">ozone</a> levels. <a class="external text" href="http://www.engadget.com/2016/03/16/pigeons-air-pollution-backpacks-london/" rel="nofollow">(Engadget)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/environment/2016/mar/14/pigeon-patrol-takes-flight-to-tackle-londons-air-pollution-crisis" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Professional_Golfers%27_Association_of_America" title="Professional Golfers' Association of America">PGA of America</a> announces it is discontinuing the <a href="/wiki/PGA_Grand_Slam_of_Golf" title="PGA Grand Slam of Golf">PGA Grand Slam of Golf</a>, a special postseason event among the year's winners of the four major championships of regular men's golf. This year, it was set to be held at <a href="/wiki/Trump_National_Golf_Club_(Los_Angeles)" title="Trump National Golf Club (Los Angeles)">Trump National Golf Club</a> in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a>, <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a>. The 2015 event was cancelled after the PGA decided to move the exhibition contest from the same Trump Club, and they couldn't find a replacement course golf course with suitable dates. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/a90f7f11936e4adc85cf76bbc3edc637/pga-america-pulls-plug-grand-slam" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.pga.com/news/pga/pga-america-discontinue-pga-grand-slam-golf" rel="nofollow">(PGA)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://espn.go.com/golf/story/_/id/13571464/pga-cancels-grand-slam-golf-trump-national-los-angeles" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iraqi_Civil_War_(2014%E2%80%93present)" title="Iraqi Civil War (2014–present)">Iraqi Civil War</a>, <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_State" title="United States Secretary of State">United States Secretary of State</a> <a href="/wiki/John_Kerry" title="John Kerry">John Kerry</a> says <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a> has committed genocide against <a href="/wiki/Genocide_of_Christians_by_ISIL" title="Genocide of Christians by ISIL">Christians</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Persecution_of_Yazidis_by_ISIL" title="Persecution of Yazidis by ISIL">Yazidis</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Persecution_of_Shias_by_ISIL" title="Persecution of Shias by ISIL">Shias</a> in areas it controls in <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a> and <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-35831711" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State</a> reports commander Hassan Aboud has died of wounds sustained about two weeks ago in a battle near <a href="/wiki/Aleppo" title="Aleppo">Aleppo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>. He was injured when a vehicle he was in struck a <a href="/wiki/Improvised_explosive_device" title="Improvised explosive device">roadside bomb</a> near <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Khanaser" title="Khanaser">Khanaser</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/03/18/world/middleeast/hassan-aboud-an-isis-commander-dies-from-battlefield-wounds.html?_r=0" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Papua_conflict" title="Papua conflict">Papua conflict</a>
<ul>
<li>Three construction workers are shot dead in <a href="/wiki/Jayapura" title="Jayapura">Jayapura</a>, <a href="/wiki/Papua_(province)" title="Papua (province)">Papua</a>, by a supposed armed group, according to <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesian</a> <a href="/wiki/Indonesian_National_Police" title="Indonesian National Police">police</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.radionz.co.nz/international/pacific-news/299231/west-papua-shooting-claims-at-least-3-road-builders" rel="nofollow">(<i>Radio New Zealand</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Radar scans at <a href="/wiki/KV62" title="KV62">the tomb</a> of <a href="/wiki/Tutankhamun" title="Tutankhamun">Tutankhamun</a>, Pharaoh of <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Egypt" title="Ancient Egypt">Ancient Egypt</a>, reveal two chambers adjoining the tomb, raising prospect of finding the resting place of Queen <a href="/wiki/Nefertiti" title="Nefertiti">Nefertiti</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/17/hidden-rooms-tutankhamun-tomb-new-treasures-queen-nefertiti" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Vatican</a> is replacing <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italian</a> <a href="/wiki/Carlo_Maria_Vigan%C3%B2" title="Carlo Maria Viganò">Archbishop Carlo Maria Viganò</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Papal_diplomacy" title="Papal diplomacy">Apostolic Nuncio</a> <a href="/wiki/Apostolic_Nunciature_to_the_United_States" title="Apostolic Nunciature to the United States">to the U.S.</a>, with <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French-born</a> <a href="/wiki/Christophe_Pierre" title="Christophe Pierre">Archbishop Christophe Pierre</a>, currently the <a href="/wiki/Apostolic_Nuncio_to_Mexico" title="Apostolic Nuncio to Mexico">Apostolic Nuncio to Mexico</a>. Viganò, who is 75, the statutory retirement age, in 2015 arranged the unexpected meeting between <a href="/wiki/Pope_Francis" title="Pope Francis">Pope Francis</a> and controversial Kentucky clerk <a href="/wiki/Kim_Davis_(county_clerk)" title="Kim Davis (county clerk)">Kim Davis</a>, who refused to follow her state's law on <a href="/wiki/Same-sex_marriage" title="Same-sex marriage">same-sex marriage</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://christiannews.net/2016/03/17/vatican-fires-ambassador-who-arranged-roman-catholic-pontiffs-meeting-with-kim-davis/" rel="nofollow">(<i>New York Daily News</i> via ChristianNews.net)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tribune_Publishing_Company" title="Tribune Publishing Company">Tribune Publishing</a>, an American company whose <a href="/wiki/Southern_California" title="Southern California">Southern California</a> media holdings include the <i><a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_Times" title="Los Angeles Times">Los Angeles Times</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/The_San_Diego_Union-Tribune" title="The San Diego Union-Tribune">The San Diego Union-Tribune</a></i>, wins an auction for bankrupt newspapers, <i><a href="/wiki/Orange_County_Register" title="Orange County Register">Orange County Register</a></i>, published in <a href="/wiki/Santa_Ana,_California" title="Santa Ana, California">Santa Ana</a>, and <i><a href="/wiki/The_Press-Enterprise" title="The Press-Enterprise">The Press-Enterprise</a></i>, headquartered in <a href="/wiki/Riverside,_California" title="Riverside, California">Riverside</a>, for $56 million, subject to judicial approval. A <a href="/wiki/United_States_bankruptcy_court" title="United States bankruptcy court">federal bankruptcy court</a> hearing is scheduled for Monday. The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Justice" title="United States Department of Justice">U.S. Justice Department</a> has warned that a Tribune purchase could violate <a href="/wiki/United_States_antitrust_law" title="United States antitrust law">antitrust laws</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usnews.com/news/business/articles/2016-03-17/tribune-publishing-places-top-bid-for-orange-county-register" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>U.S. News &amp; World Report</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/business/la-fi-freedom-tribune-auction-20160317-story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>At least 16 <a href="/wiki/Palestinians" title="Palestinians">Palestinian</a> pilgrims are killed when the bus they were traveling to <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a> on overturns in southern <a href="/wiki/Jordan" title="Jordan">Jordan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.voanews.com/content/death-toll-of-palestinian-pilgrims-in-jordan-bus-crash-rises-to-16/3241837.html" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Government_of_China" title="Government of China">People's Republic of China</a> expresses its opposition to unilateral sanctions against <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> in the wake of the imposition of new sanctions by the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> on the country in response to its recent nuclear and rocket tests. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-northkorea-nuclear-china-idUSKCN0WJ0QC" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kurds" title="Kurds">Kurdish</a> parties in <a href="/wiki/Rojava" title="Rojava">northern Syria</a> declare the establishment of a federal system in areas they control. <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> had warned this risks further destabilizing the already war-ravaged country. The move was criticized by the government of <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-35830375" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/middle_east/syrian-kurds-declare-their-own-region-raising-tensions/2016/03/17/db762950-ec4c-11e5-a9ce-681055c7a05f_story.html?wpmm=1&amp;wpisrc=nl_evening" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Territorial_disputes_in_the_South_China_Sea" title="Territorial disputes in the South China Sea">Territorial disputes in the South China Sea</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/John_M._Richardson_(admiral)" title="John M. Richardson (admiral)">Admiral John Richardson</a> says the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> has seen <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">Chinese activity</a> around <a href="/wiki/Scarborough_Shoal_standoff" title="Scarborough Shoal standoff">Scarborough Shoal</a>, which China seized from the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> nearly four years ago, in the northern part of the <a href="/wiki/Spratly_Islands" title="Spratly Islands">Spratly archipelago</a> of the <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">South China Sea</a>. An international court ruling on a case brought by the Philippines against China over its South China Sea claims is expected within a month. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-southchinasea-china-scarborough-exclu-idUSKCN0WK01B" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and Crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Judges at the <a href="/wiki/International_Criminal_Tribunal_for_the_former_Yugoslavia" title="International Criminal Tribunal for the former Yugoslavia">International Criminal Tribunal for the former Yugoslavia</a> announce that they will soon deliver their verdict against radical Serb leader <a href="/wiki/Vojislav_%C5%A0e%C5%A1elj" title="Vojislav Šešelj">Vojislav Šešelj</a>, suspected of <a href="/wiki/Crimes_against_humanity" title="Crimes against humanity">crimes against humanity</a> committed during the <a href="/wiki/Breakup_of_Yugoslavia" title="Breakup of Yugoslavia">Breakup of Yugoslavia</a>, despite him being sent back to <a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a> for medical reasons. Šešelj has vowed not to return to court. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/war-crimes-court-hague-excuses-serbian-seselj-attending-verdict/27618176.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_protests_in_Brazil" title="2015–16 protests in Brazil">2015–16 protests in Brazil</a>
<ul>
<li>Clashes erupt outside the <a href="/wiki/Pal%C3%A1cio_da_Alvorada" title="Palácio da Alvorada">presidential palace</a> in <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>'s capital <a href="/wiki/Bras%C3%ADlia" title="Brasília">Brasília</a> between anti-<a href="/wiki/Workers%27_Party_(Brazil)" title="Workers' Party (Brazil)">Workers' Party</a> protesters and supporters of ex-president <a href="/wiki/Luiz_In%C3%A1cio_Lula_da_Silva" title="Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva">Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva</a>, where he was due to be sworn in as <a href="/wiki/President_of_Brazil" title="President of Brazil">President of Brazil</a> <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff" title="Dilma Rousseff">Dilma Rousseff</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Chief_of_Staff_of_Brazil" title="Chief of Staff of Brazil">chief of staff</a>. Hundreds of anti-government protesters calling for Rousseff's impeachment and Lula's arrest also blocked the central <a href="/wiki/Paulista_Avenue" title="Paulista Avenue">Paulista Avenue</a> in <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="São Paulo">São Paulo</a>, Brazil's largest city and economic hub. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-brazil-politics-idUSKCN0WJ1WN" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> federal judge blocks the appointment of Lula as <a href="/wiki/Chief_of_Staff_of_Brazil" title="Chief of Staff of Brazil">chief of staff</a>, arguing that the appointment would derail a federal judicial investigation against him. The government said it would appeal against the decision. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-latin-america-35835795" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_presidential_candidates,_2016" title="Republican Party presidential candidates, 2016">Republican Party presidential candidates, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Anonymous_(group)" title="Anonymous (group)">hacker group Anonymous</a> follows through on its threat and releases candidate <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump's</a> personal information (unverified) including his Social Security number, his phone numbers, his agent and his legal representatives. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aol.com/article/2016/03/17/trumps-social-security-phone-numbers-released-by-anonymous-h/21329514/" rel="nofollow">(AOL)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/news/politics/onpolitics/2016/03/17/total-war-anonymous-posts-trumps-social-security-number-phone-number/81933246/" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.mirror.co.uk/tech/anonymous-declares-total-war-donald-7558647" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Mirror</i>)</a></li>
<li>A group of about 40 rabbis is planning to boycott Trump’s speech Monday at the <a href="/wiki/American_Israel_Public_Affairs_Committee#Policy_Conference" title="American Israel Public Affairs Committee">annual conference</a> of the <a href="/wiki/American_Israel_Public_Affairs_Committee" title="American Israel Public Affairs Committee">American Israel Public Affairs Committee</a> (AIPAC) because of the candidate's behavior and rhetoric on the campaign trail. Organizers of the push to boycott the speech said they are worried that Trump could gain legitimacy through the event. An AIPAC spokesperson declined to comment. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/rabbis-call-for-boycott-of-trumps-speech-to-pro-israel-group/2016/03/17/8e2f2ea6-ea14-11e5-a6f3-21ccdbc5f74e_story.html?wpmm=1&amp;wpisrc=nl_evening" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2016" title="United States presidential election, 2016">United States presidential election, 2016</a>, <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_presidential_primaries,_2016" title="Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2016">Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bernie_Sanders" title="Bernie Sanders">Bernie Sanders</a> concedes the <a href="/wiki/Missouri" title="Missouri">Missouri</a> <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_presidential_primaries,_2016#Schedule_and_results_of_primaries_and_caucuses" title="Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2016">primary</a> to <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a>, who led by 1,531 votes, 0.2 percent of those counted. Sanders says he will not ask for a <a href="/wiki/Election_recount" title="Election recount">recount</a>, an option he had because the result is under the state's requirement, 0.5 percent — one-half of one percent. The Republican contest is too close to call as <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> leads <a href="/wiki/Ted_Cruz" title="Ted Cruz">Ted Cruz</a> by a similar 0.2 percent. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msn.com/en-us/news/politics/sanders-concedes-missouri-democratic-primary-clinton-wins/ar-BBqy8m9?li=BBnbcA1" rel="nofollow">(AP via MSN.com)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> March 18, 2016<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2016-03-18</span>)</span> (Friday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_18&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_18&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_18&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Insurgency_in_the_Maghreb_(2002%E2%80%93present)" title="Insurgency in the Maghreb (2002–present)">Insurgency in the Maghreb (2002–present)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Boko_Haram" title="Boko Haram">Boko Haram</a> and <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda_in_the_Islamic_Maghreb" title="Al-Qaeda in the Islamic Maghreb">al-Qaeda</a> kill four security force personnel in two separate attacks in <a href="/wiki/Niger" title="Niger">Niger</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-africa-35842300" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="North Korea and weapons of mass destruction">North Korea and weapons of mass destruction</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/South_Korean_Joint_Chiefs_of_Staff" title="South Korean Joint Chiefs of Staff">South Korean Joint Chiefs of Staff</a> and a <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Defense" title="United States Department of Defense">U.S. defense</a> official report that <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> fired two <a href="/wiki/Ballistic_missile" title="Ballistic missile">ballistic missiles</a> from the <a href="/wiki/South_Pyongan_Province" title="South Pyongan Province">South Pyongan Province</a>. One flew 800 kilometers (497 miles) into the <a href="/wiki/Sea_of_Japan" title="Sea of Japan">Sea of Japan</a>. The other disappeared at an altitude of about 17 kilometers (10.5 miles). <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/story/1662062/north-korea-fires-ballistic-missile-into-sea" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/17/asia/north-korea-missile-launch/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_migrant_crisis" title="European migrant crisis">European migrant crisis</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> leaders offer <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> a detailed package of cash and incentives to agree that all <a href="/wiki/Immigration" title="Immigration">migrants</a> attempting to cross the <a href="/wiki/Aegean_Sea" title="Aegean Sea">Aegean Sea</a> by raft or boat would be sent back to Turkey which, in effect, becomes the region's migrant holding center. A number of stumbling blocks remain, such as raising the amount of aid from 3 billion euros to at least 6 billion euros; reducing the "72 arduous conditions" the Turks must meet to implement <a href="/wiki/Visa_requirements_for_Turkish_citizens" title="Visa requirements for Turkish citizens">visa-free travel for Turkish citizens</a>; Europe agrees to accelerate talks with <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Turkey#Executive" title="Politics of Turkey">Ankara</a> on its EU bid; etc. <a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Watch" title="Human Rights Watch">Human Rights Watch</a> protests the proposed fast-track collective expulsions that fail to take individual circumstances into account and breach peoples' <a href="/wiki/Refugee_law" title="Refugee law">right to seek asylum</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/europe/europe-offers-deal-to-turkey-to-take-back-migrants/2016/03/18/809d80ba-ebab-11e5-bc08-3e03a5b41910_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.turkishweekly.net/2016/03/18/news/eu-will-reach-deal-with-turkey-says-eu-s-schulz/" rel="nofollow">(Journal of Turkish Weekly)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> and <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkish</a> officials agree on how to handle the flood of refugees. The deal, to return irregular migrants to Turkey, includes acceleration of the country's long-stalled bid for membership in the union; billions of euros in extra aid, 3 billion euros now, another 3 billion by 2018; and, visa-free travel for Turks once the country satisfies the EU criteria. Europe will be taking in thousands of <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syrian</a> refugees directly from Turkey. <a href="/wiki/M%C3%A9decins_Sans_Fronti%C3%A8res" title="Médecins Sans Frontières">Médecins Sans Frontières</a> (Doctors Without Borders) strongly condemns the deal as "ugly and illegal." The agreement is set to go into effect Sunday, March 20, 2016. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/18/europe/eu-turkey-refugees/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.middleeasteye.net/news/eu-agrees-migration-deal-position-put-turkey-545791271" rel="nofollow">(Middle East Eye)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-europe-migrants-turkey-davutoglu-idUSKCN0WK0QQ" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Health and medicine</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Swiss</a> research, published in the medical journal <i><a href="/wiki/The_Lancet" title="The Lancet">The Lancet</a></i>, found that <a href="/wiki/Paracetamol" title="Paracetamol">paracetamol</a> -- sold as <a href="/wiki/Tylenol_(brand)" title="Tylenol (brand)">Tylenol</a> and as a generic, acetaminophen, in the United States -- was not effective at reducing pain or improving movement in patients with osteoarthritis of the knee or hip. The analysis examined 74 randomly-selected trials published between 1980 and 2015 with 58,556 patients who had osteoarthritis. The study did find the prescription drug <a href="/wiki/Diclofenac" title="Diclofenac">diclofenac</a>, sold in the U.S. as Cataflam or Voltaren, is the most effective <a href="/wiki/Nonsteroidal_anti-inflammatory_drug" title="Nonsteroidal anti-inflammatory drug">NSAID</a> available. <a href="/wiki/McNeil_Consumer_Healthcare" title="McNeil Consumer Healthcare">McNeil Consumer Healthcare</a>, the makers of Tylenol, disagree with the study's conclusions. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/news/acetaminophen-tylenol-doesnt-work-fore-osteoarthritis-study-finds/" rel="nofollow">(CBS News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.thelancet.com/journals/lancet/article/PIIS0140-6736%2816%2930002-2/abstract" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Lancet</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_United_States_Elizabethkingia_outbreak" title="2016 United States Elizabethkingia outbreak">2016 United States Elizabethkingia outbreak</a>
<ul>
<li>A rare bacterial infection from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bacterium" title="Bacterium">bacterium</a> <a href="/wiki/Elizabethkingia_anophelis" title="Elizabethkingia anophelis">Elizabethkingia anophelis</a> may have contributed to the deaths of 17 people since November 2015. <a class="external text" href="http://patch.com/illinois/chicago/rare-bacterial-infection-linked-deaths-wisconsin-michigan-0" rel="nofollow">(Patch)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.startribune.com/scientists-search-to-unravel-mystery-behind-blood-infection-outbreak-in-wisconsin/372610031/" rel="nofollow">(Star Tribune)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Geert_Wilders" title="Geert Wilders">Geert Wilders</a>, the leader of the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Dutch</a> far-right political party <a href="/wiki/Party_for_Freedom" title="Party for Freedom">Party for Freedom</a>, goes on trial again for making <a href="/wiki/Islamophobia" title="Islamophobia">anti-Islam</a> remarks. He is being accused of inciting hatred against the <a href="/wiki/Moroccan-Dutch" title="Moroccan-Dutch">Moroccan-Dutch</a> minority. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/18/dutch-far-right-leader-geert-wilders-goeson-trial-for-inciting-hatred" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Brussels_police_raids" title="2016 Brussels police raids">2016 Brussels police raids</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Salah_Abdeslam" title="Salah Abdeslam">Salah Abdeslam</a>, the alleged suspect and primary perpetrator of the <a href="/wiki/November_2015_Paris_attacks" title="November 2015 Paris attacks">November 2015 Paris attacks</a> is shot and arrested by Belgian authorities in a Brussels raid. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/18/paris-attacks-suspect-salah-abdeslam-wounded-in-brussels-terror-raid-reports" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Censorship_in_China" title="Censorship in China">Censorship in China</a>
<ul>
<li>Jia Jia, a columnist for <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China's</a> <a href="/wiki/Tencent" title="Tencent">Tencent</a> media company is reported missing after not being heard from since Tuesday, when he was on his way to <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a>. He was last heard from when he tried to warn a friend about publishing an anonymous letter calling for <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="President of the People's Republic of China">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Xi_Jinping" title="Xi Jinping">Xi Jinping's</a> resignation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-china-35828918" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump_presidential_campaign,_2016" title="Donald Trump presidential campaign, 2016">Donald Trump presidential campaign, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation" title="Federal Bureau of Investigation">FBI</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Joint_Terrorism_Task_Force" title="Joint Terrorism Task Force">Joint Terrorism Task Force</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secret_Service" title="United States Secret Service">United States Secret Service</a> and <a href="/wiki/New_York_City_Police_Department" title="New York City Police Department">New York City Police Department</a> are investigating a letter containing a suspicious white powder and a threatening note which was sent to the home of <a href="/wiki/Eric_Trump" title="Eric Trump">Eric Trump</a>, son of <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a>, in <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a>. The handwritten note within the letter said: "If your father does not drop out of the race, the next envelope won't be a fake." It was signed "X". <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/US/suspicious-letter-white-powder-donald-trumps-son/story?id=37738571" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bollea_v._Gawker" title="Bollea v. Gawker">Bollea v. Gawker</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">Florida</a> jury awards <a href="/wiki/Hulk_Hogan" title="Hulk Hogan">Hulk Hogan</a> $115m after the gossip news website <a href="/wiki/Gawker" title="Gawker">Gawker</a> published a sex tape of the retired <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling" title="Professional wrestling">professional wrestler</a>. Mr Hogan's legal team argued that the <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York City</a>-based website violated his privacy and that the video wasn't newsworthy. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-us-canada-35849140" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Apple" title="Apple">Apple</a> says it will bring two key personnel to a hearing next week, subjecting them to government cross-examination regarding the issues raised by its locked iPhone: its Chief Privacy Engineer and its Global Law Enforcement Officer. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-apple-encryption-hearing-idUSKCN0WK2A1" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Pakistan" title="President of Pakistan">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Pervez_Musharraf" title="Pervez Musharraf">Pervez Musharraf</a> travels to <a href="/wiki/Dubai" title="Dubai">Dubai</a> for medical treatment of his back and leg, before moving on to either the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> or <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">U.K.</a> for additional treatment, spokesperson <a href="/wiki/Aasia_Ishaque" title="Aasia Ishaque">Aasia Ishaque</a> said. Musharraf, 72, will return to <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> to face all pending legal cases. Earlier this week, <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Pakistan" title="Prime Minister of Pakistan">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Nawaz_Sharif" title="Nawaz Sharif">Nawaz Sharif’s</a> government implemented the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Pakistan" title="Supreme Court of Pakistan">Supreme Court</a> ruling, and lifted the 2013 ban that barred Musharraf from international trips. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-18/musharraf-leaves-pakistan-for-treatment-after-travel-ban-lifted" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iain_Duncan_Smith" title="Iain Duncan Smith">Iain Duncan Smith</a> resigns his position as the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Secretary_of_State_for_Work_and_Pensions" title="Secretary of State for Work and Pensions">Secretary of State for Work and Pensions</a>, in opposition to cuts in disability benefit proposed by <a href="/wiki/George_Osborne" title="George Osborne">George Osborne</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Chancellor_of_the_Exchequer" title="Chancellor of the Exchequer">Chancellor of the Exchequer</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-politics-35848687" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_protests_in_Brazil" title="2015–16 protests in Brazil">2015–16 protests in Brazil</a>, <a href="/wiki/Operation_Car_Wash" title="Operation Car Wash">Operation Car Wash</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Federal_Court" title="Supreme Federal Court">Supreme Court Justice</a> <a href="/wiki/Gilmar_Mendes" title="Gilmar Mendes">Gilmar Mendes</a> rules <a href="/wiki/Luiz_In%C3%A1cio_Lula_da_Silva" title="Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva">Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva</a> should be stripped of a ministerial role in <a href="/wiki/President_of_Brazil" title="President of Brazil">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff" title="Dilma Rousseff">Dilma Rousseff's</a> <a href="/wiki/Cabinet_of_Brazil" title="Cabinet of Brazil">Cabinet</a> so he can be investigated in connection with the state oil company <a href="/wiki/Petrobras" title="Petrobras">Petrobras's</a> alleged <a href="/wiki/Operation_Car_Wash" title="Operation Car Wash">kickback scheme</a>. Earlier today, injunctions suspending Lula's appointment as <a href="/wiki/Chief_of_Staff_of_Brazil" title="Chief of Staff of Brazil">chief of staff</a> were overturned at <a href="/wiki/Attorney_General_of_Brazil" title="Attorney General of Brazil">Attorney General</a> <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Eduardo_Cardozo" title="José Eduardo Cardozo">José Eduardo Cardozo's</a> request for a Supreme Court ruling on the motions. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theglobeandmail.com/news/world/brazilian-protesters-hit-with-water-cannons-tear-gas-as-impeachment-session-starts/article29288144/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Globe and Mail</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.thestar.com/news/world/2016/03/18/brazil-impeachment-gains-speed-as-lulas-job-challenged-in-court.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Toronto Star</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Deputies_(Brazil)" title="Chamber of Deputies (Brazil)">Brazil's lower house of Congress</a>, which yesterday overwhelmingly approved (433-1) a 65-member investigatory, presidential impeachment committee, was in session today -- unusual since lawmakers are generally away from the capital on Fridays. The charge alleges President Rousseff broke budget rules to boost <a href="/wiki/Government_spending" title="Government spending">public spending</a> in the run-up to her <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_general_election,_2014" title="Brazilian general election, 2014">re-election in 2014</a>. The president has 10 lower house sessions to present her defense. Friday's session means that clock has started and she now has nine sessions. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-brazil-politics-idUSKCN0WK1IF" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.swissinfo.ch/eng/reuters/brazil-lower-house-launches-impeachment-process-for-rousseff/42029958" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via Swiss Broadcasting Corporation)</a></li>
<li>Supporters of the governing <a href="/wiki/Workers%27_Party_(Brazil)" title="Workers' Party (Brazil)">Workers’ Party</a> took to the streets, in a sense answering the massive anti-government gatherings since Sunday, in all of <a href="/wiki/States_of_Brazil" title="States of Brazil">Brazil’s 26 states</a>. Organizations from both sides of the protests have called for people opposed to the Workers’ Party to stay home Friday to avoid a repeat of Thursday's clashes. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/big-crowds-demonstrate-in-brazil-in-solidarity-with-embattled-government/2016/03/18/a893a9ca-ed11-11e5-a9ce-681055c7a05f_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://latino.foxnews.com/latino/news/2016/03/18/turmoil-on-streets-brazil-as-pro-and-anti-government-protesters-face-off/" rel="nofollow">(Fox News Latino)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
