<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_2016_Istanbul_bombing" title="March 2016 Istanbul bombing">March 2016 Istanbul bombing</a>
<ul>
<li>An explosion occurs in <a href="/wiki/Taksim_Square" title="Taksim Square">Taksim Square</a> in <a href="/wiki/Istanbul" title="Istanbul">Istanbul</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>, kills five people, including two dual citizenship <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a>-<a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">Americans</a> and one <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> citizen, and injures several dozen others. <a class="external text" href="http://sputniknews.com/europe/20160319/1036574734/turkey-istanbul-blast.html" rel="nofollow">(Sputnik International)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2016/03/istanbul-taksim-square-area-hit-explosion-160319091702737.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Al Jazeera</i>)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.hurriyetdailynews.com/breaking-explosion-in-istanbuls-taksim-injuries-reported.aspx?pageID=238&amp;nID=96661&amp;NewsCatID=341" rel="nofollow">(<i>Hürriyet Daily News</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.muskokaregion.com/news-story/6398403-3-foreigners-among-5-killed-in-istanbul-suicide-bomb-attack/" rel="nofollow">(AP via MuskokaRegion.com)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>, <a href="/wiki/Palmyra_offensive_(March_2016)" title="Palmyra offensive (March 2016)">Palmyra offensive (March 2016)</a>
<ul>
<li>Airstrikes by <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Arab_Air_Force" title="Syrian Arab Air Force">Syrian</a> or <a href="/wiki/Russian_Air_Force" title="Russian Air Force">Russian</a> warplanes on <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a>'s de-facto capital <a href="/wiki/Al-Raqqah" title="Al-Raqqah">Al-Raqqah</a> in northern <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>, leaves at least 39 people dead, according to the <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Observatory_for_Human_Rights" title="Syrian Observatory for Human Rights">Syrian Observatory for Human Rights</a>. Airstrikes on the city of <a href="/wiki/Palmyra" title="Palmyra">Palmyra</a> and nearby villages are said to have killed at least 18 ISIL militants, as the <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Army" title="Syrian Army">Syrian Army</a> advance on the city. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-mideast-crisis-syria-raqqa-idUSKCN0WL0IW" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/American-led_intervention_in_Iraq_(2014%E2%80%93present)" title="American-led intervention in Iraq (2014–present)">American-led intervention in Iraq (2014–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Defense" title="United States Department of Defense">United States Department of Defense</a> official says a <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> soldier was killed in the town of <a href="/wiki/Makhmur,_Iraq" title="Makhmur, Iraq">Makhmur</a>, <a href="/wiki/Erbil_Governorate" title="Erbil Governorate">Erbil Governorate</a>, by a rocket fired by <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a>. "It was a lucky strike by ISIS," according to the official. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2016/03/19/american-soldier-killed-in-isis-rocket-attack-in-northern-iraq-official-says.html" rel="nofollow">(Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sinai_insurgency" title="Sinai insurgency">Sinai insurgency</a>
<ul>
<li>At least 13 <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_National_Police" title="Egyptian National Police">Egyptian policemen</a> are killed after a security checkpoint in the city of <a href="/wiki/Arish" title="Arish">Arish</a>, <a href="/wiki/North_Sinai_Governorate" title="North Sinai Governorate">North Sinai Governorate</a>, came under attack by militants. Ambulances were reportedly subjected to heavy gunfire as they attempted to reach the wounded. The <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant_%E2%80%93_Sinai_Province" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant – Sinai Province">Sinai branch</a> claimed responsibility for the attack. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-egypt-violence-idUSKCN0WL0VD" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Flydubai_Flight_981" title="Flydubai Flight 981">Flydubai Flight 981</a>
<ul>
<li>Flydubai Boeing 737-800 Flight FZ981, en route from <a href="/wiki/Dubai" title="Dubai">Dubai</a> for about four hours, crashes during landing in the Russian city of <a href="/wiki/Rostov-on-Don" title="Rostov-on-Don">Rostov-on-Don</a>, killing all 62 on board. It appears the jet crashed in poor visibility, some 50–100 meters left of the runway, during the second approach. <a href="/wiki/Rostov-on-Don_Airport" title="Rostov-on-Don Airport">Rostov-on-Don Airport</a> will remain closed until at least 9:00 am Moscow time. <a class="external text" href="https://www.rt.com/news/336185-boeing-crash-dubai-rostov/" rel="nofollow">(<i>RT</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://airwaysnews.com/blog/2016/03/18/flydubai-flight-981-crash/" rel="nofollow">(Airways News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-russia-crash-idUSKCN0WL036" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Nine <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuban</a> migrants die and 18 others are rescued by the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Caribbean_International" title="Royal Caribbean International">Royal Caribbean's</a> <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brilliance_of_the_Seas" title="Brilliance of the Seas">Brilliance of the Seas</a></i> cruise ship in the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico" title="Gulf of Mexico">Gulf of Mexico</a>, 130 miles west of <a href="/wiki/Marco_Island,_Florida" title="Marco Island, Florida">Marco Island, Florida</a>. The group had been sailing for 22 days in a 30-foot long "rustic" boat. The survivors were severely dehydrated and in poor condition. Those who had died were buried at sea. The cruise ship is taking the migrants to its next stop, the Mexican island of <a href="/wiki/Cozumel" title="Cozumel">Cozumel</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.pressherald.com/2016/03/19/nine-cuban-migrants-die-18-rescued-off-florida/" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Portland Press Herald</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> official and head of the UN mission for the <a href="/wiki/West_African_Ebola_virus_epidemic" title="West African Ebola virus epidemic">Ebola outbreak</a> <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Banbury" title="Anthony Banbury">Anthony Banbury</a> accuses the UN of “colossal mismanagement,” saying it had failed to uphold the principles for which it was established. He cited the organization's “<a href="/wiki/Orwellian" title="Orwellian">Orwellian</a> admonitions and <a href="/wiki/Lewis_Carroll" title="Lewis Carroll">Carrollian</a> logic” of the UN bureaucracy and minimal accountability regarding the widespread rape and sexual abuse by <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_peacekeeping" title="United Nations peacekeeping">UN peacekeepers</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/19/former-un-official-accuses-world-body-of-colossal-mismanagement" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_protests_in_Brazil" title="2015–16 protests in Brazil">2015–16 protests in Brazil</a>
<ul>
<li>A survey conducted by <a href="/wiki/Datafolha" title="Datafolha">Datafolha</a> shows a majority of <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilians</a> now favor the impeachment or resignation of <a href="/wiki/President_of_Brazil" title="President of Brazil">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff" title="Dilma Rousseff">Dilma Rousseff</a>. The poll showed 68 percent of respondents favor Rousseff's impeachment by <a href="/wiki/National_Congress_of_Brazil" title="National Congress of Brazil">Congress</a>, while 65 percent think the president should resign. The president's approval ratings have been hammered by Brazil's worst recession in decades and its <a href="/wiki/Operation_Car_Wash" title="Operation Car Wash">biggest ever corruption probe</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/uk-brazil-politics-poll-idUKKCN0WL0Y0" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_presidential_candidates,_2016" title="Republican Party presidential candidates, 2016">Republican Party presidential candidates, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Two dozen protesters park their cars in the middle of Shea Boulevard, and block the main road to the <a href="/wiki/Phoenix,_Arizona" title="Phoenix, Arizona">Phoenix</a> suburb of <a href="/wiki/Fountain_Hills,_Arizona" title="Fountain Hills, Arizona">Fountain Hills, Arizona</a>, where <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump's</a> campaign rally with former <a href="/wiki/List_of_Governors_of_Arizona" title="List of Governors of Arizona">Arizona Governor</a> <a href="/wiki/Jan_Brewer" title="Jan Brewer">Jan Brewer</a>, and controversial <a href="/wiki/Sheriff" title="Sheriff">sheriff</a> <a href="/wiki/Joe_Arpaio" title="Joe Arpaio">Joe Arpaio</a> was held. For hours, traffic was backed up for miles. The road was eventually cleared. Three protesters were arrested and two cars were towed from the boulevard. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/9aae82a47c234340b0ce5c16d8937552/protesters-block-main-road-trump-rally" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/19/politics/donald-trump-arizona-joe-arpaio/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbs5az.com/story/31516829/anti-trump-protesters-block-streets-in-fountain-hills?autostart=true" rel="nofollow">(KPHO-TV)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> <a href="/wiki/Speed_skating" title="Speed skating">speed skaters</a> <a href="/wiki/Pavel_Kulizhnikov" title="Pavel Kulizhnikov">Pavel Kulizhnikov</a>, <a href="/wiki/Semion_Elistratov" title="Semion Elistratov">Semion Elistratov</a> and Ekaterina Konstantinova test positive for <a href="/wiki/Meldonium" title="Meldonium">Meldonium</a> and are provisionally suspended by the <a href="/wiki/International_Skating_Union" title="International Skating Union">International Skating Union</a>. Kulizhnikov faces a potential lifetime ban while Elistratov and Konstantinova face up to four years. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/russian-champion-speedskaters-face-long-bans-for-doping/27622667.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Six_Nations_Championship" title="2016 Six Nations Championship">2016 Six Nations Championship</a>
<ul>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Rugby_union" title="Rugby union">rugby union</a>, <a href="/wiki/England_national_rugby_union_team" title="England national rugby union team">England</a>, which had already clinched the championship, defeat <a href="/wiki/France_national_rugby_union_team" title="France national rugby union team">France</a> 31–21 to claim their 13th <a href="/wiki/Grand_Slam_(rugby_union)" title="Grand Slam (rugby union)">Grand Slam</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/sport/live/2016/mar/19/france-v-england-six-nations-live" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/sport/rugby-union/35821697" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>

<li><a href="/wiki/March_2016_Istanbul_bombing" title="March 2016 Istanbul bombing">March 2016 Istanbul bombing</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkish</a> authorities name a Turkish man with alleged ties to the <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State</a> responsible for this weekend's suicide bombing in <a href="/wiki/Istanbul" title="Istanbul">Istanbul</a>. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/turkey-alleges-istanbul-bomber-was-a-member-of-the-islamic-state/2016/03/20/8b890b9c-eebd-11e5-a2a3-d4e9697917d1_story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/The_Church_of_Jesus_Christ_of_Latter-day_Saints_in_Utah" title="The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints in Utah">The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints in Utah</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dallin_H._Oaks" title="Dallin H. Oaks">Dallin H. Oaks</a> dedicates the <a href="/wiki/Provo_City_Center_Temple" title="Provo City Center Temple">Provo City Center Temple</a>, the 150th <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/LDS_temple" title="LDS temple">LDS temple</a> and the second temple converted from an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/LDS_tabernacle" title="LDS tabernacle">LDS tabernacle</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sltrib.com/home/3685690-155/mormons-rejoice-as-apostle-oaks-dedicates" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Salt Lake Tribune</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Cleveland" title="Cleveland">United States</a>-based <a href="/wiki/Sherwin-Williams" title="Sherwin-Williams">Sherwin-Williams Company</a> agrees to acquire rival <a href="/wiki/Minneapolis" title="Minneapolis">U.S.</a> <a href="/wiki/Paint" title="Paint">paint company</a> <a href="/wiki/Valspar" title="Valspar">Valspar Corporation</a> in an all-cash deal valued at about $9.3 billion (8.2 billion euros). <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/usa-sherwin-williams-valspar-idUSL2N16S0CK" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Erasmus_bus_crash" title="Erasmus bus crash">Erasmus bus crash</a>
<ul>
<li>Thirteen are killed and 34 others injured after a bus carrying <a href="/wiki/Erasmus_Programme" title="Erasmus Programme">Erasmus</a> <a href="/wiki/Student_exchange_program" title="Student exchange program">exchange students</a> returning from the renowned <a href="/wiki/Falles#Cavalcada_del_Foc" title="Falles">Falles fireworks festival</a> in <a href="/wiki/Valencia" title="Valencia">Valencia</a>, crashes near <a href="/wiki/Freginals" title="Freginals">Freginals</a>, <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>. The regional government of <a href="/wiki/Catalonia" title="Catalonia">Catalonia</a> said in a statement that, "... according to the latest data, the ill-fated bus had students from <a href="/wiki/Hungary" title="Hungary">Hungary</a>, <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a>, <a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norway</a>, <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">Czech Republic</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bulgaria" title="Bulgaria">Bulgaria</a>, <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ireland" title="Ireland">Ireland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a>, <a href="/wiki/Holland" title="Holland">Holland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a>, <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>, <a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/Palestine" title="Palestine">Palestine</a><sup class="plainlinks noprint Inline-Template" style="vertical-align:text-top;white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a class="external text" href="http://dispenser.homenet.org/~dispenser/cgi-bin/dab_solver.py?page=Portal:Current_events/March_2016&amp;editintro=Template:Disambiguation_needed/editintro&amp;client=Template:Dn" rel="nofollow"><span title="Link needs disambiguation. (March 2016)">disambiguation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>, <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>, (and) <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a>." <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/europe/spain-bus-crash-coach-carrying-university-students-crashes-near-barcelona-a6942316.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.euronews.com/2016/03/20/at-least-14-dead-after-bus-carrying-students-crashes-in-spain/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Euronews</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-20/urgent-spain-some-killed-injured-in-bus-crash-on-coastal-highway" rel="nofollow">(AP via Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A 6.6 <a href="/wiki/Moment_magnitude_scale" title="Moment magnitude scale">magnitude</a> <a href="/wiki/Earthquake" title="Earthquake">earthquake</a> strikes off the eastern coast of <a href="/wiki/Kamchatka_Peninsula" title="Kamchatka Peninsula">Kamchatka Peninsula</a> in <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Russian_Far_East" title="Russian Far East">Far East</a>. Shaking was felt throughout large parts of the peninsula, but there were no immediate reports of damage or casualties. <a class="external text" href="http://bnonews.com/news/index.php/news/id3900" rel="nofollow">(BNO News)</a></li>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/Indonesian_National_Armed_Forces" title="Indonesian National Armed Forces">Indonesian</a> <a href="/wiki/Military_helicopter" title="Military helicopter">military helicopter</a> crash shortly after takeoff from <a href="/wiki/Poso" title="Poso">Poso</a> kills 13 passengers. Their mission was to try to capture <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia's</a> most wanted militant, <a href="/wiki/Abu_Wardah" title="Abu Wardah">Abu Wardah Santoso</a>, leader of the <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State</a> affiliate <a href="/wiki/List_of_terrorist_incidents_in_Indonesia#2000s" title="List of terrorist incidents in Indonesia">East Indonesia Mujahidin network</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/5d377dc7b80c4531a9ee80ba2403032c/indonesian-military-helicopter-crashes-killing-12" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States%E2%80%93Cuban_Thaw" title="United States–Cuban Thaw">United States–Cuban Thaw</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">U.S. President</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> and the <a href="/wiki/First_Family_of_the_United_States" title="First Family of the United States">First Family</a> begin their three-day visit to <a href="/wiki/Havana" title="Havana">Havana</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>, to mark the end of 54 years of tensions in <a href="/wiki/Cuba%E2%80%93United_States_relations" title="Cuba–United States relations">Cuba–United States relations</a>. Obama is the first sitting U.S. president to visit the country since <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a> in 1928. <a class="external text" href="http://www.havanatimes.org/?p=117493" rel="nofollow">(<i>Havana Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.jamaicaobserver.com/news/OBAMA2016-03-20T13-29-54" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jamaica Observer</i>)</a></li>
<li>Before the President's arrival, Cuban authorities arrest more than 50 <a href="/wiki/Ladies_in_White" title="Ladies in White">Ladies in White</a> <a href="/wiki/Human_rights_activists" title="Human rights activists">human rights activists</a>. The group marches after every Sunday Mass at a church in the <a href="/wiki/Miramar,_Havana" title="Miramar, Havana">Miramar</a> <a href="/wiki/Suburb" title="Suburb">suburb</a> of Havana, and usually get arrested and detained for hours or days. They had hoped President Obama's visit would change that routine. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/news/world/2016/03/20/cuba-dissidents-protesters-arrested-president-obama-visit/82048950/" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.havanatimes.org/?p=117493" rel="nofollow">(<i>Havana Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A retired <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania_State_Police" title="Pennsylvania State Police">Pennsylvania state trooper's</a> attempted robbery of a <a href="/wiki/Armored_car_(valuables)" title="Armored car (valuables)">fare collection vehicle</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania_Turnpike" title="Pennsylvania Turnpike">Pennsylvania Turnpike's</a> <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania_Turnpike#Exit_list" title="Pennsylvania Turnpike">Fort Littleton toll plaza</a>, 65 miles west of the capital <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Harrisburg" title="Harrisburg">Harrisburg</a>, results in three deaths -- a <a href="/wiki/Toll_house" title="Toll house">toll collector</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Security_guard" title="Security guard">security guard</a>, and himself. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/US/wireStory/turnpike-employee-worker-suspect-killed-robbery-attempt-37796138" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Beninese_presidential_election,_2016" title="Beninese presidential election, 2016">Beninese presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voting for the second round of <a href="/wiki/Benin" title="Benin">Benin's</a> election begins with current <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_Benin" title="List of heads of state of Benin">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Boni_Yayi" title="Thomas Boni Yayi">Thomas Boni Yayi</a> stepping down after completing two terms. <a class="external text" href="http://townhall.com/news/politics-elections/2016/03/20/benin-rivals-face-off-in-hotly-contested-presidential-runoff-n2136728" rel="nofollow">(Townhall via Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cape_Verdean_parliamentary_election,_2016" title="Cape Verdean parliamentary election, 2016">Cape Verdean parliamentary election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/Cape_Verde" title="Cape Verde">Cape Verde</a> go to the polls for an election. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-africa-35854768" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kazakhstani_legislative_election,_2016" title="Kazakhstani legislative election, 2016">Kazakhstani legislative election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voting is underway in today's parliamentary election in the former Soviet republic. <a href="/wiki/List_of_leaders_of_Kazakhstan#Presidents_of_the_Republic_of_Kazakhstan_.281990-present.29" title="List of leaders of Kazakhstan">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Nursultan_Nazarbayev" title="Nursultan Nazarbayev">Nursultan Nazarbayev's</a> <a href="/wiki/Nur_Otan" title="Nur Otan">Nur Otan</a> party is expected to win easily, and retain control of the 107-seat <a href="/wiki/Mazhilis" title="Mazhilis">Mazhilis</a>, the lower house of parliament. The recent crackdown on political activists and media dims chances this election will be the first judged free and fair by Western observers. <a class="external text" href="http://siouxcityjournal.com/news/world/asia/voting-in-parliamentary-election-begins-in-kazakhstan/article_4f0ef6a6-1e2a-5a10-a14f-d13661f70273.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Sioux City Journal</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://townhall.com/news/politics-elections/2016/03/20/kazakhstans-election-could-yield-clue-to-succession-n2136691" rel="nofollow">(Townhall.com)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Laotian_parliamentary_election,_2016" title="Laotian parliamentary election, 2016">Laotian parliamentary election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>An election is held in <a href="/wiki/Laos" title="Laos">Laos</a>, with voter turnout expected to be low. The only legal party in Laos is the <a href="/wiki/Lao_People%27s_Revolutionary_Party" title="Lao People's Revolutionary Party">Lao People's Revolutionary Party</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.vidalatinasd.com/news/2016/mar/20/laos-holds-national-assembly-elections/" rel="nofollow">(Vida Latina)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nigerien_general_election,_2016" title="Nigerien general election, 2016">Nigerien general election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>A run-off election begins in <a href="/wiki/Niger" title="Niger">Niger</a> with current <a href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_Niger" title="List of heads of state of Niger">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Mahamadou_Issoufou" title="Mahamadou Issoufou">Mahamadou Issoufou</a> highly favored to win as his main opponent <a href="/wiki/Hama_Amadou" title="Hama Amadou">Hama Amadou</a>, who was earlier jailed, was flown out of the country for medical reasons. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-niger-election-idUSKCN0WM08N" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Philippine_presidential_election,_2016" title="Philippine presidential election, 2016">Philippine presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/PiliPinas_Debates_2016_%E2%80%93_Visayas_leg" title="PiliPinas Debates 2016 – Visayas leg">second leg</a> of the <a href="/wiki/PiliPinas_Debates_2016" title="PiliPinas Debates 2016">presidential debates</a> was held in <a href="/wiki/Cebu_City" title="Cebu City">Cebu City</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.japantimes.co.jp/news/2016/03/21/asia-pacific/philippine-presidential-debate-erupts-heated-exchanges-gets-personal/#.Vu-d9tJ96t9" rel="nofollow">AP via <i>The Japan Times</i></a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republic_of_the_Congo_presidential_election,_2016" title="Republic of the Congo presidential election, 2016">Republic of the Congo presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voters in the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Republic of the Congo">Republic of the Congo</a> go to the polls with current <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_the_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="List of heads of state of the Republic of the Congo">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Denis_Sassou_Nguesso" title="Denis Sassou Nguesso">Denis Sassou Nguesso</a> expected to extend his 32-year rule. Telephone, internet and SMS services have been shut down in what has been called a "media blackout." <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2016/03/congo-media-blackout-presidential-elections-160320044041238.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Al Jazeera</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Senegalese_constitutional_referendum,_2016" title="Senegalese constitutional referendum, 2016">Senegalese constitutional referendum, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>A referendum is underway in <a href="/wiki/Senegal" title="Senegal">Senegal</a> where voters will vote on whether or not to reduce presidential term limits from seven to five years. Senegal's referendum also calls for a strengthened <a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_(Senegal)" title="National Assembly (Senegal)">National Assembly</a>, better representation for Senegalese abroad, greater rights for the opposition and participation of independent candidates in elections among the 15 changes. <a class="external text" href="https://www.dailystar.com.lb/News/World/2016/Mar-20/343128-senegal-votes-on-referendum-to-reduce-presidential-term.ashx" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Star</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tanzanian_general_election,_2015" title="Tanzanian general election, 2015">Tanzanian general election, 2015</a>
<ul>
<li>A rerun of <a href="/wiki/Zanzibar" title="Zanzibar">Zanzibar's</a> presidential election takes place amid an opposition boycott. The election originally occurred at the same time as <a href="/wiki/Tanzania" title="Tanzania">Tanzania's</a> general election in 2015 but was annulled because of supposed fraud. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nation.co.ke/news/africa/Zanzibar-holds-presidential-election-amid-rising-tension/-/1066/3123290/-/g7dkln/-/index.html" rel="nofollow">(Daily Nation)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> March 21, 2016<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2016-03-21</span>)</span> (Monday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_21&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_21&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_21&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A man detonates a grenade inside a bakery in <a href="/wiki/Belgrade" title="Belgrade">Belgrade</a>, <a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a>, killing himself. No other casualties were reported. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/serbia-belgrade-grenade-bakery/27626225.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
<li>Gunmen attack a <a href="/wiki/Military_of_the_European_Union" title="Military of the European Union">European Union military training operation</a> housed in a converted hotel in the <a href="/wiki/Mali" title="Mali">Mali</a> capital, <a href="/wiki/Bamako" title="Bamako">Bamako</a>. There are no casualties among the mission personnel. One suspect is killed and two are arrested. No group has claimed responsibility. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-mali-attack-idUSKCN0WN234" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The competition regulators of the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> have halted their investigation into a prospective acquisition of <a href="/wiki/Baker_Hughes" title="Baker Hughes">Baker Hughes</a> by <a href="/wiki/Halliburton" title="Halliburton">Halliburton</a>, effectively freezing any such combination between two giant providers of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Oilfield_services" title="Oilfield services">oilfield services</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-bakerhughes-m-a-halliburton-eu-idUSKCN0WN11J" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Erasmus_bus_crash" title="Erasmus bus crash">Erasmus bus crash</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Catalans" title="Catalans">Catalan</a> official says the 13 <a href="/wiki/Student_exchange_program" title="Student exchange program">exchange students</a> killed in Sunday's accident were 19-to-25-year-old women, seven from <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>, two <a href="/wiki/Germans" title="Germans">Germans</a>, an <a href="/wiki/Austrians" title="Austrians">Austrian</a>, a woman from <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Romanians" title="Romanians">Romanian</a> and an <a href="/wiki/Uzbekistan" title="Uzbekistan">Uzbek</a>. Twenty-four people are being treated in hospital with one student in critical condition, and six people, including the driver, in serious condition. Reports from officials indicate the driver lost control of the coach and crashed to the other side before running into an oncoming car. The bus driver, who passed alcohol and drug tests, is being investigated for possible negligent homicide as police seek to determine the cause of the crash. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/europe/spain-7-of-13-student-bush-crash-victims-were-italian/2016/03/21/e5fcf894-ef45-11e5-a2a3-d4e9697917d1_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>the Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/7-italians-2-germans-among-spain-coach-crash-082422852.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Yahoo! News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/North_Korea_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="North Korea and weapons of mass destruction">North Korea and weapons of mass destruction</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korean</a> <a href="/wiki/Joint_Chiefs_of_Staff_(South_Korea)" title="Joint Chiefs of Staff (South Korea)">Joint Chiefs of Staff</a> official reports <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> launched five <a href="/wiki/Ballistic_missile#Missile_types" title="Ballistic missile">short-range missiles</a> from the eastern city of <a href="/wiki/Hamhung" title="Hamhung">Hamhung</a> into the <a href="/wiki/Sea_of_Japan" title="Sea of Japan">Sea of Japan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msn.com/en-us/news/world/n-korea-fires-five-short-range-missiles-into-sea/ar-BBqICNc?li=BBnb7Kz&amp;ocid=edgsp" rel="nofollow">(AFP via msn.com)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States%E2%80%93Cuban_Thaw" title="United States–Cuban Thaw">United States–Cuban Thaw</a>
<ul>
<li>At a 55-minute joint press conference, following their two-hour closed door meeting, <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">United States President</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Barrack_Obama" title="Barrack Obama">Barrack Obama</a> and <a href="/wiki/President_of_Cuba" title="President of Cuba">Cuban President</a> <a href="/wiki/Ra%C3%BAl_Castro" title="Raúl Castro">Raúl Castro</a> agreed this “new day” of openness between the two countries benefits the entire hemisphere as well. Each acknowledged more needs to be done. Obama said he spoke frankly about human rights, free expression, and democracy; Castro said the U.S. needs to remove the <a href="/wiki/Guantanamo_Bay_Naval_Base" title="Guantanamo Bay Naval Base">military base at Guantanamo Bay</a>, and completely end the U.S. embargo. Obama's experience gave him an advantage when journalists delved into sensitive areas. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/on-first-full-day-in-cuba-obama-to-meet-with-castro-and-address-the-public/2016/03/20/931e4ff6-eef5-11e5-89c3-a647fcce95e0_story.html?wpmm=1&amp;wpisrc=nl_headlines" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/03/22/world/americas/obama-and-raul-castro-to-meet-in-pivotal-moment-for-us-cuba-thaw.html?em_pos=large&amp;emc=edit_nn_20160322&amp;nl=morning-briefing&amp;nlid=11553763&amp;_r=0" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tea_tape_scandal" title="Tea tape scandal">Tea tape scandal</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_New_Zealand" title="Prime Minister of New Zealand">New Zealand Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/John_Key" title="John Key">John Key</a> settles a <a href="/wiki/Defamation" title="Defamation">defamation</a> case with freelance cameraman Bradley Ambrose, acknowledging comments he made about the man caused him professional and personal harm. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/e33d9ce1ff87423cb951d646eab31b47/new-zealand-premier-settles-defamation-case-journalist" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/International_Criminal_Court" title="International Criminal Court">International Criminal Court</a> finds ex-Vice President of the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a> <a href="/wiki/Jean-Pierre_Bemba" title="Jean-Pierre Bemba">Jean-Pierre Bemba</a> guilty of <a href="/wiki/War_crime" title="War crime">war crimes</a>. Bemba is accused of not taking steps to stop his <a href="/wiki/Movement_for_the_Liberation_of_the_Congo" title="Movement for the Liberation of the Congo">militia</a> from committing mass murder, rape and pillage in neighbouring <a href="/wiki/Central_African_Republic" title="Central African Republic">Central African Republic</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/21/icc-finds-ex-congolese-vice-president-jean-pierre-bemba-guilty-of-war-crimes" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">United States Supreme Court</a>, in a 6-2 ruling, essentially upholds the state of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cannabis_policy_of_Colorado" title="Cannabis policy of Colorado">Colorado's legalization of marijuana</a>, turning down complaints by the neighboring states of Nebraska and Oklahoma that, by <a href="/wiki/Legal_history_of_cannabis_in_the_United_States" title="Legal history of cannabis in the United States">federal and their state law</a>, Colorado's statutes allow "illegal marijuana" to pour into their states. Last year, the justices asked the federal government to weigh in; in December, <a href="/wiki/Solicitor_General_of_the_United_States" title="Solicitor General of the United States">Solicitor General</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Donald_B._Verrilli,_Jr." title="Donald B. Verrilli, Jr.">Donald Verrilli Jr.</a> urged the court to turn away the lawsuit. Justices <a href="/wiki/Clarence_Thomas" title="Clarence Thomas">Clarence Thomas</a> and <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Alito" title="Samuel Alito">Samuel Alito</a> dissented. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sfgate.com/nation/article/Supreme-Court-rejects-challenge-to-Colorado-pot-6929460.php" rel="nofollow">(<i>San Francisco Chronicle</i></a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/news/us-news/u-s-supreme-court-declines-referee-state-disputes-over-marijuana-n542551" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/news/2015/12/16/feds-ask-supreme-court-stay-out-lawsuit-over-colorado-marijuana/77457652/" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Myanmar" title="Myanmar">Myanmar</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Assembly_of_the_Union" title="Assembly of the Union">new parliament</a>, in its first legislative act, votes (611-3) to eliminate 15 government ministries. President-elect <a href="/wiki/Htin_Kyaw" title="Htin Kyaw">Htin Kyaw</a> says by eliminating the ministers' salaries, the nation will save $4 million over five years. No civil servants will lose their jobs. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/4c8c2d58f58b475b9a690f3190f03465/myanmar-parliament-votes-reduce-number-ministries" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Two possibly-twin <a href="/wiki/Near-Earth_object" title="Near-Earth object">near-Earth objects</a>, <a href="/wiki/252P/LINEAR" title="252P/LINEAR">252P/LINEAR</a> and P/2016 BA14, will safely pass by <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">Earth</a> at relatively close distances today and Tuesday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.csmonitor.com/Science/2016/0319/Twin-comets-will-buzz-by-Earth-but-not-too-close" rel="nofollow">(<i>Christian Science Monitor</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.sciencealert.com/two-comets-will-make-the-closest-flyby-of-earth-since-1770-this-week" rel="nofollow">(Science Alert)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://www.nasa.gov/feature/jpl/a-tail-of-two-comets" rel="nofollow">(NASA)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.virtualtelescope.eu/webtv/" rel="nofollow">(Virtual Telescope Project)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_22&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Brussels_bombings" title="2016 Brussels bombings">2016 Brussels bombings</a>
<ul>
<li>Three explosions in the <a href="/wiki/Brussels_Airport" title="Brussels Airport">Brussels Airport</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maelbeek/Maalbeek_metro_station" title="Maelbeek/Maalbeek metro station">Maalbeek metro station</a> kill at least 34 people and wound at least 170 more, according to <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgian</a> media. Belgian federal Prosecutor Frederic Van Leeuw cautions it is too soon to know exactly how many people died in the bombings. The <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a> claims responsibility. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-35869254" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/22/europe/brussels-explosions/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/22/europe/brussels-explosions/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN²)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/03/23/world/europe/brussels-airport-explosions.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabian-led_intervention_in_Yemen" title="Saudi Arabian-led intervention in Yemen">Saudi Arabian-led intervention in Yemen</a>
<ul>
<li>Airstrikes near the <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemeni</a> port city of <a href="/wiki/Al_Mukalla" title="Al Mukalla">Al Mukalla</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hadhramaut_Governorate" title="Hadhramaut Governorate">Hadhramaut Governorate</a>, reportedly kill at least 30 <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda_in_the_Arabian_Peninsula" title="Al-Qaeda in the Arabian Peninsula">Al-Qaeda</a> militants. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-yemen-security-strikes-idUSKCN0WO2TV" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">German</a> tax authorities are investigating <a href="/wiki/Citigroup" title="Citigroup">Citigroup</a> over its use of a "dividend stripping" strategy, which allowed both the buyer and seller of a stock to claim the tax credits. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-citigroup-germany-taxes-idUSKCN0WO127" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Brussels_bombings" title="2016 Brussels bombings">2016 Brussels bombings</a>
<ul>
<li>In light of the <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgian</a> attacks, <a href="/wiki/Warner_Bros." title="Warner Bros.">Warner Bros.</a> cancels the <a href="/wiki/Red_carpet#Publicity_events" title="Red carpet">red carpet</a> but will hold the European premiere of the highly-publicized film, <i><a href="/wiki/Batman_v_Superman:_Dawn_of_Justice" title="Batman v Superman: Dawn of Justice">Batman v Superman: Dawn of Justice</a></i>, at <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London's</a> <a href="/wiki/Leicester_Square" title="Leicester Square">Leicester Square</a> tonight. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/film/batman-v-superman-dawn-of-justice/premiere-london-cancelled-brussels/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Colombian_conflict" title="Colombian conflict">Colombian conflict</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_State" title="United States Secretary of State">Secretary of State</a> <a href="/wiki/John_Kerry" title="John Kerry">John Kerry</a> holds a meeting with leaders of <a href="/wiki/FARC" title="FARC">FARC</a> in a sign of encouragement in ending <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia's</a> half-century old conflict. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/22/john-kerry-unprecedented-peace-talks-colombia-farc-rebels-havana" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Finland%E2%80%93Russia_relations" title="Finland–Russia relations">Finland–Russia relations</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Finland" title="Finland">Finland</a> and <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> agree to impose temporary restrictions at two Arctic border crossing points on the <a href="/wiki/Finnish%E2%80%93Russian_border" title="Finnish–Russian border">Finnish–Russian border</a> following an increased flow of asylum seekers from Russia to Finland. Under a deal clinched by <a href="/wiki/President_of_Russia" title="President of Russia">Russian President</a> <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a> and <a href="/wiki/President_of_Finland" title="President of Finland">Finnish President</a> <a href="/wiki/Sauli_Niinist%C3%B6" title="Sauli Niinistö">Sauli Niinistö</a> in <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a>, crossings at two popular entry points, <a href="/wiki/Salla" title="Salla">Salla</a> and Raja-Jooseppi, will be reserved only for Finnish, Russian and <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarusian</a> citizens and their family members for a period of 180 days. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-europe-migrants-finland-russia-idUSKCN0WO32P" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia%E2%80%93United_States_relations" title="Russia–United States relations">Russia–United States relations</a>, <a href="/wiki/Syrian_peace_process" title="Syrian peace process">Syrian peace process</a>, <a href="/wiki/War_in_Donbass" title="War in Donbass">War in Donbass</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_State" title="United States Secretary of State">Secretary of State</a> <a href="/wiki/John_Kerry" title="John Kerry">John Kerry</a> leaves for <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> for talks on <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a> with <a href="/wiki/President_of_Russia" title="President of Russia">Russian President</a> <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Minister_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Russia)" title="Minister of Foreign Affairs (Russia)">Foreign Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Sergey_Lavrov" title="Sergey Lavrov">Sergey Lavrov</a> on Wednesday. Kerry is also expected to discuss the case of <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukrainian</a> <a href="/wiki/Nadiya_Savchenko" title="Nadiya Savchenko">pilot Nadiya Savchenko</a>, who today was sentenced to 22 years in prison in the city of <a href="/wiki/Donetsk,_Russia" title="Donetsk, Russia">Donetsk</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/Politics/wireStory/kerry-off-russia-syria-talks-brussels-attacks-loom-37850028" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.themoscowtimes.com/article/563143.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Moscow Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-35873683" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A court in southern <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> finds <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukrainian</a> pilot <a href="/wiki/Nadiya_Savchenko" title="Nadiya Savchenko">Nadiya Savchenko</a> guilty of being complicit in the killing of two Russian journalists, killing civilians and illegal border crossing and is sentenced to 22 years in prison and a fine of 30,000 <a href="/wiki/Russian_ruble" title="Russian ruble">rubles</a>. Savchenko denies all the charges and the Ukrainian government said that they would continue to press for her release. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/russian-court-resumes-reading-savchenko-verdict/27627982.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/FBI%E2%80%93Apple_encryption_dispute" title="FBI–Apple encryption dispute">FBI–Apple encryption dispute</a>
<ul>
<li>A federal judge postpones Tuesday's hearing at the government's request. The <a href="/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation" title="Federal Bureau of Investigation">FBI</a> says a third party demonstrated a way to access <a href="/wiki/2015_San_Bernardino_attack" title="2015 San Bernardino attack">Syed Rizwan Farook's</a> <a href="/wiki/IPhone" title="IPhone">iPhone</a>. Melanie Newman, <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Justice" title="United States Department of Justice">U.S. Department of Justice</a> spokeswoman, says officials are cautiously optimistic a test of this method will allow access to the phone without compromising the data. <a class="external text" href="http://www.npr.org/sections/thetwo-way/2016/03/21/471353161/fbi-says-it-may-be-able-to-access-shooters-iphone-without-apples-help" rel="nofollow">(NPR)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/Technology/us-government-apples-encryption-case/story?id=37838682" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">United States Supreme Court</a>, in a 6-2 ruling written by <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Kennedy" title="Anthony Kennedy">Justice Anthony Kennedy</a>, upholds the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Court_of_Appeals_for_the_Eighth_Circuit" title="United States Court of Appeals for the Eighth Circuit">8th U.S. Circuit Court of Appeals'</a> $5.8 million <a href="/wiki/Class_action" title="Class action">class action</a> judgment against <a href="/wiki/Tyson_Foods" title="Tyson Foods">Tyson Foods Incorporated</a> filed by workers at an <a href="/wiki/Iowa" title="Iowa">Iowa</a> pork-processing facility who contended they were underpaid. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-usa-court-tyson-foods-idUSKCN0WO1Y1" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2016" title="United States presidential election, 2016">United States presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voters in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> states of <a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election_in_Arizona,_2016" title="United States presidential election in Arizona, 2016">Arizona</a>, <a href="/wiki/Idaho_Democratic_caucuses,_2016" title="Idaho Democratic caucuses, 2016">Idaho</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election_in_Utah,_2016" title="United States presidential election in Utah, 2016">Utah</a> and the overseas territory of <a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election_in_American_Samoa,_2016" title="United States presidential election in American Samoa, 2016">American Samoa</a> head to the polls for <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_presidential_primaries,_2016" title="Republican Party presidential primaries, 2016">Republican</a> and <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_presidential_primaries,_2016" title="Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2016">Democratic Party</a> primaries and caucuses. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ibtimes.co.uk/everything-you-need-know-about-22-march-races-arizona-idaho-utah-1550652" rel="nofollow">(International Business Times)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Arizona" title="Arizona">Arizona</a> primary. <a class="external text" href="http://www.decisiondeskhq.com/results/2016/primary/gop/president/arizona/" rel="nofollow">(Decision Desk HQ)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Toronto_City_Council" title="Toronto City Council">Toronto city councillor</a> and former <a href="/wiki/List_of_mayors_of_Toronto" title="List of mayors of Toronto">mayor</a> <a href="/wiki/Rob_Ford" title="Rob Ford">Rob Ford</a> dies after an 18-month battle with <a href="/wiki/Liposarcoma" title="Liposarcoma">liposarcoma</a>, a rare and aggressive cancer. It was first diagnosed in the midst of his 2014 bid to be re-elected mayor. He was 46. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thestar.com/news/gta/2016/03/22/rob-ford-former-toronto-mayor-dead-after-battle-with-cancer.html" rel="nofollow">(Toronto Star)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.blogto.com/city/2016/03/former_toronto_mayor_rob_ford_has_died/" rel="nofollow">(BlogTO)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_protests_in_Brazil" title="2015–16 protests in Brazil">2015–16 protests in Brazil</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_Brazil" title="President of Brazil">Brazil President</a> <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff" title="Dilma Rousseff">Dilma Rousseff</a> says she will not resign under any circumstances because she hadn't committed a crime, and equated a bid to impeach her to a <a href="/wiki/Coup_d%27%C3%A9tat" title="Coup d'état">coup d'état</a> against democratic rule. A congressional impeachment committee has started hearings. Rousseff could be suspended if the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Deputies_(Brazil)" title="Chamber of Deputies (Brazil)">Chamber of Deputies</a> approves the motion to impeach. The president urged the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Federal_Court" title="Supreme Federal Court">Supreme Court</a> to remain impartial in this political crisis. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-brazil-politics-idUSKCN0WO2LU" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://au.news.yahoo.com/world/a/31149721/brazils-lula-victim-of-intimidation-campaign-foundation/" rel="nofollow">(Yahoo7)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Indian_Wells_Masters" title="Indian Wells Masters">Indian Wells</a> (<a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a>) CEO and tennis tournament director <a href="/wiki/Raymond_Moore_(tennis)" title="Raymond Moore (tennis)">Raymond Moore</a> resigns following reactions of outrage, including by top-ranked <a href="/wiki/Serena_Williams" title="Serena Williams">Serena Williams</a> and retired legend <a href="/wiki/Martina_Navratilova" title="Martina Navratilova">Martina Navratilova</a>, to his comment that top-level women's players rode "on the coattails of the men" and were "very, very lucky" to have equal prize money. This is the event's second controversy involving female players. Serena and her sister <a href="/wiki/Venus_Williams" title="Venus Williams">Venus</a> boycotted the tournament (also known as the <a href="/wiki/BNP_Paribas" title="BNP Paribas">BNP Paribas</a> Open) until 2015 following verbal abuse directed toward the sisters in the 2001 open. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-tennis-indianwells-moore-idUSKCN0WO0F8" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://economictimes.indiatimes.com/magazines/panache/sexist-remark-costs-indian-wells-raymond-moore-his-director-job/articleshow/51510559.cms" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>The Economic Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://time.com/3694659/serena-williams-indian-wells/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Time</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Brussels_bombings" title="2016 Brussels bombings">2016 Brussels bombings</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgian</a> federal prosecutor Frederic Van Leeuw says two brothers of Belgian nationality, Khalid and Brahim el-Bakraoui, were responsible for yesterday's suicide bombings. Khalid bombed the subway station while Ibrahim bombed the airport, he added. A third suspect, who died at the airport, is identified as Najim Laachraoui, says <i><a href="/wiki/De_Standaard" title="De Standaard">De Standaard</a></i>. A fourth suspect seen in the airport photo, who left a massive bomb at the airport that did not detonate, is unidentified and still at large. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2016/03/23/Belgian-prosecutor-confirms-Brussels-bombing-brothers-identities-describes-note-left-by-one/8501458722374/?spt=hts&amp;or=1" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/world/europe/la-fg-suspect-in-brussels-attacks-is-sought-20160323-story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.standaard.be/cnt/dmf20160322_02197048" rel="nofollow">(<i>De Standaard</i>)</a></li>
<li>Van Leeuw says 31 people died and 271 are injured in the bombings. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2016/03/23/Belgian-prosecutor-confirms-Brussels-bombing-brothers-identities-describes-note-left-by-one/8501458722374/?spt=hts&amp;or=1" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
<li>Referring to the Brussels bombings, <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a> abandons a pledge to shelter <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syrian</a> migrants under a <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> relocation agreement. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-belgium-blast-poland-idUSKCN0WP1D1" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yemeni_Civil_War_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Yemeni Civil War (2015–present)">Yemeni Civil War (2015–present)</a>, <a href="/wiki/War_on_Terror" title="War on Terror">War on Terror</a>
<ul>
<li>At least 50 militants are reportedly killed in a <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> air strike on an <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda_in_the_Arabian_Peninsula" title="Al-Qaeda in the Arabian Peninsula">Al-Qaeda</a> training camp in southern <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-usa-yemen-strike-idUSKCN0WO37I" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Labor" title="United States Department of Labor">U.S. Labor Department</a> releases a long-awaited rule, the so-called persuader rule that was first proposed in 2011. The regulation requires companies to disclose when they seek advice about <a href="/wiki/Opposition_to_trade_unions" title="Opposition to trade unions">countering union campaigns</a>. The final rule will apply to contracts beginning on July 1, 2016. Several business groups, such as the <a href="/wiki/National_Retail_Federation" title="National Retail Federation">National Retail Federation</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Associated_Builders_and_Contractors" title="Associated Builders and Contractors">Associated Builders and Contractors</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Chamber_of_Commerce" title="United States Chamber of Commerce">U.S. Chamber of Commerce</a> and the <a href="/wiki/National_Association_of_Manufacturers" title="National Association of Manufacturers">National Association of Manufacturers</a>, object because the rule limits employers' free speech rights to counter union organizing, it could interfere with attorney-client privilege, etc. Court challenges are expected. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-usa-labor-persuader-idUSKCN0WP2GX" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://thehill.com/regulation/pending-regs/274022-dol-unveils-persuader-rule" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Hill</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_North_American_winter" title="2015–16 North American winter">2015–16 North American winter</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Late_March_2016_North_American_blizzard" title="Late March 2016 North American blizzard">Late March 2016 North American blizzard</a>
<ul>
<li>A powerful <a href="/wiki/Blizzard" title="Blizzard">blizzard</a> sweeping <a href="/wiki/Denver" title="Denver">Denver</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colorado" title="Colorado">Colorado</a>, forces authorities to close <a href="/wiki/Denver_International_Airport" title="Denver International Airport">Denver International Airport</a>, <a href="/wiki/Interstate_70_in_Colorado" title="Interstate 70 in Colorado">Interstate 70</a>, <a href="/wiki/Interstate_25_in_Colorado" title="Interstate 25 in Colorado">Interstate 25</a> and leaves more than 100,000 people without power. The <a href="/wiki/Colorado_Army_National_Guard" title="Colorado Army National Guard">Colorado Army National Guard</a> has been deployed to help rescue those stranded by the storm. <a class="external text" href="http://www.denverpost.com/weathernews/ci_29674648/denver-under-blizzard-warning-between-6-12-inches" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Denver Post</i>)</a></li>
<li>Denver International Airport reopens at 7 pm (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mountain_Daylight_Time#United_States" title="Mountain Daylight Time">Mountain Daylight Time</a>). Over 1,300 flights were canceled. Just a few flights are expected to arrive or depart through the night. The <a href="/wiki/National_Weather_Service" title="National Weather Service">National Weather Service</a> estimates that parts of Denver received 19.5 inches of snow as of 3:59 pm (MDT). <a class="external text" href="http://www.denverpost.com/weathernews/ci_29674737/blizzard-causes-250-flight-cancellations-power-outages-at" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Denver Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.denverpost.com/weathernews/ci_29674842/colorado-snow-totals-march-23-2016?source=pkg" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Denver Post</i>²)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_migrant_crisis" title="European migrant crisis">European migrant crisis</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/M%C3%A9decins_Sans_Fronti%C3%A8res" title="Médecins Sans Frontières">Médecins Sans Frontières</a> (Doctors Without Borders) and the UN refugee agency, <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_High_Commissioner_for_Refugees" title="United Nations High Commissioner for Refugees">UNHCR</a>, announce they are withdrawing from the so-called hotspots on the Greek islands because of the new EU-Turkey deal. UNHCR's Melissa Fleming says, "Under the new provisions, these sites (hotspots) have now become <a href="/wiki/Immigration_detention" title="Immigration detention">detention facilities</a>." MSF's Marie Elisabeth Ingres says, “We will not allow our assistance to be instrumentalized (sic) for a mass expulsion operation, and we refuse to be part of a system that has no regard for the <a href="/wiki/Humanitarianism" title="Humanitarianism">humanitarian</a> or protection needs of <a href="/wiki/Refugee#Asylum_seekers" title="Refugee">asylum seekers</a> and <a href="/wiki/Immigration" title="Immigration">migrants</a>.” <a class="external text" href="http://www.vox.com/2016/3/23/11291612/eu-greece-refugee-inhumane" rel="nofollow">(Vox Media)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://neurope.eu/article/unhcr-msf-withdraw-hotspots-calling-prisons/" rel="nofollow">(<i>New Europe</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Passengers are evacuated from the south domestic terminal at <a href="/wiki/Hartsfield%E2%80%93Jackson_Atlanta_International_Airport" title="Hartsfield–Jackson Atlanta International Airport">Hartsfield–Jackson Atlanta International Airport</a> in the U.S. state of <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(U.S._state)" title="Georgia (U.S. state)">Georgia</a> after a suspicious package is found. The package is declared safe by a bomb squad. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news24.com/news24/World/News/suspicious-package-at-atlanta-airport-cleared-20160323" rel="nofollow">(AP via News24)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">Supreme Court of the United States</a>, which currently has just <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States#Current_justices" title="Supreme Court of the United States">eight justices</a>, today heard the case brought by the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Pittsburgh" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Pittsburgh">Roman Catholic Diocese of Pittsburgh</a> (<i>Zubik v. Burwell</i>, which includes similar ones by other religious organizations) that challenges the <a href="/wiki/Patient_Protection_and_Affordable_Care_Act" title="Patient Protection and Affordable Care Act">Patient Protection and Affordable Care Act</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Contraceptive_mandate_(United_States)" title="Contraceptive mandate (United States)">provision</a> that employer-paid <a href="/wiki/Health_insurance_in_the_United_States" title="Health insurance in the United States">health insurance plans</a> provide women with access to <a href="/wiki/Birth_control" title="Birth control">contraceptives</a> at no additional out-of-pocket cost, and challenges the federal government accommodation offered in 2014 that would have a third-party provide the coverage with costs paid by the federal government. The plaintiffs state that both are unconstitutional because they violate the <a href="/wiki/Free_Exercise_Clause" title="Free Exercise Clause">free exercise of religion</a>. The decision is expected in June. If the result is a split decision (4-4), there would be no national precedent and <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States#Decision" title="Supreme Court of the United States">each case's final decision would be the one made in court before the case was forwarded to the Supreme Court</a>. In the group of cases presented today, all but one appeals court upheld the government mandate. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-usa-court-contraception-idUSKCN0WP0A9" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/news/politics/2016/03/23/supreme-court-little-sisters-religious-freedom-contraceptive-mandate/82135678/" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.npr.org/sections/health-shots/2016/03/23/471599946/supreme-court-takes-up-birth-control-access-yet-again" rel="nofollow">(NPR)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nigerien_general_election,_2016" title="Nigerien general election, 2016">Nigerien general election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_Niger" title="List of heads of state of Niger">Nigerien President</a> <a href="/wiki/Mahamadou_Issoufou" title="Mahamadou Issoufou">Mahamadou Issoufou</a> wins re-election in a second round of voting, receiving 92 percent of the vote in an election that was boycotted by the opposition. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2016/03/niger-president-issoufou-scores-landslide-election-win-160323053403939.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Al Jazeera</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Senegalese_constitutional_referendum,_2016" title="Senegalese constitutional referendum, 2016">Senegalese constitutional referendum, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/Senegal" title="Senegal">Senegal</a> approve a series of constitutional reforms, which include a reduction of presidential terms from seven to five years, with 63 percent of the vote. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-africa-35885465" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2016" title="United States presidential election, 2016">United States presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Tuesday, March 22 primaries/caucuses
<ul>
<li>Front runners <a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> and <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> each won the Democratic and Republican primary in <a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election_in_Arizona,_2016" title="United States presidential election in Arizona, 2016">Arizona</a>, respectively. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/election-us-2016-35869785" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bernie_Sanders" title="Bernie Sanders">Bernie Sanders</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ted_Cruz" title="Ted Cruz">Ted Cruz</a> each won their party's votes in <a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election_in_Idaho,_2016" title="United States presidential election in Idaho, 2016">Idaho</a> and <a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election_in_Utah,_2016" title="United States presidential election in Utah, 2016">Utah</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/election-us-2016-35869785" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>The early results for Tuesday's GOP caucus in <a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election_in_American_Samoa,_2016" title="United States presidential election in American Samoa, 2016">American Samoa</a> -- nine uncommitted. The <a href="/wiki/American_Samoa_Democratic_caucus,_2016" title="American Samoa Democratic caucus, 2016">Democratic caucus</a> was held on March 1, 2016, with Hillary Clinton getting eight delegates and Bernie Sanders three. <a class="external text" href="https://caffeinatedthoughts.com/2016/03/four-takeaways-gop-western-tuesday-arizona-utah/" rel="nofollow">(caffeinatedthoughts.com)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.thegreenpapers.com/P16/AS-D" rel="nofollow">(The Green Papers)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_24&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_24&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_24&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
