<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Starboard Value LP, an activist <a href="/wiki/Hedge_fund" title="Hedge fund">hedge fund</a>, begins a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Proxy_contest" title="Proxy contest">proxy contest</a> to oust the entire <a href="/wiki/Board_of_directors" title="Board of directors">board of directors</a> of internet pioneer <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yahoo" title="Yahoo">Yahoo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-yahoo-starboard-proxy-idUSKCN0WQ0D7" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanese</a> daily newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/As-Safir" title="As-Safir">As-Safir</a></i> ("The Ambassador" in Arabic) is to cease print and online operations after over 40 years, citing falling revenues and Lebanon's political environment and sectarian problems as reasons for its closure. The newspaper has close ties to <a href="/wiki/Hezbollah" title="Hezbollah">Hezbollah</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/lebanon-newspapers-idUSL5N16O36I" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Malaysia_Airlines_Flight_370" title="Malaysia Airlines Flight 370">Malaysia Airlines Flight 370</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australian</a> infrastructure and transport minister <a href="/wiki/Darren_Chester" title="Darren Chester">Darren Chester</a> says in a statement that debris recovered this month in <a href="/wiki/Mozambique" title="Mozambique">Mozambique</a> was highly likely to be from the missing <a href="/wiki/Malaysia_Airlines" title="Malaysia Airlines">Malaysia Airlines</a> flight. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-malaysia-airlines-idUSKCN0WQ041" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England international footballer</a> <a href="/wiki/Adam_Johnson_(footballer)" title="Adam Johnson (footballer)">Adam Johnson</a> is sentenced to six years in prison for child grooming and child sexual activity. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-35891143" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Judges at the <a href="/wiki/International_Criminal_Tribunal_for_the_former_Yugoslavia" title="International Criminal Tribunal for the former Yugoslavia">International Criminal Tribunal for the former Yugoslavia</a> find former President of the <a href="/wiki/Republika_Srpska" title="Republika Srpska">Republika Srpska</a> <a href="/wiki/Radovan_Karad%C5%BEi%C4%87" title="Radovan Karadžić">Radovan Karadžić</a> guilty of committing genocide and crimes against humanity in <a href="/wiki/Bosnia_and_Herzegovina" title="Bosnia and Herzegovina">Bosnia</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Bosnian_War" title="Bosnian War">Bosnian War</a> and is sentenced to 40 years in prison. Karadžić is found to be "criminally responsible" for the <a href="/wiki/Srebrenica_massacre" title="Srebrenica massacre">Srebrenica massacre</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/bosnian-serb-leader-karadzic-faces-hague-courts-verdict/27632392.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/24/radovan-karadzic-criminally-responsible-for-genocide-at-srebenica" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>In Toronto, <a href="/wiki/Jian_Ghomeshi" title="Jian Ghomeshi">Jian Ghomeshi</a> is acquitted on all charges of sexual assault and choking. The judge found the claimants had "lied, had been manipulative and hid pertinent information" from the court and this created reasonable doubt. Protests against <a href="/wiki/Due_process" title="Due process">due process</a> emerged immediately afterwards. <a class="external text" href="http://news.nationalpost.com/toronto/jian-ghomeshi-ruling" rel="nofollow">(National Post)</a></li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/New_York" title="New York">New York</a>, an appeals court upheld a lower court's decision to dismiss a lawsuit trying to keep <a href="/wiki/Ted_Cruz" title="Ted Cruz">Ted Cruz</a> off the ballot in the U.S. Presidential contest on the ground of his Canadian birth. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-usa-election-cruz-citizenship-idUSKCN0WQ27D" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Myanmar_general_election,_2015" title="Myanmar general election, 2015">Myanmar general election, 2015</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Myanmar" title="Myanmar">Myanmar</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Assembly_of_the_Union" title="Assembly of the Union">parliament</a> approves <a href="/wiki/List_of_Nobel_Peace_Prize_laureates" title="List of Nobel Peace Prize laureates">Nobel Peace Prize laureate</a> <a href="/wiki/Aung_San_Suu_Kyi" title="Aung San Suu Kyi">Aung San Suu Kyi</a> and 17 other nominees to positions in the incoming government's <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Myanmar#Members_of_the_Myanmar_Cabinet" title="Politics of Myanmar">cabinet</a>. Which ministry each will head was not announced. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-24/myanmar-s-parliament-approves-suu-kyi-for-cabinet-position" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Amnesty_International" title="Amnesty International">Amnesty International</a> urges Suu Kyi and her <a href="/wiki/National_League_for_Democracy" title="National League for Democracy">National League for Democracy</a> party make release of <a href="/wiki/Political_prisoner" title="Political prisoner">political prisoners</a>, and rescinding laws that made incarceration possible, a top priority when they take office next Friday, April 1, 2016. Amnesty International adds it knows of almost 100 political prisoners still behind bars, with hundreds of others in detention. AI's Jasmine Heiss says, "The incoming government must take bold steps to show that human rights abuses are a problem of the past.” <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/asia_pacific/amnesty-to-suu-kyi-government-break-cycle-of-repression/2016/03/24/33f6bdfe-f181-11e5-a2a3-d4e9697917d1_story.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/news/world/2016/03/24/myanmar-amnesty-international-report-political-prisoners/82171192/" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Tday</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.amnestyusa.org/news/press-releases/new-government-in-myanmar-must-break-vicious-cycle-of-repression-and-political-arrests" rel="nofollow">(Amnesty International)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_flag_debate" title="New Zealand flag debate">New Zealand flag debate</a>
<ul>
<li>New Zealanders vote to retain the <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_New_Zealand" title="Flag of New Zealand">current flag</a> over the <a href="/wiki/Lockwood_silver_fern_flag" title="Lockwood silver fern flag">proposed design</a> in the nation's <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand_flag_referendums,_2015%E2%80%9316" title="New Zealand flag referendums, 2015–16">flag referendum</a>. More than 2 million people vote in the referendum. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/nz/news/article.cfm?c_id=1&amp;objectid=11611333" rel="nofollow">(<i>NZ Herald</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.radionz.co.nz/news/national/299860/nz-flag-results-current-flag-to-stay" rel="nofollow">(Radio New Zealand)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/24/new-zealand-votes-to-keep-its-flag-in-referendum" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republic_of_the_Congo_presidential_election,_2016" title="Republic of the Congo presidential election, 2016">Republic of the Congo presidential election, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Current <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_the_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="List of heads of state of the Republic of the Congo">President</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Republic of the Congo">Republic of the Congo</a> <a href="/wiki/Denis_Sassou_Nguesso" title="Denis Sassou Nguesso">Denis Sassou Nguesso</a> is reelected with 60 percent of the vote amid tight security and a communications blackout. Opposition leaders say that they will not accept the outcome. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2016/03/congo-president-denis-sassou-nguesso-wins-election-160324040212900.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Al Jazeera</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Dutch</a> iconic professional footballer and manager <a href="/wiki/Johan_Cruyff" title="Johan Cruyff">Johan Cruyff</a> dies from lung cancer at the age of 68. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2016/03/24/football/football-johan-cruyff-death/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Six <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> athletes are to be stripped of the medals they won at <a href="/wiki/IAAF_World_Championships_in_Athletics" title="IAAF World Championships in Athletics">World</a> and <a href="/wiki/European_Athletics_Championships" title="European Athletics Championships">European championships</a> in <a href="/wiki/2010_European_Athletics_Championships" title="2010 European Athletics Championships">2010</a> and <a href="/wiki/2011_World_Championships_in_Athletics" title="2011 World Championships in Athletics">2011</a> and the <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics" title="2012 Summer Olympics">2012 Summer Olympics</a> following a ruling by the <a href="/wiki/Court_of_Arbitration_for_Sport" title="Court of Arbitration for Sport">Court of Arbitration for Sport</a>. The athletes affected are Sergei Balukin, <a href="/wiki/Valeriy_Borchin" title="Valeriy Borchin">Valeriy Borchin</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vladimir_Kanaikin" title="Vladimir Kanaikin">Vladimir Kanaikin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Olga_Kaniskina" title="Olga Kaniskina">Olga Kaniskina</a>, Yulia Zaripova and <a href="/wiki/Sergey_Kirdyapkin" title="Sergey Kirdyapkin">Sergey Kirdyapkin</a>. The ruling means Kirdyapkin is set to lose his gold medal won at the 2012 Olympics. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/russia-athletes-stripped-of-medals-2012-gold/27633205.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Aftermath of the <a href="/wiki/2016_Brussels_bombings" title="2016 Brussels bombings">2016 Brussels bombings</a>
<ul>
<li>Six suspects are arrested in the <a href="/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">Brussels</a> <a href="/wiki/Schaerbeek" title="Schaerbeek">Schaerbeek</a> district. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-35897417" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2016/03/25/europe/brussels-investigation/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgian</a> officials confirm 24-year-old suicide bomber Najim Laachraoui, who also used the pseudonym Soufiane Kayawas, was suspected of being the bomb-maker who supplied <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_vest" title="Suicide vest">suicide vests</a> for the <a href="/wiki/November_2015_Paris_attacks" title="November 2015 Paris attacks">November 13, 2015, Paris attacks</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/storyline/brussels-attacks/suspected-paris-bomb-maker-najim-laachraoui-was-brussels-attacker-n545521" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Boko_Haram_insurgency" title="Boko Haram insurgency">Boko Haram insurgency</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Nigerian_Army" title="Nigerian Army">Nigerian Army</a> claims to have rescued more than 800 hostages from <a href="/wiki/Boko_Haram" title="Boko Haram">Boko Haram</a> while performing a "clearance operation" in the Northeastern part of <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a> with fighting killing 22 insurgents. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2016/03/nigeria-army-800-boko-haram-hostages-rescued-160325061847145.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Al Jazeera</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Military_intervention_against_ISIL" title="Military intervention against ISIL">Military intervention against ISIL</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Pentagon" title="Pentagon">Pentagon</a> announces the death of <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a> finance minister and deputy leader, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Abu_Ala_al-Afri" title="Abu Ala al-Afri">Abu Ala al-Afri</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2016/03/25/politics/isis-no-2-in-command-killed-u-s-believes/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Palmyra_offensive_(March_2016)" title="Palmyra offensive (March 2016)">Palmyra offensive (March 2016)</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Army" title="Syrian Army">Syrian Army</a> and allies make major advances near <a href="/wiki/Palmyra" title="Palmyra">Palmyra</a> against ISIL as the group start pulling out its equipment from the town. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-35898995" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2016/03/26/world/middleeast/syrian-army-said-to-be-closer-to-retaking-palmyra.html?_r=0" rel="nofollow">(NYTimes)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iraqi_Civil_War_(2014%E2%80%93present)" title="Iraqi Civil War (2014–present)">Iraqi Civil War (2014–present)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Iskandariya_suicide_bombing" title="Iskandariya suicide bombing">Iskandariya suicide bombing</a>
<ul>
<li>At least 30 people are killed in a suicide attack on a football stadium south of <a href="/wiki/Baghdad" title="Baghdad">Baghdad</a>, <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a> claims responsibility for attack. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2016/03/25/suicide-blast-kills-29-at-iraq-football-stadium-isis-claims-responsibility.html" rel="nofollow">(FOX News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yemeni_Civil_War_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Yemeni Civil War (2015–present)">Yemeni Civil War (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Aden_car_bombing" title="2016 Aden car bombing">2016 Aden car bombing</a>
<ul>
<li>At least 22 people are killed following three suicide bombings in the <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemeni</a> port city of <a href="/wiki/Aden" title="Aden">Aden</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a> claims responsibility for the bombings. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-middle-east-35901733" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_Donbass" title="War in Donbass">War in Donbass</a>
<ul>
<li>The body of <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukrainian</a> lawyer Yurij Grabovsky, who defended two ex-<a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> soldiers charged in <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Ukraine" title="Eastern Ukraine">Eastern Ukraine</a> with terrorism and waging an aggressive war against the country, is found on the grounds of a former farming collective in <a href="/wiki/Zhashkiv" title="Zhashkiv">Zhashkiv</a>, Ukraine. Grabovsky went missing from <a href="/wiki/Kiev" title="Kiev">Kiev</a> on March 9. Information from one of two men being held in this case led police to the remains. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-ukraine-crisis-lawyer-death-idUSKCN0WR0WF" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.jurist.org/paperchase/2016/03/ukraine-lawyer-for-russia-soldiers-found-dead.php" rel="nofollow">(Jurist)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Callaway_train_crash" title="Callaway train crash">Callaway train crash</a>
<ul>
<li>The evacuation order for the 200-person town of <a href="/wiki/Callaway,_Minnesota" title="Callaway, Minnesota">Callaway</a>, <a href="/wiki/Minnesota" title="Minnesota">Minnesota</a>, which was emptied after a <a href="/wiki/Canadian_Pacific_Railway" title="Canadian Pacific Railway">Canadian Pacific</a> train crashed with a propane truck, is lifted. None of the <a href="/wiki/Railroad_car" title="Railroad car">train cars</a> were carrying hazardous materials. <a class="external text" href="http://www.valleynewslive.com/home/headlines/Train-crash-with-propane-truck-closes-Highway-59--373392491.html?device=phone&amp;c=y" rel="nofollow">(Valley News Live)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.fox9.com/news/113247655-story" rel="nofollow">(KMSP-TV)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Twelve <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_people" title="Portuguese people">Portuguese nationals</a>, who were residents of <a href="/wiki/Fribourg" title="Fribourg">Fribourg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a>, are killed in a head-on collision between their <a href="/wiki/Minibus" title="Minibus">minibus</a> and a truck, on a highway 300 kilometers (185 miles) south of <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a>, <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>. The only survivor from the bus is the driver; the two <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italian</a> occupants of the truck are slightly injured. <a class="external text" href="http://www.postbulletin.com/news/world/portuguese-killed-in-bus-crash-in-central-france/article_580da7d2-b2d2-5806-b967-3c4b63e8da87.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Post-Bulletin</i>)</a></li>
<li>An <a href="/wiki/Air_medical_services" title="Air medical services">air ambulance</a> helicopter crashes in <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a>'s southern <a href="/wiki/Fars_Province" title="Fars Province">Fars Province</a>, killing everyone on board. The official <a href="/wiki/Islamic_Republic_News_Agency" title="Islamic Republic News Agency">Islamic Republic News Agency</a> (IRNA) put the death toll at 10. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-iran-helicopter-crash-idUSKCN0WR1GE" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan%E2%80%93Russia_relations" title="Japan–Russia relations">Japan–Russia relations</a>, <a href="/wiki/NATO%E2%80%93Russia_relations" title="NATO–Russia relations">NATO–Russia relations</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> announces it will deploy state-of-the art missile defense systems to the far eastern <a href="/wiki/Kuril_Islands" title="Kuril Islands">Kuril Islands</a> where they and <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> have <a href="/wiki/Kuril_Islands_dispute" title="Kuril Islands dispute">rival territorial claims</a> dating to the end of the <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">Second World War</a>. Russian <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Defence_(Russia)" title="Ministry of Defence (Russia)">Defence Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Sergey_Shoygu" title="Sergey Shoygu">Sergey Shoygu</a> also says that Russia will form new defence units in the country's <a href="/wiki/Western_Military_District" title="Western Military District">Western Military District</a> in response to <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO's</a> recent deployment of forces to <a href="/wiki/Member_states_of_NATO" title="Member states of NATO">member states</a> near its border. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/russia-new-weapons-west-pacific/27635405.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/United_States_district_court" title="United States district court">United States federal district judge</a> rules unconstitutional a provision in an <a href="/wiki/Alabama" title="Alabama">Alabama</a> state law that requires doctors who perform abortions to have admitting privileges at a local hospital. A <a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">Florida</a> law enacted today contains a comparable provision to Alabama's. The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">U.S. Supreme Court</a> heard arguments a few weeks ago on the constitutionality of similar abortion restrictions in <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-alabama-abortion-idUSKCN0WR1IL" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.al.com/news/index.ssf/2016/03/judge_strips_admitting_privile.html" rel="nofollow">(Alabama Media Group)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.heraldcourier.com/news/judge-rules-state-abortion-restriction-unconstitutional/article_ae9f3c15-ae31-5a0a-babd-9e6701f31bae.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Bristol Herald Courier</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Netflix" title="Netflix">Netflix</a> acknowledges it's been slowing its video transmission on <a href="/wiki/Mobile_network_operator" title="Mobile network operator">wireless mobile carriers</a> around the world, including <a href="/wiki/Verizon_Wireless" title="Verizon Wireless">Verizon</a> and <a href="/wiki/AT%26T_Mobility" title="AT&amp;T Mobility">AT&amp;T</a>, for five years to "protect consumers from exceeding mobile data caps." Last week, these carriers were accused of this. The company told <i><a href="/wiki/The_Wall_Street_Journal" title="The Wall Street Journal">The Wall Street Journal</a></i> that <a href="/wiki/T-Mobile_US" title="T-Mobile US">T-Mobile</a> or <a href="/wiki/Sprint_Corporation" title="Sprint Corporation">Sprint</a> users weren't affected because, "historically those two companies have had more consumer-friendly policies." In May, Netflix plans to shift some of that control to viewers themselves. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnet.com/news/netflix-admits-throttling-video-speeds-on-at-t-verizon/" rel="nofollow">(C|net)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.pcmag.com/news/343220/netflix-throttling-video-streams-for-most-mobile-users" rel="nofollow">(<i>PC Magazine</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_26&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_26&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Palmyra_offensive_(March_2016)" title="Palmyra offensive (March 2016)">Palmyra offensive (March 2016)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Army" title="Syrian Army">Syrian troops</a> advance into <a href="/wiki/Palmyra" title="Palmyra">Palmyra</a> on multiple fronts with the help of <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> airstrikes and take several neighbourhoods, according to the <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Observatory_for_Human_Rights" title="Syrian Observatory for Human Rights">Syrian Observatory for Human Rights</a>. However they were unable to encircle the city. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-35903375" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> rock band <a href="/wiki/The_Rolling_Stones" title="The Rolling Stones">The Rolling Stones</a> performs in <a href="/wiki/Havana" title="Havana">Havana</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>, playing an open-air free concert in the country, in what has been called a "historic moment." Western music used to be banned in Cuba as being "ideologically divergent." <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/music/2016/mar/26/rolling-stones-enjoy-historic-cuba-gig-havana-obama" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tribeca_Film_Festival" title="Tribeca Film Festival">Tribeca Film Festival</a> co-founder <a href="/wiki/Robert_De_Niro" title="Robert De Niro">Robert De Niro</a> announces the film, <i><a href="/wiki/Vaxxed" title="Vaxxed">Vaxxed: From Cover-Up to Catastrophe</a></i>, will not be screened at the 2016 Festival as previously announced. “<a href="/wiki/Grace_Hightower" title="Grace Hightower">Grace [Hightower]</a> and I have a child with <a href="/wiki/Autism" title="Autism">autism</a> and we believe it is critical that all of the issues surrounding the causes of autism be openly discussed and examined," Mr. De Niro said. "... (our) Tribeca Film Festival team and others from the scientific community ... do not believe (this film) contributes to or furthers the discussion (about autism) I hoped for," the actor/producer said. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/life/movies/2016/03/26/festival-robert-de-niro-pull-anti-vaccination-film/82311576/" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>British newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/The_Independent" title="The Independent">The Independent</a></i> publishes its last print edition. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/story/1667395/independent-newspaper-prints-final-edition" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Reuters" title="Reuters">Reuters</a> reports, based on an unnamed "person familiar with the situation," that <a href="/wiki/Microsoft" title="Microsoft">Microsoft</a> executives are lining up financing for a possible acquisition of troubled dotcom pioneer <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yahoo" title="Yahoo">Yahoo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-microsoft-yahoo-idUSKCN0WS067" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>All four on board are killed when a <a href="/wiki/Air_medical_services" title="Air medical services">medical services helicopter</a>, transporting a patient from a car accident, crashes in a wooded area in <a href="/wiki/Coffee_County,_Alabama" title="Coffee County, Alabama">Coffee County, Alabama</a>. The helicopter pilot, a nurse, a medic, and the patient were killed. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-alabama-helicopter-idUSKCN0WT04J" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Health and medicine</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zika_virus_outbreak_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Zika virus outbreak (2015–present)">Zika virus outbreak</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a> confirms its first case of <a href="/wiki/Sexually_transmitted_infection" title="Sexually transmitted infection">sexually transmitted</a> <a href="/wiki/Zika_virus" title="Zika virus">Zika virus</a>. The case involves a 46-year-old woman whose partner was infected while in <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-zika-chile-idUSKCN0WT00Q" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Centers_for_Disease_Control_and_Prevention" title="Centers for Disease Control and Prevention">U.S. Centers for Disease Control and Prevention</a> advises women exposed to Zika, which means traveling to <a href="/wiki/South_America" title="South America">South American</a> (or other) countries where the disease is rampant, have <a href="/wiki/Safe_sex" title="Safe sex">protected sex</a> for at least two months before attempting to get <a href="/wiki/Pregnancy" title="Pregnancy">pregnant</a>. Men exposed should not have unprotected sex for at least six months. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Health_News/2016/03/26/Women-shouldnt-attempt-conception-for-2-months-after-Zika-exposure-CDC/7911459026299/?spt=hs&amp;or=hn" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Flint_water_crisis" title="Flint water crisis">Flint water crisis</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Federal_Emergency_Management_Agency" title="Federal Emergency Management Agency">U.S. Federal Emergency Management Agency</a> extends the <a href="/wiki/Disaster_area" title="Disaster area">federal disaster declaration</a> for <a href="/wiki/Flint,_Michigan" title="Flint, Michigan">Flint</a>, <a href="/wiki/Michigan" title="Michigan">Michigan</a>, so water deliveries can continue through mid-August. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/US/2016/03/26/FEMA-extends-water-deliveries-in-Flint-Mich-through-August/4741459020200/?spt=hs&amp;or=tn_us" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A study, published in <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_American_Journal_of_Sports_Medicine" title="The American Journal of Sports Medicine">The American Journal of Sports Medicine</a></i>, finds <a href="/wiki/Amateur_sports" title="Amateur sports">high school athletes</a> who focus on a single sport may be at increased risk for <a href="/wiki/Knee" title="Knee">knee</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hip" title="Hip">hip</a> injuries. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Health_News/2016/03/26/Injuries-More-Common-in-Teens-Who-Focus-on-Single-Sport/8341458998305/?spt=rln&amp;or=3" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> <a href="/wiki/Chairman_of_the_Joint_Chiefs_of_Staff" title="Chairman of the Joint Chiefs of Staff">Chairman of the Joint Chiefs of Staff</a> <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Dunford" title="Joseph Dunford">Joseph Dunford</a> makes a proposal to <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> to increase the number of <a href="/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces" title="United States Armed Forces">American troops</a> in <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>, so as to help the <a href="/wiki/Iraqi_Army" title="Iraqi Army">Iraqi Army</a> with advisors closer to the front lines and to recapture <a href="/wiki/Mosul" title="Mosul">Mosul</a>, which fell to <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a> in June 2014. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/pentagon-proposing-add-more-us-troops-iraq/27636550.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2016" title="United States presidential election, 2016">United States presidential election, 2016</a>, <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_presidential_primaries,_2016" title="Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2016">Democratic Party presidential primaries, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li>Voters in the U.S. states of <a href="/wiki/Alaska_Democratic_caucuses,_2016" title="Alaska Democratic caucuses, 2016">Alaska</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hawaii_Democratic_caucuses,_2016" title="Hawaii Democratic caucuses, 2016">Hawaii</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Washington_Democratic_caucuses,_2016" title="Washington Democratic caucuses, 2016">Washington</a> gather for Democratic Party caucuses. <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtontimes.com/news/2016/mar/26/bernie-sanders-seeks-caucus-trifecta-win-close-del/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Washington Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bernie_Sanders" title="Bernie Sanders">Senator Bernie Sanders</a> is the projected winner in Alaska, Washington and Hawaii. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usnews.com/news/us/articles/2016-03-26/the-latest-bustling-caucus-sites-in-washington-state" rel="nofollow">(<i>U.S. News &amp; World Report</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_27&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Palmyra_offensive_(March_2016)" title="Palmyra offensive (March 2016)">Palmyra offensive (March 2016)</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Army" title="Syrian Army">Syrian Army</a> takes full control of <a href="/wiki/Palmyra" title="Palmyra">Palmyra</a> after heavy fighting with <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a> forces, according to a Syrian military source. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/story/1667695/syrian-troops-retake-all-of-palmyra-from-is" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Lahore_suicide_bombing" title="2016 Lahore suicide bombing">2016 Lahore suicide bombing</a>
<ul>
<li>A suicide bomber from a <a href="/wiki/Jamaat-ul-Ahrar" title="Jamaat-ul-Ahrar">Pakistani Taliban</a> faction kills at least 60 people and injures 300 others at a park in <a href="/wiki/Lahore" title="Lahore">Lahore</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>, and the group claimed responsibility for the attack, saying it <a href="/wiki/Persecution_of_Christians#Pakistan" title="Persecution of Christians">intentionally targeted Christians</a> celebrating on Easter Sunday. An official says the explosion took place close to <a href="/wiki/Gulshan-e-Iqbal_Park" title="Gulshan-e-Iqbal Park">Gulshan-e-Iqbal Park's</a> children's rides. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/27/asia/pakistan-lahore-deadly-blast/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-pakistan-blast-idUSKCN0WT0HR" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2016/03/deadly-blast-hits-pakistan-lahore-160327143110195.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Al Jazeera</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/72e6954d7c1a4c259e2ab1ee5879d658/latest-bomb-blast-pakistan-park-kills-44-wounds-91" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Arts and culture</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Thousands of people in <a href="/wiki/Dublin" title="Dublin">Dublin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a>, attend the Irish government's commemoration of the 1916 <a href="/wiki/Easter_Rising" title="Easter Rising">Easter Rising</a> against <a href="/wiki/British_Empire" title="British Empire">British rule</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/27/easter-rising-centenary-to-be-marked-in-dublin-gpo-amid-heavy-security" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>At least 12 <a href="/wiki/People%27s_National_Army_(Algeria)" title="People's National Army (Algeria)">Algerian Army</a> soldiers are killed in a military helicopter crash near the town of <a href="/wiki/Reggane" title="Reggane">Reggane</a>, in <a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a>'s southern <a href="/wiki/Adrar_Province" title="Adrar Province">Adrar Province</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-algeria-crash-idUSKCN0WT0RJ" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Israel" title="Supreme Court of Israel">Israel's Supreme Court</a> blocks the government's plan, signed last December by <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel" title="Prime Minister of Israel">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu" title="Benjamin Netanyahu">Benjamin Netanyahu</a> with the U.S. <a href="/wiki/Noble_Energy" title="Noble Energy">Noble Energy</a> and the Israeli <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Delek_Group" title="Delek Group">Delek Group</a> companies, to develop <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel's</a> <a href="/wiki/Natural_gas_field" title="Natural gas field">offshore gas deposits</a>. The court found the so-called "stability clause," that would prevent Israel from making significant regulatory changes for the next 10 years, undemocratically restricts the <a href="/wiki/Knesset" title="Knesset">Knesset's</a> power. The government has one year to come up with an alternative arrangement or the plan will be canceled. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/518f246087d34784956bd01c77010dbc/israels-supreme-court-shoots-down-gas-deal" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.ynetnews.com/articles/0,7340,L-4783787,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Ynetnews)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-israel-natgas-court-idUSKCN0WT0J6" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Myanmar_general_election,_2015" title="Myanmar general election, 2015">Myanmar general election, 2015</a>
<ul>
<li>Senior General <a href="/wiki/Min_Aung_Hlaing" title="Min Aung Hlaing">Min Aung Hlaing</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tatmadaw" title="Tatmadaw">Myanmar's military</a> chief, pledges to work with the new civilian government that takes over the <a href="/wiki/Southeast_Asia" title="Southeast Asia">Southeast Asian</a> country next week, after 54 years of direct or indirect rule by the military. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/5a282a96ec7a4a05950583e3f17cc611/myanmars-military-vows-join-hands-civilian-leaders" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9316_Venezuelan_protests" title="2014–16 Venezuelan protests">2014–16 Venezuelan protests</a>
<ul>
<li>According to a new poll, two-thirds of <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuelans</a> think <a href="/wiki/President_of_Venezuela" title="President of Venezuela">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Nicol%C3%A1s_Maduro" title="Nicolás Maduro">Nicolás Maduro</a> should end his presidency this year or be removed via a recall referendum amid a worsening <a href="/wiki/Economic_policy_of_the_Nicol%C3%A1s_Maduro_government" title="Economic policy of the Nicolás Maduro government">economic crisis</a>. In the event of a referendum, 52.1 percent of Venezuelans would vote to remove him from office, up from 44.5 percent in January, according to the poll. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-venezuela-politic*s-idUSKCN0WS0JO" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_protests_in_Moldova" title="2015–16 protests in Moldova">2015–16 protests in Moldova</a>
<ul>
<li>Thousands of people rally in the streets of <a href="/wiki/Chi%C8%99in%C4%83u" title="Chișinău">Chișinău</a>, the capital of <a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">Moldova</a>, demanding <a href="/wiki/Unification_of_Romania_and_Moldova" title="Unification of Romania and Moldova">reunification</a> with <a href="/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a>. The rally is meant to mark the 98th anniversary since the former Romanian province of <a href="/wiki/Bessarabia" title="Bessarabia">Bessarabia</a> was unified with the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Romania" title="Kingdom of Romania">Kingdom of Romania</a> on March 27, 1918. The protesters say unification with Romania is the way for corruption-ridden Moldova to move forward and join the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/moldova-rally-romania-unification/27638163.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Aftermath of the <a href="/wiki/2016_Brussels_bombings" title="2016 Brussels bombings">2016 Brussels bombings</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_in_Belgium" title="Law enforcement in Belgium">Police</a> in <a href="/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">Brussels</a>, <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a>, forcibly break up an apparent far-right demonstration with water cannons after they joined a crowd of people paying tribute to the victims of the bombings. The demonstrators claim to have marched against terrorism but police intervened when the demonstrators confronted Muslim women and made <a href="/wiki/Nazi_salute" title="Nazi salute">Nazi salutes</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.euronews.com/2016/03/27/brussels-police-use-water-cannon-against-far-right-demonstrators/" rel="nofollow">(Euronews)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-35907469" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
<div id="2016_March_28"></div>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> March 28, 2016<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2016-03-28</span>)</span> (Monday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_28&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_28&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_28&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Afghanistan (2015–present)">War in Afghanistan (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> fighters fire explosives at <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan's</a> <a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_(Afghanistan)" title="National Assembly (Afghanistan)">Parliament</a> while it is in session. Members of Parliament said no one was wounded while a Taliban spokesperson claims it caused heavy casualities. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2016/03/taliban-fires-explosives-afghanistan-parliament-compound-160328074227812.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Al Jazeera</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_Somalia_(2009%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Somalia (2009–present)">War in Somalia (2009–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>At least 115 <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">Al-Shabaab</a> militants are killed and a further 110 are captured following heavy fighting with pro-government forces in the <a href="/wiki/Galmudug" title="Galmudug">Galmudug region</a> of <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>, according to the regional government. There has been no independent confirmation of this claim. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-africa-35910675" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Brussels_bombings" title="2016 Brussels bombings">Aftermath of the Brussels bombings</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Federal_Government_of_Belgium" title="Federal Government of Belgium">Belgian prosecutors</a> release Faycal C., a man charged in connection with last week's deadly <a href="/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">Brussels</a> bombings. The prosecutor's office says the evidence which led to his arrest has not been backed up by the ongoing investigation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-belgium-blast-charges-idUSKCN0WU0M6" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Lahore_suicide_bombing" title="2016 Lahore suicide bombing">2016 Lahore suicide bombing</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> officials tell <a href="/wiki/Reuters" title="Reuters">Reuters</a> its forces will launch a <a href="/wiki/Paramilitary" title="Paramilitary">paramilitary</a> crackdown on <a href="/wiki/Islamism" title="Islamism">Islamist</a> militants in <a href="/wiki/Punjab_(region)" title="Punjab (region)">Punjab</a>. Sunday's attack was <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a>-affiliated <a href="/wiki/Jamaat-ul-Ahrar" title="Jamaat-ul-Ahrar">Jamaat-ul-Ahrar's</a> fifth bombing since December. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-pakistan-blast-idUSKCN0WT0HR" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>In response to the $13.6 billion cash-and-stock offer by the <a href="/wiki/Marriott_International" title="Marriott International">Marriott International</a> to purchase <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Starwood_Hotels_and_Resorts_Worldwide" title="Starwood Hotels and Resorts Worldwide">Starwood Hotels and Resorts Worldwide</a>, <a href="/wiki/Anbang_Insurance_Group" title="Anbang Insurance Group">Anbang Insurance Group</a> raises its bidding offer to $14 billion. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/6f8bc9df96724ddebae77b9623cfcc0e/starwood-receives-sweetened-15b-bid-anbang-led-group" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-starwood-m-a-anbang-idUSKCN0WU11V" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Business_News/2016/03/21/Starwood-agrees-to-increased-136B-merger-deal-with-Marriott/7721458570373/?spt=sec&amp;or=bn" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/business/capitalbusiness/marriott-gets-outbid--again--for-starwood-hotels/2016/03/28/496cb012-f4f1-11e5-8b23-538270a1ca31_story.html?hpid=hp_local-news_no-name%3Ahomepage%2Fstory" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UK_and_Ireland_windstorm_season" title="2015–16 UK and Ireland windstorm season">2015–16 UK and Ireland windstorm season</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Met_Office" title="Met Office">Met Office</a> warns of major travel disruption due to heavy rain, flooding and "damaging" high winds as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Storm_Katie" title="Storm Katie">Storm Katie</a> moves in from the <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">Atlantic Ocean</a> bringing winds of up to 75mph. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/story/1667780/storm-katie-threatens-easter-monday-misery" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Alaska" title="Alaska">Alaska</a> village of <a href="/wiki/Nelson_Lagoon,_Alaska" title="Nelson Lagoon, Alaska">Nelson Lagoon</a> is coated in <a href="/wiki/Tephra" title="Tephra">volcanic ash</a> after an especially vigorous and ongoing eruption of <a href="/wiki/Mount_Pavlof" title="Mount Pavlof">Mount Pavlof</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.adn.com/article/20160328/volcanic-eruption-covers-alaska-village-ash-launches-lava-sky" rel="nofollow">(Alaska Dispatch News)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Alaska_Airlines" title="Alaska Airlines">Alaska Airlines</a> cancels 41 flights to and from six cities across the state, <a href="/wiki/Barrow,_Alaska" title="Barrow, Alaska">Barrow</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bethel,_Alaska" title="Bethel, Alaska">Bethel</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fairbanks,_Alaska" title="Fairbanks, Alaska">Fairbanks</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kotzebue,_Alaska" title="Kotzebue, Alaska">Kotzebue</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nome,_Alaska" title="Nome, Alaska">Nome</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Prudhoe_Bay,_Alaska" title="Prudhoe Bay, Alaska">Prudhoe Bay</a>, due to Pavlof's "massive ash cloud." The carrier announces flights will remain grounded pending Tuesday's assessment of flying conditions. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ktuu.com/news/news/pavlof-eruption-alaska-village-covered-in-ash-20-flights-cancelled/38732402" rel="nofollow">(KTUU-TV)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International Relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Senkaku_Islands_dispute" title="Senkaku Islands dispute">Senkaku Islands dispute</a>, <a href="/wiki/China%E2%80%93Japan_relations" title="China–Japan relations">China–Japan relations</a>
<ul>
<li>As part of its wider <a href="/wiki/Japan_Self-Defense_Forces" title="Japan Self-Defense Forces">military</a> build up along the <a href="/wiki/Japanese_archipelago" title="Japanese archipelago">Japanese archipelagos</a> in the <a href="/wiki/East_China_Sea" title="East China Sea">East China Sea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> activates a new radar station on the <a href="/wiki/Yonaguni" title="Yonaguni">island of Yonaguni</a> that is close to the <a href="/wiki/Senkaku_Islands_dispute" title="Senkaku Islands dispute">disputed Senkaku Islands</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-japan-china-eastchinasea-idUSKCN0WT0QZ" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabian-led_intervention_in_Yemen" title="Saudi Arabian-led intervention in Yemen">Saudi Arabian-led intervention in Yemen</a>
<ul>
<li>A Saudi coalition says it's traded 109 <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemeni</a> prisoners for nine captive <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/4e356e6451154410b8a3fb5e17cac388/saudi-arabia-says-109-yemenis-traded-9-saudis-amid-war" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A three-year-old girl is decapitated in an apparently random killing by a man with a <a href="/wiki/Cleaver" title="Cleaver">cleaver</a> in <a href="/wiki/Taipei" title="Taipei">Taipei</a>, <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>. The man was arrested shortly afterwards. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/28/three-year-old-girl-decapitated-by-man-with-cleaver-taipei-taiwan" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Capitol" title="United States Capitol">United States Capitol</a> in <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a> is on lockdown following reports of shots fired at the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Capitol_Visitor_Center" title="United States Capitol Visitor Center">Capitol Visitor Center</a>. The <a href="/wiki/White_House" title="White House">White House</a>, in what appears to be an unrelated incident, was briefly locked down this afternoon. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/28/politics/u-s-capitol-and-white-house-on-lockdown/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a>
<ul>
<li>Police lift the lockdown. An armed man was shot by police, is in police custody, and is undergoing surgery at <a href="/wiki/MedStar_Washington_Hospital_Center" title="MedStar Washington Hospital Center">MedStar Washington Hospital Center</a>. A female bystander suffers what appears to be a minor injury. <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/local/public-safety/gunshots-reported-at-us-capitol-complex/2016/03/28/f1b961ba-f515-11e5-8b23-538270a1ca31_story.html?hpid=hp_rhp-top-table-main_no-name%3Ahomepage%2Fstory" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/FBI%E2%80%93Apple_encryption_dispute" title="FBI–Apple encryption dispute">FBI–Apple encryption dispute</a>
<ul>
<li>Federal prosecutors announce the case against <a href="/wiki/Apple_Inc." title="Apple Inc.">Apple Inc.</a>, concerning <a href="/wiki/Encryption" title="Encryption">encrypted</a> data on an <a href="/wiki/IPhone" title="IPhone">iPhone</a> belonging to one of the <a href="/wiki/2015_San_Bernardino_attack" title="2015 San Bernardino attack">San Bernardino</a> <a href="/wiki/2015_San_Bernardino_attack#Perpetrators" title="2015 San Bernardino attack">shooters</a>, has been dropped since the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation" title="Federal Bureau of Investigation">FBI</a> has found a means to access the data without com­prom­ising any in­form­a­tion on the phone. <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/local/lanow/la-me-ln-fbi-drops-fight-to-force-apple-to-unlock-san-bernardino-terrorist-iphone-20160328-story.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://documents.latimes.com/government-no-longer-requires-apples-help-iphone-case/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Los Angeles Times</i>²)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/United_States_District_Court_for_the_District_of_Puerto_Rico" title="United States District Court for the District of Puerto Rico">U.S. federal district court</a>, in a case filed by retailer <a href="/wiki/Walmart" title="Walmart">Wal-Mart Stores. Inc.</a>, strikes down a <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rican</a> tax increase for on-island companies, with more than $2.75 billion in revenues that buy goods from off-island "related parties," because the levy clearly discriminates against <a href="/wiki/Commerce_Clause" title="Commerce Clause">interstate commerce</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/wal-mart-puertorico-idUSL2N1701MV" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secret_Service" title="United States Secret Service">United States Secret Service</a> says only <a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_officer" title="Law enforcement officer">law enforcement officers</a> will be allowed to have <a href="/wiki/Gun" title="Gun">guns</a> inside the <a href="/wiki/2016_Republican_National_Convention" title="2016 Republican National Convention">Republican National Convention</a> to be held in the <a href="/wiki/Cleveland" title="Cleveland">Cleveland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ohio" title="Ohio">Ohio</a>, arena on July 18–21, 2016; responding to an online petition demanding <a href="/wiki/Quicken_Loans_Arena" title="Quicken Loans Arena">Quicken Loans Arena</a> revoke its ban on open carrying of <a href="/wiki/Firearm" title="Firearm">firearms</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/news/politics/onpolitics/2016/03/28/secret-service-no-gunsrepublican-convention/82348324/" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/American_Civil_Liberties_Union" title="American Civil Liberties Union">American Civil Liberties Union</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lambda_Legal" title="Lambda Legal">Lambda Legal</a> file a federal lawsuit against a new <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">North Carolina</a> law that bars <a href="/wiki/Transgender" title="Transgender">transgender people</a> from choosing bathrooms consistent with their <a href="/wiki/Gender_identity" title="Gender identity">gender identity</a>, arguing the measure is discriminatory and threatens individuals' personal safety. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-north-carolina-transgender-idUSKCN0WU15H" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ferguson_unrest" title="Ferguson unrest">Ferguson unrest</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Missouri_Circuit_Courts" title="Missouri Circuit Courts">Missouri court</a> strikes down parts of a law, meant to address concerns raised after the police <a href="/wiki/Shooting_of_Michael_Brown" title="Shooting of Michael Brown">shooting of Michael Brown</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ferguson,_Missouri" title="Ferguson, Missouri">Ferguson, Missouri</a>, that limit cities' ability to profit from <a href="/wiki/Traffic_ticket" title="Traffic ticket">traffic tickets</a> and <a href="/wiki/Court_costs" title="Court costs">court fines</a>. The judge wrote the law unconstitutionally targeted <a href="/wiki/Greater_St._Louis" title="Greater St. Louis">St. Louis-area municipalities</a> with caps on revenues from traffic fines that were lower than other cities in the state. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/0d3eb4e5ca934c8ba6c6370ef598f2a1/court-strikes-down-law-passed-after-doj-report-ferguson" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Thousands of protestors rally in front of the <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Pakistan" title="Parliament of Pakistan">Parliament</a> of <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> in <a href="/wiki/Islamabad" title="Islamabad">Islamabad</a> in support of <a href="/wiki/Mumtaz_Qadri" title="Mumtaz Qadri">Mumtaz Qadri</a>, the killer of reformist <a href="/wiki/Punjab,_Pakistan" title="Punjab, Pakistan">Punjab</a> governor <a href="/wiki/Salmaan_Taseer" title="Salmaan Taseer">Salmaan Taseer</a> in 2011 who was subsequently executed last February. The <a href="/wiki/Pakistan_Army" title="Pakistan Army">Pakistan Army</a> was called in to control the situation. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-asia-35909716" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2016/03/pro-blasphemy-protesters-clash-police-pakistan-160327142503305.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Al Jazeera</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_Governors_of_Georgia" title="List of Governors of Georgia">Governor</a> <a href="/wiki/Nathan_Deal" title="Nathan Deal">Nathan Deal</a>, of the American state of <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(U.S._state)" title="Georgia (U.S. state)">Georgia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Veto" title="Veto">vetoes</a> a religious liberties bill that would have protected people whose religious beliefs don't include <a href="/wiki/Same-sex_marriage" title="Same-sex marriage">same-sex marriage</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://politics.blog.ajc.com/2016/03/28/breaking-nathan-deal-will-veto-georgias-religious-liberty-bill/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Atlanta Journal-Constitution</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/post-nation/wp/2016/03/28/georgia-governor-to-veto-religious-freedom-bill-criticized-as-anti-gay/?hpid=hp_rhp-top-table-main_georgia-1045am%3Ahomepage%2Fstory" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://espn.go.com/nfl/story/_/id/15082904/georgia-gov-nathan-deal-veto-house-bill-757-aiding-atlanta-falcons-super-bowl-hopes" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Governor_of_New_York" title="Governor of New York">New York Governor</a> <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Cuomo" title="Andrew Cuomo">Andrew Cuomo</a> signs an order banning all non-essential travel to <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">North Carolina</a>, i.e., travel not necessary for the enforcement of New York state law, public health, and/or safety, following the state's passage of a law blocking local governments from passing anti-discrimination ordinances. <a class="external text" href="http://newyork.cbslocal.com/2016/03/28/cuomo-north-carolina-travel/" rel="nofollow">(CBS News)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed attacks and conflicts</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Brussels_bombings" title="2016 Brussels bombings">2016 Brussels bombings</a>
<ul>
<li>Belgium officials lower the official death toll from 35 to 32, with nearly 100 still hospitalized. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2016/03/29/Brussels-May-take-weeks-for-airport-to-fully-reopen-death-toll-lowered-to-32/8081459256059/?spt=hs&amp;or=tn_int" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">Brussels</a> <a href="/wiki/Brussels_Airport" title="Brussels Airport">Zaventem International Airport</a> CEO Arnaud Feist says the airport will reopen at less than a quarter capacity Wednesday, as ongoing tests determine which flights can resume. It could take months for the airport to return to full capacity, Feist added. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2016/03/29/Brussels-May-take-weeks-for-airport-to-fully-reopen-death-toll-lowered-to-32/8081459256059/?spt=hs&amp;or=tn_int" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>

<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">U.S. Supreme Court's</a> even split among the current eight justices turns down a group of California teachers' challenge to <a href="/wiki/Agency_shop" title="Agency shop">agency fees</a> <a href="/wiki/Public-sector_trade_union" title="Public-sector trade union">public sector unions</a> representing government employees charge employees for <a href="/wiki/Collective_bargaining" title="Collective bargaining">collective bargaining</a> costs, whether or not they choose to join the union. Twenty-four other states and the District of Columbia have a similar provision. The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Court_of_Appeals_for_the_Ninth_Circuit" title="United States Court of Appeals for the Ninth Circuit">ninth circuit federal appellate court ruling</a> in the union’s favor stands. Employees challenging the law may bring the appeal again, once the <a href="/wiki/Appointment_and_confirmation_to_the_Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Appointment and confirmation to the Supreme Court of the United States">vacancy on the nation’s highest court</a> is filled. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bostonherald.com/news/columnists/kimberly_atkins/2016/03/atkins_split_court_gives_unions_a_win" rel="nofollow">(<i>Boston Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>The U.S. <a href="/wiki/National_Labor_Relations_Board" title="National Labor Relations Board">National Labor Relations Board</a> files an official complaint against a <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a> warehouse after finding evidence it violated workers' rights to organize. The allegations of wrongdoing submitted by a worker group against California Cartage Company, LLC, which serves <a href="/wiki/Amazon.com" title="Amazon.com">Amazon.com, Inc.</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lowe%27s" title="Lowe's">Lowe's Companies. Inc.</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Balance" title="New Balance">New Balance</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Sears_Holdings" title="Sears Holdings">Sears Holdings Corp.</a>, will be heard by an NLRB <a href="/wiki/Administrative_law_judge" title="Administrative law judge">administrative law judge</a> in June 2016. None of the retailers were named in the NLRB complaint. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-labor-warehouse-idUSKCN0WW01G" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>

<dt>Health and medicine</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Terminix" title="Terminix">Terminix</a>, in the <a href="/wiki/District_Court_of_the_Virgin_Islands" title="District Court of the Virgin Islands">U.S. District Court</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Thomas,_Virgin_Islands" title="St. Thomas, Virgin Islands">St. Thomas, Virgin Islands</a>, admits it "knowingly" applied <a href="/wiki/Fumigation" title="Fumigation">fumigants</a> including <a href="/wiki/Bromomethane" title="Bromomethane">methyl bromide</a>, which the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Environmental_Protection_Agency" title="United States Environmental Protection Agency">EPA</a> banned for residential use in 1984, at a resort in <a href="/wiki/Saint_John,_U.S._Virgin_Islands" title="Saint John, U.S. Virgin Islands">St. John</a> that seriously sickened a family of four, and agrees to pay $10 million in fines and restitution. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/news/us-news/terminix-pay-10-million-using-banned-pesticide-sickened-family-n547566" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/news/us-news/family-four-sickened-u-s-virgin-islands-resort-after-fumigation-n336401" rel="nofollow">(NBC News²)</a></li>
<li>New research, published in <i><a href="/wiki/Circulation_(journal)" title="Circulation (journal)">Circulation: Cardiovascular Quality and Outcomes</a></i>, finds women who have <a href="/wiki/Endometriosis" title="Endometriosis">endometriosis</a>, the abnormal growth of uterine tissue outside the <a href="/wiki/Uterus" title="Uterus">uterus</a>, may face a 60 percent higher risk of developing <a href="/wiki/Cardiovascular_disease" title="Cardiovascular disease">heart disease</a> than women without the disorder. The potential risk was especially high for women 40 or younger. At least 10 percent of women of reproductive age suffer from endometriosis (endo) says Dr. Stacey Missmer of <a href="/wiki/Brigham_and_Women%27s_Hospital" title="Brigham and Women's Hospital">Brigham and Women's Hospital</a>, who co-authored the study. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Health_News/2016/03/29/Endometriosis-linked-to-heart-disease-in-study/4411459284938/?spt=rln&amp;or=4" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/health/womens-health/endometriosis-increases-risk-heart-disease-young-women-n547381" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
</ul>

Burwell">Zubik v. Burwell</a></i>
<ul>
<li>In a move designed to head off a 4-4 decision, the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">U.S. Supreme Court</a> directs lawyers for the Obama administration, and for the religious groups who challenge it, to submit written briefs on a possible remedy to the case: whether coverage could be provided through the group's insurance companies without any actual notice to the government. A 4-4 decision would not set a national precedent, and would let stand the preceding decision in each case. In these <a href="/wiki/Zubik_v._Burwell#Supreme_Court_review" title="Zubik v. Burwell">seven cases</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_States_courts_of_appeals" title="United States courts of appeals">appeals court</a> in six upheld the government mandate. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/news/us-news/supreme-court-raises-new-obamacare-questions-n547421" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>

<li>A legal request has been filed to impeach <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazilian</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_Brazil" title="President of Brazil">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff" title="Dilma Rousseff">Dilma Rousseff</a> for obstructing justice and fiscal accounting tricks, the second impeachment request against her. In response to the request, <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Tourism_(Brazil)" title="Ministry of Tourism (Brazil)">Minister of Tourism</a> <a href="/wiki/Henrique_Eduardo_Alves" title="Henrique Eduardo Alves">Henrique Eduardo Alves</a> turned in a resignation letter while the <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Democratic_Movement_Party" title="Brazilian Democratic Movement Party">Brazilian Democratic Movement Party</a> is expected to hold a party vote on whether or not to leave Rousseff's coalition government. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2016/03/brazil-rousseff-faces-impeachment-coalition-collapse-160329044900462.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Al Jazeera</i>)</a></li>
<li>The Brazilian Democratic Movement Party, the country's largest party, decides unanimously to leave President Rousseff's governing coalition. While Rousseff will remain in office, it's likely she could be impeached in a matter of months, which would make <a href="/wiki/Vice_President_of_Brazil" title="Vice President of Brazil">Vice President</a> <a href="/wiki/Michel_Temer" title="Michel Temer">Michel Temer</a> president. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-brazil-politics-idUSKCN0WU1AC" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>

</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Federal_Communications_Commission" title="Federal Communications Commission">U.S. Federal Communications Commissioner</a> <a href="/wiki/Michael_O%27Rielly" title="Michael O'Rielly">Michael O'Rielly</a> says, during a speech at the <a href="/wiki/American_Action_Network" title="American Action Network">American Action Forum</a>, that <a href="/wiki/Netflix" title="Netflix">Netflix</a>'s admission last week that it has been intentionally slowing its video streaming transmission on some wireless mobile carriers for five years "deeply disturbing" which might warrant an investigation by the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Trade_Commission" title="Federal Trade Commission">Federal Trade Commission</a> and/or <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">Congress</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Business_News/2016/03/29/FCC-commissioner-Netflix-capping-mobile-streaming-video-data-deeply-disturbing/9201459287264/?spt=hs&amp;or=bn" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
