<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> March 30, 2016<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2016-03-30</span>)</span> (Wednesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_30&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_30&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2016_March_30&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Libyan_Civil_War_(2014%E2%80%93present)" title="Libyan Civil War (2014–present)">Libyan Civil War (2014–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>Blasts and gunfire are reported in <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-libya-security-idUSKCN0WW01A" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Naxalite%E2%80%93Maoist_insurgency" title="Naxalite–Maoist insurgency">Naxalite–Maoist insurgency</a>
<ul>
<li>At least seven <a href="/wiki/Central_Reserve_Police_Force" title="Central Reserve Police Force">Central Reserve Police Force</a> (CRPF) personnel are killed in an <a href="/wiki/Improvised_explosive_device" title="Improvised explosive device">IED</a> attack on their vehicle in the <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> state of <a href="/wiki/Chhattisgarh" title="Chhattisgarh">Chhattisgarh</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Dantewada_district" title="Dantewada district">Dantewada district</a>. <a href="/wiki/Naxalite" title="Naxalite">Naxalite</a> insurgents are suspected to have been behind the attack. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ibtimes.co.in/7-crpf-jawans-killed-suspected-maoist-attack-672725" rel="nofollow">(<i>International Business Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economy</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwanese</a> electronics company <a href="/wiki/Foxconn" title="Foxconn">Foxconn</a> agrees to buy 60% of the <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japanese</a> <a href="/wiki/Sharp_Corporation" title="Sharp Corporation">Sharp Corporation</a> for 389 billion yen ($3.5 billion). <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-30/foxconn-group-says-taking-control-of-sharp-in-reduced-buyout" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a> and neighbouring countries suffer from the worst <a href="/wiki/Drought" title="Drought">drought</a> in decades as an <a href="/wiki/El_Ni%C3%B1o" title="El Niño">El Niño</a>-induced water shortage reduces reservoirs to critical levels. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2016/03/thailand-hit-worst-drought-decades-160330102123735.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Al Jazeera</i>)</a></li>
<li>At least nine people are injured in severe storms that spawned multiple <a href="/wiki/Tornado" title="Tornado">tornado</a> touchdowns in northeastern <a href="/wiki/Oklahoma" title="Oklahoma">Oklahoma</a> and sections of the <a href="/wiki/Southwestern_United_States" title="Southwestern United States">Southwestern United States</a>. One patient is in critical condition; the others suffered serious injuries, according to the <a href="/wiki/Emergency_Medical_Services_Authority" title="Emergency Medical Services Authority">Emergency Medical Services Authority</a>. Parts of <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>, <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">Louisiana</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Arkansas" title="Arkansas">Arkansas</a> are also impacted. A flash flood watch has been issued through Thursday evening. Two (2) to 4 inches of rain is expected, with perhaps 6 inches in some locations. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/b78151f352eb4965bda2402dc1bc6b85" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Health and medicine</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A new study by researchers at <a href="/wiki/McGill_University" title="McGill University">McGill University</a> and the <a href="/wiki/University_of_California,_Los_Angeles" title="University of California, Los Angeles">University of California, Los Angeles</a>, finds that each additional month a woman has paid <a href="/wiki/Parental_leave" title="Parental leave">maternity leave</a> is associated with decreased <a href="/wiki/Infant_mortality" title="Infant mortality">infant mortality</a> by more than 10 percent. Researchers noted that paid maternity leave reduces stress because of the guarantee of income and job security, increases the chances for breastfeeding and other infant care, and allows a mother to seek more medical attention for herself. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Health_News/2016/03/30/Study-Longer-maternity-leave-linked-to-better-infant-health/4971459363627/?spt=hs&amp;or=hn" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://journals.plos.org/plosmedicine/article?id=10.1371/journal.pmed.1001985" rel="nofollow">(PLOS Medicine)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Food_and_Drug_Administration" title="Food and Drug Administration">United States Food and Drug Administration</a> announces it has relaxed its official requirements regarding the use of the abortion drug <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mifeprex" title="Mifeprex">Mifeprex</a> (RU-486). The current guidelines were based on 1990s medical evidence. Changes include reducing the number of physician visits required by abortion-seeking women, reducing drug dosage, and allowing women to take the drug for three weeks longer -- now a total of 70 days. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/US/2016/03/30/FDA-revises-instructions-for-use-of-abortion-drug-Mifeprex-womens-health-advocates-hail-victory/4721459361592/?spt=hts&amp;or=2" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Air_pollution_in_Mexico_City" title="Air pollution in Mexico City">Air pollution in Mexico City</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mexico_City" title="Mexico City">Mexico City</a>, facing the capital's worst air-quality crisis in over a decade, issues a temporary order that all cars remain idle one day a week. Today, authorities report a pollution index of 108 (bad) after low readings during <a href="/wiki/Holy_Week" title="Holy Week">Holy Week</a>. Vehicles will also be forced from the roads one Saturday a month. The measure will begin next Tuesday, April 5, and run until Thursday, June 30, 2016. Starting July 1, improved technology will be in place at <a href="/wiki/Emission_standard" title="Emission standard">smog-check centers</a> where all vehicles must be tested every six months. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2016/03/30/mexico-city-temporarily-restricts-all-cars-after-smog-alert.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The Wallenberg family files an application to formally declare <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Swedish</a> diplomat <a href="/wiki/Raoul_Wallenberg" title="Raoul Wallenberg">Raoul Wallenberg</a> (born in 1912) to be dead. Wallenberg saved the lives of thousands of Jews in <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a> only to disappear at the hands of the <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet</a> forces. <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesofisrael.com/raoul-wallenberg-to-be-officially-declared-dead-by-sweden/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of Israel</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia%E2%80%93Ukraine_relations" title="Russia–Ukraine relations">Russia–Ukraine relations</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Verkhovna_Rada" title="Verkhovna Rada">Ukrainian parliament</a> votes to ban all <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> films released after January 1, 2014, saying the move is aimed at improving “national security"; more than 430 Russian films and TV series fall under the new measures. Last month, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/State_Committee_in_Television_and_Radio-broadcasting_(Ukraine)" title="State Committee in Television and Radio-broadcasting (Ukraine)">State Committee in Television and Radio-broadcasting</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a> removed 15 Russian TV channels from being broadcast in Ukraine. <a class="external text" href="https://www.rt.com/news/337728-ukraine-bans-russian-movies/" rel="nofollow">(RT)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">U.K. Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a>, at the upcoming <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_Security_Summit" title="Nuclear Security Summit">Nuclear Security Summit</a> in <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a>, will announce a three-way deal with the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> and <a href="/wiki/European_Atomic_Energy_Community" title="European Atomic Energy Community">Euratom</a>, the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> nuclear agency, to turn <a href="/wiki/Radioactive_waste" title="Radioactive waste">nuclear waste</a> into <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_medicine" title="Nuclear medicine">medical isotopes</a> to help fight <a href="/wiki/Cancer" title="Cancer">cancer</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-30/cameron-to-announce-moves-to-boost-nuclear-industry-security" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh" title="Bangladesh">Bangladesh</a> Court issues an arrest warrant, the second one so far, for former <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Bangladesh" title="Prime Minister of Bangladesh">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Khaleda_Zia" title="Khaleda Zia">Khaleda Zia</a> and 27 opposition <a href="/wiki/Bangladesh_Nationalist_Party" title="Bangladesh Nationalist Party">Bangladesh Nationalist Party</a> members over political violence, mostly petrol-bomb attacks, that occurred during anti-government protests last year that killed at least 120 people. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2016/03/bangladesh-arrest-warrant-issued-pm-160330125529350.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Al Jazeera</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/EgyptAir_Flight_181" title="EgyptAir Flight 181">EgyptAir Flight 181</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Larnaca" title="Larnaca">Larnaca</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cyprus" title="Cyprus">Cyprus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Judiciary_of_Cyprus" title="Judiciary of Cyprus">court</a> orders that 59-year-old Seif Eddin Mustafa, who was arrested by <a href="/wiki/Cyprus_Police" title="Cyprus Police">Cypriot police</a> yesterday, remain in local police custody for eight days to assist Cyprus's own investigation. Mustafa faces charges of hijacking, illegal possession of explosives, kidnapping, and threats to commit violence. It's unclear if Mustafa had any explosives; the bomb belt he wore was fake, and officials are waiting for testing results on unidentified liquids found among his possessions. <a class="external text" href="http://www.kelownadailycourier.ca/news/world_news/article_12660d73-51c7-5805-b5c4-8dec3074a343.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The Daily Courier</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a> General Prosecutor Nabil Sadek formally requests Mustafa's <a href="/wiki/Extradition" title="Extradition">extradition</a> from Cyprus. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-egypt-airplane-hijacking-extradition-idUSKCN0WW1GC" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2016" title="United States presidential election, 2016">United States presidential election, 2016</a>:
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/National_Border_Patrol_Council" title="National Border Patrol Council">National Border Patrol Council</a> (NBPC), which organizes some 16,500 border patrol agents, endorses <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> for President of the United States, NBPC's first-ever endorsement in a presidential election. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2016/03/30/politics/border-patrol-union-endorses-donald-trump/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Myanmar_general_election,_2015" title="Myanmar general election, 2015">Myanmar general election, 2015</a>
<ul>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Myanmar" title="Myanmar">Myanmar's</a> capital <a href="/wiki/Naypyidaw" title="Naypyidaw">Naypyidaw</a>, <a href="/wiki/Htin_Kyaw" title="Htin Kyaw">Htin Kyaw</a> is sworn in by House Speaker <a href="/wiki/Mahn_Win_Khaing_Than" title="Mahn Win Khaing Than">Mahn Win Khaing Than</a> as the first civilian president in 54 years. Htin Kyaw, a close aide to <a href="/wiki/Aung_San_Suu_Kyi" title="Aung San Suu Kyi">Aung San Suu Kyi</a>, takes power from former general <a href="/wiki/Thein_Sein" title="Thein Sein">Thein Sein</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/wires/afp/article-3515031/Suu-Kyi-aide-sworn-Myanmar-president-historic-power-shift.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Mail</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The government of <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> warns that it will push to clear the <a href="/wiki/Islamism" title="Islamism">Islamist</a> protests occurring in <a href="/wiki/Islamabad" title="Islamabad">Islamabad</a>. Protests have broken out in the capital and other cities ever since <a href="/wiki/Mumtaz_Qadri" title="Mumtaz Qadri">Mumtaz Qadri</a> was executed last February for his role in killing <a href="/wiki/Punjab,_Pakistan" title="Punjab, Pakistan">Punjab</a> governor <a href="/wiki/Salmaan_Taseer" title="Salmaan Taseer">Salmaan Taseer</a> in 2011 because he opposed Pakistan's blasphemy laws. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/pakistan-warns-will-clear-islamic-protesters-islamabad-/27643397.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Libyan_Civil_War_(2014%E2%80%93present)" title="Libyan Civil War (2014–present)">Libyan Civil War (2014–present)</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>-backed <a href="/wiki/Presidential_Council_(Libya)" title="Presidential Council (Libya)">Libyan Presidential Council</a> arrives in <a href="/wiki/Tripoli" title="Tripoli">Tripoli</a> despite warnings by hardliners opposed to any unity government that they will attempt to keep them out of the city. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2016/mar/30/libyan-presidential-council-unity-government-fayez-sarraj-tripoli" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The opposition controlled <a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_(Venezuela)" title="National Assembly (Venezuela)">National Assembly</a> of <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a> passes an amnesty bill that could potentially free over 70 opposition leaders and activists jailed during <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9316_Venezuelan_protests" title="2014–16 Venezuelan protests">protests</a> last year, including prominent leader <a href="/wiki/Leopoldo_L%C3%B3pez" title="Leopoldo López">Leopoldo López</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.com/news/world-latin-america-35924647" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_Venezuela" title="President of Venezuela">Venezuelan President</a> <a href="/wiki/Nicol%C3%A1s_Maduro" title="Nicolás Maduro">Nicolás Maduro</a> vows to <a href="/wiki/Veto" title="Veto">veto</a> this amnesty bill. The opposition can override the veto since it holds a <a href="/wiki/Supermajority" title="Supermajority">supermajority</a> in the <a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_(Venezuela)" title="National Assembly (Venezuela)">National Assembly</a>. Maduro can also send the bill to the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Tribunal_of_Justice_(Venezuela)" title="Supreme Tribunal of Justice (Venezuela)">Supreme Tribunal</a> to determine its constitutionality. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2016/03/30/Venezuelas-Maduro-vows-to-veto-amnesty-bill-passed-by-National-Assembly/2471459353316/?spt=hts&amp;or=5" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
<li>The opposition plans to generate a <a href="/wiki/Recall_election" title="Recall election">recall referendum</a> that would ask voters if President Maduro should be removed from office. The <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_Venezuela" title="Constitution of Venezuela">Constitution</a> states a recall referendum can be held once the president has served half of his six-year term (Maduro became President on April 19, 2013) and at least 20 percent of registered voters sign the petition. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2016/03/29/Venezuelan-opposition-preparing-referendum-to-oust-Maduro/7201459269012/?st" rel="nofollow">(UPI²)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sports</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Two <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russian_people" title="Russian people">Russian</a> cyclists, former world champion <a href="/wiki/Anastasia_Chulkova" title="Anastasia Chulkova">Anastasia Chulkova</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pavel_Yakushevskiy" title="Pavel Yakushevskiy">Pavel Yakushevskiy</a>, test positive for <a href="/wiki/Meldonium" title="Meldonium">meldonium</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/8f7ca5f04a454bfda94997714769f13c/russia-says-2-cyclists-have-tested-positive-meldoniun" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
<li>Three-time <a href="/wiki/Kentucky_Derby" title="Kentucky Derby">Kentucky Derby</a> winning jockey <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Borel" title="Calvin Borel">Calvin Borel</a> announces his retirement. <a class="external text" href="http://www.courier-journal.com/story/sports/horses/triple/derby/2016/03/30/videos--jockey-calvin-borels-memorable-moments/82434194/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Louisville Courier-Journal</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<dl>
<dt>Armed conflicts and attacks</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="Israeli–Palestinian conflict (2015–present)">Israeli–Palestinian conflict (2015–present)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> security forces arrest 16 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_people" title="Palestinian people">Palestinian</a> suspects on the <a href="/wiki/West_Bank" title="West Bank">West Bank</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.jpost.com/Breaking-News/Security-forces-arrest-16-Palestinian-suspects-in-West-Bank-sweeps-449826?utm_source=dlvr.it&amp;utm_medium=twitter" rel="nofollow">(<i>Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_Somalia_(2009%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Somalia (2009–present)">War in Somalia</a>
<ul>
<li>A suicide bomber in <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia’s</a> <a href="/wiki/Puntland" title="Puntland">Puntland region</a> detonates while hugging Saeed Ali, the treasurer of <a href="/wiki/Galkayo" title="Galkayo">Galkayo</a>, killing him and several police officers guarding him. Islamic militant group <a href="/wiki/Al-Shabaab_(militant_group)" title="Al-Shabaab (militant group)">Al-Shabaab</a> claims responsibility. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ibtimes.com/terrorism-somalia-al-shabab-suicide-bomber-hugs-puntland-official-detonating-2346055" rel="nofollow">(<i>International Business Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://af.reuters.com/article/topNews/idAFKCN0WX0V3" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/PKK_rebellion_(2015%E2%80%93present)" title="PKK rebellion (2015–present)">PKK rebellion</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turkey%E2%80%93ISIL_conflict" title="Turkey–ISIL conflict">Turkey–ISIL conflict</a>
<ul>
<li>A car bomb, targeting an armored vehicle transporting police personnel, explodes close to a bus terminal in the Bağlar district of <a href="/wiki/Diyarbak%C4%B1r" title="Diyarbakır">Diyarbakır</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>, killing at least seven <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/General_Directorate_of_Security" title="General Directorate of Security">police officers</a> and wounding 27 more people, including 13 officers, according to a joint statement by Turkish officials and the police. The attack comes one day before <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Turkey" title="Prime Minister of Turkey">Turkish Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Ahmet_Davuto%C4%9Flu" title="Ahmet Davutoğlu">Ahmet Davutoğlu's</a> scheduled visit to the city. There has been no claim of responsibility. <a href="/wiki/CNN" title="CNN">CNN</a> points out both <a href="/wiki/Kurdistan_Workers%27_Party" title="Kurdistan Workers' Party">Kurdish rebels</a> and <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a> militants have claimed similar recent incidents. <a class="external text" href="http://www.aljazeera.com/news/2016/03/loud-explosion-rocks-turkey-diyarbakir-160331142831391.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Al Jazeera</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/31/europe/turkey-violence/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/e0fcaea56a3843b3ae9708d7c9083052" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.arabnews.com/news/903911" rel="nofollow">(<i>Arab News</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Observatory_for_Human_Rights" title="Syrian Observatory for Human Rights">Syrian Observatory for Human Rights</a> reports a drone attack, “most likely operated by the US-led coalition,” kills Abu al-Hija, a high-ranking <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisian</a> <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a> commander, near the Islamic State's de facto <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syrian</a> capital <a href="/wiki/Al-Raqqah" title="Al-Raqqah">Raqqa</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://english.alarabiya.net/en/News/middle-east/2016/03/31/ISIS-commander-killed-in-strike-near-Syria-s-Raqqa.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Arabiya)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Business and economics</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Federal_Trade_Commission" title="Federal Trade Commission">U.S. Federal Trade Commission</a> files an <a href="/wiki/Competition_law" title="Competition law">anti-trust suit</a> against <a href="/wiki/Endo_International_plc" title="Endo International plc">Endo Pharmaceuticals, Inc.,</a> and several other drug companies for using <a href="/wiki/Reverse_payment_patent_settlement" title="Reverse payment patent settlement">pay-for-delay settlements</a> to block consumers’ access to lower-cost <a href="/wiki/Generic_drug" title="Generic drug">generic</a> versions of <a href="/wiki/Analgesic" title="Analgesic">pain medications</a>, <a href="/wiki/Oxymorphone" title="Oxymorphone">Opana ER</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lidocaine" title="Lidocaine">Lidoderm</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.streetinsider.com/Corporate+News/FTC+Suit+Alleges+Endo+%28ENDP%29+Entered+into+Pay-for-Delay+Patent+Settlements+with+Impax+%28IPXL%29+and+Watson+to+Delay+Generic+Versions+of+Branded+Drugs+Opana+ER+and+Lidoderm/11462674.html" rel="nofollow">(StreetInsider.com)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Consortium" title="Consortium">consortium</a> led by <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China's</a> <a href="/wiki/Anbang_Insurance_Group" title="Anbang Insurance Group">Anbang Insurance Group</a> announces it will walk away from its $14 billion takeover bid for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Starwood_Hotels_and_Resorts_Worldwide" title="Starwood Hotels and Resorts Worldwide">Starwood Hotels</a>. This restores <a href="/wiki/Marriott_International" title="Marriott International">Marriott International</a> as the highest bidder ($13.6 billion). <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnbc.com/2016/03/31/anbang-walking-away-from-starwood-deal-dj-citing-sources.html" rel="nofollow">(CNBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2016-03-31/anbang-said-to-withdraw-14-billion-bid-for-starwood-hotels" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Disasters and accidents</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2016_Kolkata_overpass_collapse" title="2016 Kolkata overpass collapse">2016 Kolkata overpass collapse</a>
<ul>
<li>At least 21 people are killed, 70 injured and up to 150 people are feared trapped after a half-built <a href="/wiki/Overpass" title="Overpass">overpass</a> collapses in the <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Kolkata" title="Kolkata">Kolkata</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://indianexpress.com/article/india/india-news-india/kolkata-under-construction-bridge-collapses-several-feared-dead-latest-updates/" rel="nofollow">(<i>Indian Express</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/kolkata-overpass-collapse-kills-least-14-scores-feared-trapped-n548361" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>International relations</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2016_Nuclear_Security_Summit" title="2016 Nuclear Security Summit">2016 Nuclear Security Summit</a>
<ul>
<li>More than 50 heads of state as well as representatives from international organizations attend the annual <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_Security_Summit" title="Nuclear Security Summit">Nuclear Security Summit</a> in <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">Washington, D.C.</a>, with the notable exception of <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>, which declined to attend. The main agenda of the two-day gathering is the discussion of <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> and the threat it poses with its <a href="/wiki/North_Korea_and_weapons_of_mass_destruction" title="North Korea and weapons of mass destruction">nuclear weapons</a> and the possibility of <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIS</a> extremists getting a nuclear weapon. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rferl.org/content/nuclear-summit-washington-islamic-state-north-korea/27645847.html" rel="nofollow">(Radio Free Europe/Radio Liberty)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Law and crime</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Yugoslav_Wars" title="Yugoslav Wars">Yugoslav Wars</a>
<ul>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/Deputy_Prime_Minister_of_Serbia" title="Deputy Prime Minister of Serbia">Deputy Prime Minister of Serbia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Serbian_nationalism" title="Serbian nationalism">nationalist</a> politician, <a href="/wiki/Vojislav_%C5%A0e%C5%A1elj" title="Vojislav Šešelj">Vojislav Šešelj</a>, is acquitted of all nine charges of committing atrocities in <a href="/wiki/Bosnia_and_Herzegovina" title="Bosnia and Herzegovina">Bosnia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Croatia" title="Croatia">Croatia</a> during the early 1990s by the <a href="/wiki/International_Criminal_Tribunal_for_the_former_Yugoslavia" title="International Criminal Tribunal for the former Yugoslavia">International Criminal Tribunal for the former Yugoslavia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/law/2016/mar/31/serb-nationalist-vojislav-seselj-acquitted-war-crimes-crimes-against-humanity-icty-the-hague" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> official announces that <a href="/wiki/The_Pentagon" title="The Pentagon">The Pentagon</a> plans to transfer about a dozen inmates from the <a href="/wiki/Guantanamo_Bay_detention_camp" title="Guantanamo Bay detention camp">Guantanamo Bay detention camp</a> to at least two countries that have agreed to take them, in the latest move in <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama’s</a> final push to close the facility. The official declined to name the countries ready to take them in. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2016/mar/31/guantanamo-prisoner-transfer-cuba-pentagon-obama-close-gitmo" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Malaysia_Airlines_Flight_370" title="Malaysia Airlines Flight 370">Malaysia Airlines Flight 370</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysian</a> court dismisses <a href="/wiki/Malaysia_Airlines" title="Malaysia Airlines">Malaysia Airlines's</a> bid to throw out a lawsuit filed by relatives of three people who went missing on Flight 370. The company argued that the disappearance of MH370 on March 8, 2014, occurred before the company came into existence as Malaysia Airlines Berhad (MAB) on September 1, 2015, and therefore has no liability to relatives. The court ruled MAB's liability would be determined in a trial. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2016/03/31/MH370-Malaysian-court-refuses-to-throw-out-lawsuit-against-airline/5791459423249/?spt=hts&amp;or=4" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.themalaymailonline.com/malaysia/article/court-dismisses-malaysia-airlines-bid-to-strike-out-mh370-suit" rel="nofollow">(<i>Malay Mail</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A 37-year-old <a href="/wiki/Virginia_State_Police" title="Virginia State Police">Virginia State Police trooper</a> taking part in a police training mission is killed by a gunman inside the <a href="/wiki/Greyhound_Lines" title="Greyhound Lines">Greyhound</a> <a href="/wiki/Bus_station" title="Bus station">bus station</a> in <a href="/wiki/Richmond,_Virginia" title="Richmond, Virginia">Richmond, Virginia</a>. Two officers standing nearby return fire and fatally strike the suspect. Two civilian women are injured. <a class="external text" href="http://wtvr.com/2016/03/31/active-shooter-reported-at-richmond-greyhound-bus-station/" rel="nofollow">(WTVR)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nbcnews.com/news/us-news/trooper-severely-injured-gunman-dead-shooting-greyhound-station-richmond-virginia-n548686" rel="nofollow">(NBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Politics and elections</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a> elects <a href="/wiki/Nguy%E1%BB%85n_Th%E1%BB%8B_Kim_Ng%C3%A2n" title="Nguyễn Thị Kim Ngân">Nguyễn Thị Kim Ngân</a> chairwoman of the <a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_(Vietnam)" title="National Assembly (Vietnam)">National Assembly</a>. Ngân, who won 95.5 percent of the votes, is the first woman to lead Vietnam's legislature. In January, she was re-elected to the powerful <a href="/wiki/Politburo_of_the_Communist_Party_of_Vietnam" title="Politburo of the Communist Party of Vietnam">Politburo</a> at the <a href="/wiki/National_Congress_of_the_Communist_Party_of_Vietnam" title="National Congress of the Communist Party of Vietnam">Communist Party Congress</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://bigstory.ap.org/article/b67c25180ae04c37a56853f9e8328895/vietnam-elects-first-chairwoman-parliament" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Constitutional_Court_of_South_Africa" title="Constitutional Court of South Africa">Constitutional Court of South Africa</a> delivered a unanimous judgement that President <a href="/wiki/Jacob_Zuma" title="Jacob Zuma">Jacob Zuma</a> and the <a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_of_South_Africa" title="National Assembly of South Africa">National Assembly</a> failed to uphold the country's constitution by ignoring the findings of the <a href="/wiki/Public_Protector" title="Public Protector">Public Protector</a> regarding public expenditure on Zuma's private homestead. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dailymaverick.co.za/article/2016-03-31-nkandla-concourt-ruling-president-zuma-and-national-assembly-in-breach-of-constitution/#.Vvz5raT5jIW" rel="nofollow">(<i>Daily Maverick</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2016" title="United States presidential election, 2016">United States presidential election, 2016</a>, <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_presidential_candidates,_2016" title="Republican Party presidential candidates, 2016">Republican Party presidential candidates, 2016</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Pennsylvania" title="Supreme Court of Pennsylvania">Pennsylvania's Supreme Court</a> upholds the previous court ruling that dismissed the case against <a href="/wiki/Ted_Cruz" title="Ted Cruz">Ted Cruz</a> which challenged his <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States#eligibility" title="President of the United States">eligibility</a> to appear on the state's GOP primary ballot, and serve as president. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/Politics/wireStory/cruz-wins-citizenship-case-pennsylvania-supreme-court-38059265" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Japan" title="Prime Minister of Japan">Japan's Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Shinz%C5%8D_Abe" title="Shinzō Abe">Shinzō Abe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Foreign_Affairs_(Japan)" title="Minister for Foreign Affairs (Japan)">Foreign Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Fumio_Kishida" title="Fumio Kishida">Fumio Kishida</a> forcibly reject, as has the <a href="/wiki/Executive_Office_of_the_President" title="Executive Office of the President">White House</a>, candidate <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump's</a> suggestion that the U.S. military be withdrawn from Japan and South Korea with nuclear weapons replacing them. A small minority in South Korea, such as the think tank <a href="/wiki/Sejong_Institute" title="Sejong Institute">Sejong Institute</a>, agree with Trump on this issue, but this is not mainstream policy. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/31/politics/trump-view-from-south-korea-japan/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.vox.com/2016/3/31/11339040/trump-nukes-japan-south-korea" rel="nofollow">(Vox Media)</a>
<ul>
<li>Another Trump statement, "<a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> is a money machine but they pay us peanuts," is greeted with "howls of inaccuracy" from the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_(South_Korea)" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs (South Korea)">South Korean Foreign Ministry</a> and the White House. <a href="/wiki/United_States_Ambassador_to_South_Korea" title="United States Ambassador to South Korea">U.S. Ambassador to South Korea</a> <a href="/wiki/Mark_Lippert" title="Mark Lippert">Mark Lippert</a> says "Seoul pays for 55% of all non-personnel costs." <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2016/03/31/politics/trump-view-from-south-korea-japan/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_(Venezuela)" title="National Assembly (Venezuela)">Venezuela's National Assembly</a>, responding to last month's <a href="/wiki/Central_Bank_of_Venezuela" title="Central Bank of Venezuela">Central Bank of Venezuela</a> report that the country experienced a 180.9 percent <a href="/wiki/Inflation" title="Inflation">inflation</a> increase in 2015, passes legislation, <i>The Law of Bonds for Food and Medicine for Retirees and Pensioners</i>, that could make it easier for pensioners and retirees to pay for food and medicine. The approved bill has been forwarded for <a href="/wiki/President_of_Venezuela" title="President of Venezuela">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Nicol%C3%A1s_Maduro" title="Nicolás Maduro">Nicolás Maduro's</a> signature. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/World-News/2016/03/31/Venezuelan-retirees-could-see-grocery-bill-help-in-wake-of-180-inflation/5651459438964/?spt=hs&amp;or=tn_int" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Italian_Minister_of_Economic_Development" title="Italian Minister of Economic Development">Minister of Economic Development</a>, <a href="/wiki/Federica_Guidi" title="Federica Guidi">Federica Guidi</a>, resigns amid allegations that she passed along confidential information to her boyfriend that helped his business interests. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/world/2016/03/31/italy-economic-minister-resigns-amid-oil-probe.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_protests_in_Brazil" title="2015–16 protests in Brazil">Brazil protests</a>
<ul>
<li>Brazil's <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Federal_Court" title="Supreme Federal Court">Supreme Court</a> voted 8-2 to take over the corruption investigation of former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Brazil" title="President of Brazil">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Luiz_In%C3%A1cio_Lula_da_Silva" title="Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva">Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva</a>. Silva alleges <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A9rgio_Moro" title="Sérgio Moro">Judge Sérgio Moro</a> unfairly targets him. The court also overruled Moro's decision to release the recording of Silva's call with <a href="/wiki/President_of_Brazil" title="President of Brazil">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Dilma_Rousseff" title="Dilma Rousseff">Dilma Rousseff</a>, since it is the only court that can authorize a wiretap on presidential conversations. The full court is still to rule on the injunction that prevents Silva from taking office as the <a href="/wiki/Chief_of_Staff_of_Brazil" title="Chief of Staff of Brazil">President's Chief of Staff</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/brazils-sports-minister-resigns-presidents-office-38055272" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC news)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-brazil-politics-lula-idUSKCN0WX2L5" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Today, thousands of demonstrators gathered in more than 20 states in support of Silva and Rousseff. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/us-brazil-politics-protests-idUSKCN0WX2RI?mod=related&amp;channelName=worldNews" rel="nofollow">(Reuters²)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/brazils-sports-minister-resigns-presidents-office-38055272" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC news)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Sports_(Brazil)" title="Ministry of Sports (Brazil)">Brazil sports minister</a> George Hilton resigns and will be replaced on an interim basis by Ricardo Leyser, a senior official in the ministry. Leyser, 45, has worked in the sports ministry since 2003, and has been heavily involved with the <a href="/wiki/2016_Summer_Olympics" title="2016 Summer Olympics">Olympic Games</a>, which will be held in <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Rio de Janeiro">Rio de Janeiro</a>, August 5-21, 2016. <a class="external text" href="http://riotimesonline.com/brazil-news/rio-sports/brazils-sports-minister-resigns-months-before-the-olympics/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Rio Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.insidethegames.biz/articles/1035934/brazilian-sports-minister-officially-steps-down-and-is-replaced-by-leyser" rel="nofollow">(insidethegames)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Science and technology</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Astronomers' study reveals the surface of <a href="/wiki/Exoplanet" title="Exoplanet">exoplanet</a> <a href="/wiki/55_Cancri_e" title="55 Cancri e">55 Cancri e</a> has a 2500°C liquid face, constantly facing its star <a href="/wiki/55_Cancri" title="55 Cancri">55 Cancri</a>, while the other side is relatively colder and solid. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/2016-03-31/two-faced-alien-planet-55-cancri-e-has-solid-and-liquid-surfaces/7287638" rel="nofollow">(Discovery via ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Sport</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Five <a href="/wiki/United_States_women%27s_national_soccer_team" title="United States women's national soccer team">U.S. women’s national soccer team players</a> file federal <a href="/wiki/Gender_pay_gap" title="Gender pay gap">wage discrimination complaints</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Equal_Employment_Opportunity_Commission" title="Equal Employment Opportunity Commission">Equal Employment Opportunity Commission</a> against the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Soccer_Federation" title="United States Soccer Federation">U.S. Soccer Federation</a> (USSF). In the filing, the players cite 2015 USSF figures which show they were paid nearly four times less than men’s players despite generating nearly $20 million more revenue. A U.S. Soccer statement says, "... we are disappointed about this action." <a class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/news/early-lead/wp/2016/03/31/five-u-s-womens-soccer-players-file-wage-discrimination-complaint/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Washington Post</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://espn.go.com/espnw/sports/article/15102506/women-national-team-files-wage-discrimination-action-vs-us-soccer-federation" rel="nofollow">(ESPN)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
